# gr-qc [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Dark Energy Stars in Finch-Skea Spacetime with a Schwarzschild-(Anti)-de Sitter Exterior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30398)
*Muhamad Ashraf Azman*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 在爱因斯坦引力框架下，系统研究了宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）对 Finch-Skea 时空中暗能量星（dark energy star）结构、平衡及稳定性的影响。结果表明，正宇宙学常数导致更大但更不致密的构型，负宇宙学常数则带来更致密、引力效应更强的星体；能量条件始终满足，但过大的宇宙学常数会破坏流体静力学平衡并影响因果性与动态稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）如何影响暗能量星（dark energy star）在 Finch-Skea 时空中的结构参数与稳定性，以揭示宇宙学常数在致密星物理中的作用。

Method: 采用复杂度因子（complexity factor）形式化方法获取时间度规势（temporal metric potential），构建由普通物质与暗能量组成的静态各向异性（static and anisotropic）星体模型；通过适当的边界条件将内部解平滑匹配到外部 Schwarzschild-(anti-)de Sitter 时空。

Result: 正宇宙学常数产生更大、致密度更低的构型，负宇宙学常数则使星体更致密且引力效应更强；所有情形下能量条件（energy conditions）均满足，但足够大的宇宙学常数会偏离流体静力学平衡（hydrostatic equilibrium），并影响模型的因果性与动态稳定性。

Conclusion: 宇宙学常数在决定 Finch-Skea 时空中暗能量星的致密度、平衡及稳定性方面起关键作用。

Abstract: In this work, the effects of the cosmological constant on dark energy stars in Finch-Skea spacetime are systematically investigated within the framework of Einstein gravity. A static and anisotropic stellar configuration composed of ordinary matter and dark energy is constructed by employing the complexity factor formalism to obtain the temporal metric potential. The interior solution is smoothly matched to the exterior Schwarzschild-(anti-)de Sitter spacetime through appropriate boundary conditions. The influence of positive and negative cosmological constants on the structural and stability properties of the compact star candidate Vela X-1 is investigated in detail. The results show that positive values of the cosmological constant produce larger and less compact configurations, whereas negative values lead to denser and more compact stars with stronger gravitational effects. The energy conditions are satisfied throughout the stellar interior for all considered cases. However, sufficiently large values of the cosmological constant introduce deviations from hydrostatic equilibrium and affect the causal and dynamical stability behavior of the model. Overall, the results demonstrate that the cosmological constant plays an important role in determining the compactness, equilibrium and stability behavior of dark energy stars in Finch-Skea spacetime.

</details>


### [2] [Toward a Phenomenologically Acceptable Quantum Cyclic Universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30405)
*Sean M. Carroll,Nadiia Diachenko,Saakshi Dulani*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种精确周期性的量子宇宙学模型，通过有限维希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）中的幺正演化（unitary evolution）以及能量本征值（energy eigenvalues）的可公度性（commensurability），避免了玻尔兹曼大脑（Boltzmann Brain）问题。模型从最小热力学熵出发，产生一个显著的熵 excursion（可对应大爆炸），随后平衡态中的玻尔兹曼涨落极少，最终以大挤压（Big Crunch）结束并重启周期。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的周期性宇宙模型面临玻尔兹曼大脑问题——宇宙在大部分时间处于高熵平衡态，绝大多数观测者将是偏离平衡的最小涨落，即“玻尔兹曼大脑”，这在现象学上不可接受。本文旨在证明这种担忧并非必然成立。

Method: 论文假设宇宙由一个在有限维希尔伯特空间中发生幺正演化的量子态描述，并引入能量本征值之间的可公度条件，使演化从简单的回复性（recurrence）变为严格周期性（exactly periodic）。在此基础上，设定初始态处于最小热力学熵（minimum thermodynamic entropy），从而产生一个远大于常规表达式 $P(ΔS) \propto \exp(-ΔS)$ 所预期的显著熵 excursion。

Result: 当能量本征值可公度时，宇宙演化不再是简单的回复性，而是精确周期性。若初始态处于最小热力学熵，其演化过程中会出现一个显著突出的熵 excursion，其幅度远大于标准统计涨落公式的预期。该 excursion 可对应大爆炸，而后续平衡阶段中出现的玻尔兹曼涨落相对极少。

Conclusion: 该量子宇宙模型成功规避了玻尔兹曼大脑问题，并提供了一个周期性的宇宙学图景：从大爆炸开始，经历熵的 excursion，随后进入平衡态，最终以大挤压结束并重启循环。论文还对这种量子宇宙的时空解释进行了推测。

Abstract: We put forward a quantum model of cosmology that is exactly periodic but avoids the Boltzmann Brain problem. If the universe is described by a quantum state evolving unitarily in a finite-dimensional Hilbert space, its evolution will be recurrent: given enough time, the state will return arbitrarily close to its initial state. There is a worry that such a scenario cannot be phenomenologically acceptable, because the state will spend most of its time in a high-entropy equilibrium macrostate, with rare fluctuations downward in entropy, and the vast majority of observers will be minimal fluctuations away from equilibrium, or ``Boltzmann Brains." Here we show that this is not necessarily true. If the differences in energy eigenvalues are commensurable, the evolution is not simple recurrent, but exactly periodic. Moreover, if the state starts at minimum thermodynamic entropy, its evolution can feature a distinguished entropy excursion that is much more pronounced than one would expect from the conventional expression $P(ΔS) \propto \exp(-ΔS)$. This excursion could represent our Big Bang, with relatively few Boltzmann fluctuations occurring in the subsequent equilibrium phase before a Big Crunch occurs and the cycle begins again. We speculate on the spacetime interpretation of this kind of quantum universe.

</details>


### [3] [Black hole evolutions: Lessons from bifurcation theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30458)
*Ivan Booth,Graham Cox,Chiamaka Mary Okpala*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究外边缘陷俘面（MOTS）稳定性算子（stability operator）不可逆时演化行为的非唯一性，利用分支理论（bifurcation theory）对可能的非唯一演化进行分类，并通过解析与数值工具在多种时空（如Reissner-Nordström-de Sitter、Weyl-distorted Schwarzschild）中识别鞍结分支（saddle-node bifurcation）、叉形分支（pitchfork bifurcation）及跨临界分支（transcritical bifurcation）等例子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究表明，当MOTS的稳定性算子可逆时，其时间演化是唯一的。本文旨在探讨稳定性算子不可逆的情形，理解此时可能出现的非唯一演化及其分类。

Method: 将MOTS类比为动力系统的不动点（fixed points），将稳定性算子视为MOTS定义方程的线性化（linearization），从而引入分支理论进行分类；同时定义广义MOTS稳定性算子（generalized MOTS stability operator），并利用解析与数值工具在球对称与轴对称时空中识别各类分支。

Result: 发现MOTS对的产生/湮灭（pair creation/annihilation）对应鞍结分支，此外还存在叉形分支和跨临界分支等多种分支类型；在Reissner-Nordström-de Sitter时空（球对称）和Reissner-Nordström及Weyl-distorted Schwarzschild时空（轴对称）中均找到了相应实例。

Conclusion: 该分支理论框架具有高度普适性，可适用于任何包含MOTS（或其推广）的引力理论；此类结构的可能分支类型在任何这样的理论中都受到相同方式的约束。

Abstract: We explore the role of the stability operator in regulating the evolution of marginally outer trapped surfaces (MOTSs). In 2005, Andersson, Mars and Simon showed that if the stability operator is invertible, then the time evolution of a MOTS is unique. Here we focus on moments at which that stability operator is not invertible. Understanding MOTSs as analogous to fixed points, and the stability operator as a linearization of the system of the MOTS-defining equations, bifurcation theory can be used to classify possible non-unique evolutions. MOTS pair creation/annihilation is an example of a saddle-node bifurcation but other possibilities can occur, including pitchfork and transcritical bifurcations. Analytical and numerical tools are used to identify examples of the various bifurcations in a variety of spacetimes. To help analyze those results, we define a generalized MOTS stability operator and discuss the (partial) barrier properties of unstable MOTSs. Spherically symmetric examples are given in Reissner-Nordström-de Sitter spacetime and axisymmetric examples are studied in Reissner-Nordström and Weyl-distorted Schwarzschild. This application of bifurcation theory is very general and so applies to any theory of gravity containing MOTSs (or some generalization thereof). Possible bifurcations of those structures are constrained in any such theory in the same way.

</details>


### [4] [Quantification of the parameter estimation error from Rotating Core Collapse supernovae](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30665)
*Claudia Moreno,Javier M. Antelis,Michele Zanolin*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用解析模型对快速旋转核坍缩超新星（core collapse supernova）的引力波参数 $β$（转动动能与引力势能之比）进行估计，通过与数值模板库及O4噪声模拟的比较验证模型可靠性，平均拟合因子（fitting factor）达94%，并基于匹配滤波（Matched Filter）与Cramér-Rao下界（Cramér Rao Lower Bound）分析参数估计误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核坍缩超新星核心反弹阶段的引力波信号携带星体内部动力学信息，现有研究缺乏对关键参数 $β$ 进行高精度解析建模与误差定量评估的方法。

Method: 采用解析模型模拟快速旋转核坍缩超新星核心反弹阶段的引力波辐射，利用Abylkairovś引力波波形目录构建数值模板库（numerical template bank），并模拟O4噪声（以干涉仪功率谱密度表征）验证模型的可靠性。使用匹配滤波方法估计参数 $β$，并将估计误差与Cramér-Rao下界（Cramér Rao Lower Bound）进行比较。

Result: 在0.02 < $β$ < 0.14区间内，平均拟合因子（fitting factor）达94%，表明解析模型高精度复现核心反弹波形关键特征，最优信噪比（signal to noise ratio）仅降低6%。在5、10和50 kpc距离下考虑噪声与波形后，参数估计误差的渐近展开给出理论下界低于 $10^{-1}$，且随距离增大而减小。

Conclusion: 该解析模型可有效用于快速旋转核坍缩超新星 $β$ 参数估计，在0.02 < $β$ < 0.14范围内模型准确性高，误差下界的推导为未来引力波观测中的参数估计精度提供了理论参考。

Abstract: In this paper, we perform parameter estimation with an analytical model to simulate the gravitational wave emission during the core bounce phase of a rapidly rotating core collapse supernova progenitor. This approach enables us to estimate the parameter $β$, defined as the ratio of rotational kinetic energy to gravitational potential energy in core collapse supernovae. To verify the reliability of both the analytical model and the inferred value of $β$, we use a numerical template bank constructed from Abylkairovś gravitational waveform catalog and simulate O4 noise, characterized by the interferometers power spectral density.
  An average fitting factor of 94\% over the interval 0.02 $< β<$ 0.14 shows that our analytical model reproduces the key characteristics of the core-bounce waveform with high accuracy, leading to only a 6\% reduction in the optimal signal to noise ratio. This provides a quantitative measure of how well the analytical model performs. Subsequently, we analyze the error in estimating $β$ using a Matched Filter method and compare it to the corresponding Cramér Rao Lower Bound. The results obtained by considering noise and waveforms at distances of 5, 10, and 50 kpc enable an assessment of how accurately the selected statistical model fits the observed data. From the asymptotic expansion of the variance, we derive a theoretical lower bound for the error that falls below $10^{-1}$ when the parameter $β$ decreases with distance.

</details>


### [5] [Dirac-Field Black Hole Entropy in \(f(Q)\) Gravity from the RVB Residue Method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31012)
*Wen-Xiang Chen*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文结合基于留数的RVB方法与薄膜态计数方法，计算了(f(Q))引力中静态球对称黑洞附近的Dirac量子场熵，发现熵仍与视界面积成正比，但其系数被RVB温度的三次方因子修正，并在二次型模型(f(Q)=Q+αQ^{2})下得到了显式表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在修正引力理论（如(f(Q))引力）框架下，黑洞热力学性质（尤其是量子场熵）尚未被充分研究，特别是Dirac场在弯曲时空中的熵计算需要结合更精确的方法进行推广。

Method: 采用Robson–Villari–Biancalana（RVB）留数修正方案修正Hawking温度，并利用薄膜态计数（thin-film state-counting）方法，通过近视界WKB模密度（WKB mode density）和费米子自由能（fermionic free energy）计算Dirac场熵。具体步骤包括推导(f(Q))变形度量下的Hamilton–Jacobi方程、径向动量、模式数，并在留数修正温度下获得熵。

Result: Dirac场熵在正则化后仍与黑洞视界面积成正比，但其比例系数被RVB温度的三次方因子所修正。对于二次型模型(f(Q)=Q+αQ^{2})，得到了熵的显式解析表达式。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法有效推广了Dirac场熵的计算至(f(Q))引力的静态球对称黑洞，揭示了修正引力理论中熵-面积关系的修正形式，并给出了具体模型下的解析结果。

Abstract: We compute the entropy of a Dirac quantum field near a static, spherically symmetric black hole in (f(Q)) gravity by combining the residue-based Robson--Villari--Biancalana method with the thin-film state-counting approach. The RVB prescription introduces a residue correction to the Hawking temperature, while the Dirac field entropy is obtained from the near-horizon WKB mode density and fermionic free energy. For an (f(Q))-deformed metric, we derive the Hamilton--Jacobi equation, radial momentum, mode number, and entropy at the residue-corrected temperature. The result shows that the Dirac-field entropy remains proportional to the horizon area after regularization, but its coefficient is modified by a cubic RVB temperature factor. An explicit expression is obtained for the quadratic model (f(Q)=Q+αQ^{2}).

</details>


### [6] [Classical Corrections to Black Hole Entropy II](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31211)
*Daulet Berkimbayev,Martin Blaschke*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文重新审视黑洞生长的一比特吸收模型，将其视为离散递归而非连续方程。针对 Schwarzschild Tangherlini 黑洞，离散处理给出预期的面积标度并产生对数修正；扩展到 Reissner-Nordström 情形后，对数系数获得显式电荷依赖。研究还区分了动力学熵、热力学态熵、历史熵与隐藏条件熵，指出多项分布公式仅是一种受限历史计数结果，并不能证明不同历史对应唯一或相同的微观黑洞态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典的比特吸收模型通常采用连续方程描述黑洞生长。本文的动机在于重新以离散递归（discrete recursion）的方式处理该模型，以期揭示连续处理可能忽略的修正项，并进一步将分析推广到带电黑洞情形，澄清历史计数与微观态计数之间的区别。

Method: 将一比特吸收模型重新表述为离散递归关系（而非连续方程）；一比特在此定义为以自然对数单位度量的基本吸收单元。对 Schwarzschild Tangherlini 黑洞进行离散分析，得到面积标度（area scaling）与对数修正项（logarithmic correction）；随后将构造扩展至固定电荷的 Reissner-Nordström 黑洞。进一步通过正电荷、负电荷与中性标签构建有序历史（ordered histories）并定义形式系综（formal ensemble）。

Result: 离散处理产生预期面积标度及对数修正，修正系数由质量步长的维度依赖固定。在 Reissner-Nordström 情形中，对数系数获得显式的电荷依赖（explicit charge dependence）。带电吸收影响初始截断，而大质量递归控制弱电荷终态的支配熵。有序历史构成形式系综而非直接对微观态计数；在酉描述中，不同历史可对应相同的约化宏观态。添加质量或能量标签可降低端点简并度，但无法完全消除。

Conclusion: 该修正解释将动力学熵（dynamical entropy）、热力学态熵（thermodynamic state entropy）、历史熵（history entropy）与隐藏条件熵（hidden conditional entropy）区分开来。多项分布公式（multinomial formula）仅为一种受限历史计数结果，并非不同历史对应唯一或相同微观黑洞态的证据。

Abstract: We reconsider the classical one bit absorption model of black hole growth as a discrete recursion rather than a continuum equation. In this paper, one bit means one elementary absorption unit measured in natural logarithmic units. For a Schwarzschild Tangherlini black hole, the discrete treatment gives the expected area scaling and also produces a logarithmic correction. The coefficient of this correction is fixed by the dimensional dependence of the mass step. We then extend the construction to the Reissner Nordström case at fixed charge. In this sector, the logarithmic coefficient gains an explicit charge dependence. The fixed charge calculation can be interpreted as the large mass neutral growth stage after a charged seed has already formed. In that interpretation, realistic charged absorption affects the initial cutoff, while the large mass recursion controls the dominant entropy for weakly charged final states. We also study ordered histories built from positively charged, negatively charged, and neutral labels. These histories define a formal ensemble rather than a direct count of black hole microstates. In a unitary description, two different histories may lead to the same reduced macroscopic state, described by mass, charge, and entropy, while remaining different in hidden or environmental degrees of freedom. Adding a mass or energy label reduces the endpoint degeneracy, but it does not remove it in the ensembles considered here. The corrected interpretation separates dynamical entropy, thermodynamic state entropy, history entropy, and hidden conditional entropy. It also clarifies that the multinomial formula is a restricted history counting result, not a proof that different histories correspond to unique or identical microscopic black hole states.

</details>


### [7] [Stability and instability of torus-symmetric Einstein spacetimes with square-integrable connection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31585)
*Bruno Le Floch,Philippe G. LeFloch*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究了T³流形上具有T²对称性的爱因斯坦方程（Einstein equations）的全局演化问题，涵盖真空、标量场和可压缩流体物质模型。在面积规范（areal gauge）下，通过引入新的流体和几何变量，将爱因斯坦-欧拉系统（Einstein-Euler system）重新表述为带约束的非线性平衡律一阶系统，并建立了首个非微扰、全局存在性与稳定性理论，允许连接系数仅为平方可积，从而同时允许多脉冲引力波和激波。主要结果包括面积叶层的全局存在性定理、适定初值的非线性稳定性定理以及几何振荡数据的非线性不稳定性定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在T²对称性下，为爱因斯坦方程与物质场（真空、标量场、可压缩流体）的耦合系统建立非微扰（non-perturbative）的全局存在性与稳定性理论，特别是允许连接系数（connection coefficients）仅为平方可积（square-integrable）的弱正则性框架，以同时涵盖脉冲引力波（impulsive gravitational waves）和激波（shock waves）这两类重要的奇异性。

Method: 在面积规范下引入新的流体和几何变量，将爱因斯坦-欧拉系统重新表述为一个带约束的非线性平衡律（balance laws）一阶系统，并赋予其熵结构（entropy structure）。该形式化框架具有双曲性（hyperbolicity）、零形式（null forms）、熵流（entropy currents）、散度-旋度结构（div-curl structure）、最大值原理（maximum principles）和时空估计（spacetime estimates）。

Result: 主要结果包括三个定理：面积叶层（areal foliation）的全局存在性定理；适定初值（well-prepared initial data）的非线性稳定性定理；几何振荡数据（geometrically oscillatory data）的非线性不稳定性定理，后者会导致应力-能量张量（stress-energy tensor）产生测度修正。在未来收缩（future-contracting）区域，面积函数在非真空Gowdy对称和真空环面对称情况下一般会退化到零，导致几何奇点；在未来膨胀（future-expanding）区域，面积叶层是完备的。

Conclusion: 该研究在非微扰和弱正则性设定下，为T²对称的爱因斯坦-物质系统建立了全局存在性与稳定性理论。即使Weyl曲率（Weyl curvature）沿类时超曲面（timelike hypersurfaces）集中为Dirac质量、Ricci曲率仅为可积时，方程组依然有意义。这表明该框架能够描述比传统方法更广泛的奇异性行为，包括脉冲引力波和激波的共存。

Abstract: We study the global evolution problem for the Einstein equations under T2 symmetry on T3, allowing vacuum, scalar-field, and compressible-fluid matter models, governed by a general equation of state including isothermal and polytropic fluids. Under this symmetry, we obtain the first non-perturbative, global existence and stability theory with connection coefficients being merely square-integrable, which allows both impulsive gravitational waves and shock waves. In areal gauge, we introduce new fluid and geometric variables and reformulate the Einstein-Euler system as a first-order system of nonlinear balance laws with constraints and an entropy structure. The resulting formulation exhibits hyperbolicity, null forms, entropy currents, div-curl structure, maximum principles, and spacetime estimates. This leads to a notion of tame Einstein-Euler flow for which the essential geometric and fluid variables are square-integrable (finite energy), and the secondary variables are absolutely continuous (or, more generally, of bounded variation). In this non-perturbative and weak regularity setting, the equations remain meaningful even when the Weyl curvature concentrates into Dirac masses along timelike hypersurfaces, and the Ricci curvature remains only integrable. Our main results are a global existence theorem for areal foliations, a nonlinear stability theorem for well-prepared initial data, and a nonlinear instability theorem for geometrically oscillatory data, the latter producing measure corrections to the stress energy tensor. In the future-contracting regime, the areal foliation reaches a geometric singularity where the volume of T3 spatial slices degenerates to zero. The areal function reaches zero generically in the non-vacuum Gowdy-symmetric and vacuum torus-symmetric cases. In the future-expanding regime, the areal foliation is complete.

</details>

# cs.CE [[Back]](#toc)

### [8] [Can dents and gouges compromise the structural integrity of hydrogen transport pipelines?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31560)
*R. Das,B. Bezensek,E. Martínez-Pañeda*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文通过实验与数值模拟相结合，构建了一个针对大塑性应变场景的氢脆（hydrogen embrittlement）模型，用于评估天然气管道改造为氢气输送管道后，外部缺陷（dent和gouge）在氢气暴露下的结构完整性。模型经X65管线钢实验验证，发现仅在氢气完全无法从管道外表面逸出的极端条件下，氢才会显著加剧缺陷损伤。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将天然气管道改用于氢气输送（hydrogen transport）时，需明确外部缺陷（如凹痕dents和划痕gouges）在氢气暴露环境下如何影响管道的结构完整性（structural integrity），目前对此缺乏系统性的理论模型与实验验证。

Method: 采用实验与模型相结合的方法：构建了一个针对大塑性应变（large plastic straining）的氢脆模型，包含(i)多陷阱氢输运（multi-trap hydrogen transport）、(ii)有限应变塑性（finite-strain plasticity）以及(iii)依赖于氢浓度和应力三轴度（triaxiality）的损伤判据；分别通过氢渗透实验、全尺寸压痕实验和不同氢浓度与三轴度下的力学试验对模型的各组分进行验证。

Result: 验证后的模型被用于分析被动缺陷（先压痕后暴露于氢气）和主动缺陷（在氢气中压痕）两类场景。结果表明，除非氢气从管道外表面的逸出（egress）被完全阻断，且管道内部存在预先形成的被动凹痕与划痕并承受内压，否则氢气不会显著增加这些缺陷的损伤严重程度。

Conclusion: 氢气对管道外部缺陷损伤的加剧作用仅在极其严苛的条件下成立（内外压力差导致氢无法从外表面逸出），这意味着在大多数实际工况下，氢气对含缺陷的X65管线钢管道结构完整性的影响有限。

Abstract: Repurposing natural gas pipelines for hydrogen transport requires understanding how external defects, like dents and gouges, affect structural integrity under H$_2$ exposure. To address this, we combine experiments with a new hydrogen embrittlement model aimed at large plastic straining scenarios, which integrates: (i) multi-trap hydrogen transport, (ii) finite-strain plasticity, and (iii) a hydrogen- and triaxiality-dependent damage law. Each constituent of the model is validated with experiments on X65 pipeline steel: (i) hydrogen permeation, (ii) full-scale pipe-indentation, and (iii) mechanical testing at different hydrogen and triaxiality levels. The validated model is used to study \textit{passive} (indent before H$_2$ exposure) and \textit{active} (indent with H$_2$) dents and gouges. Results reveal that hydrogen does not significantly increase the damage severity of those defects, unless hydrogen egress is completely precluded at the outer surface of a pipeline that is being pressurised internally and contains a pre-existing \textit{passive} dent with a gouge.

</details>

### [9] [Reconciling GW170817 and GW190814 with a Nonmonotonic Sound-Speed Equation of State](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30369)
*Marlon M. S. Mendes,Odilon Lourenço da Silva Filho,César H. Lenzi*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文通过约束演化TOV发现管道（CETD）在广义相对论（General Relativity）框架内，发现了一组结构化因果状态方程（EoS）盆地，成功调和了GW170817与GW190814两个引力波事件之间的张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决GW170817与GW190814两个引力波观测事件在致密星状态方程（equation of state, EoS）约束上存在的张力（tension）。

Method: 采用约束演化TOV发现管道（Constrained Evolutionary TOV Discovery pipeline, CETD），在广义相对论（General Relativity）框架内系统搜索满足因果性（causality）条件的状态方程空间。

Result: 发现了一个包含约1.4×10^4条唯一状态方程（EoS）的结构化盆地（basin），最大质量（M_max）范围为2.3–2.8 M_⊙，1.4倍太阳质量下的半径（R_1.4）为11.97–12.29 km，对应的潮汐形变参数（Λ_1.4）不超过580，且声速平方（c_s²/c²）呈现双峰结构，峰值达0.86–0.99。

Conclusion: GW170817与GW190814之间的张力可以在广义相对论（General Relativity）框架内，通过一类特定的结构化因果状态方程（EoS） basin得到调和，无需引入超出广义相对论的新物理。

Abstract: We show that the GW170817-GW190814 tension can be reconciled within General Relativity by a structured causal EoS basin found with a Constrained Evolutionary TOV Discovery pipeline (CETD). The basin contains ~1.4x10^4 unique EoS with M_max = 2.3-2.8 M_sun, R_1.4 = 11.97-12.29 km, Lambda_1.4 <= 580, and double-peaked sound speeds reaching c_s^2/c^2 = 0.86-0.99.

### [10] [Magnetic Eruption and Nucleosynthesis in GRνMHD Simulations of Spinning Neutron Star Mergers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30548)
*Allen Wen,Jay V. Kalinani,Michail Chabanov,Manuela Campanelli,Riccardo Ciolfi,Yosef Zlochower*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文通过三维广义相对论磁流体动力学（general relativistic magnetohydrodynamics, GRMHD）模拟，研究了自旋对齐与反平行于轨道角动量的双中子星并合，发现自旋对齐可产生更多冷中子富潮汐抛射物与更准直的极向喷流，而反平行自旋则破坏磁场放大并阻碍磁驱动风；并合后极向流出物被中微子再处理产生富质子物质（$Y_e \geq 0.49$），合成包括$^{56}Ni$在内的轻r过程元素，但抛射物密度与速度不足以产生典型短伽马射线暴（short gamma-ray burst）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有双中子星并合（binary neutron star merger）模拟多假设无自旋或仅考虑特定自旋配置，对自旋如何影响并合动力学、磁场演化、抛射物及核合成尚缺乏系统理解。本文旨在通过包含自旋对齐与反平行配置的模拟，系统评估自旋对长寿命遗迹形成与早期演化的作用。

Method: 采用三维广义相对论磁流体动力学（GRMHD）模拟等质量双中子星并合，考虑不同中子星自旋构型（无自旋、自旋与轨道角动量对齐/反平行），并耦合二阶矩中微子输运（second-moment neutrino transport），追踪长寿命遗迹的形成与早期演化。

Result: 自旋对齐配置在赤道面释放更多冷中子富潮汐抛射物（cold, neutron-rich tidal ejecta），产生更准直的极向喷流；反平行自旋导致并合碰撞更剧烈，破坏磁放大，阻碍磁驱动风。无自旋与自旋对齐情形下，极向流出物受到强中微子再处理（neutrino reprocessing），产生$2.4\times10^{-3}\,M_\odot$富质子物质（$Y_e \geq 0.49$），合成包括$^{56}Ni$在内的轻r过程元素；但所有抛射物密度和速度均不足以解释典型短伽马射线暴。

Conclusion: 自旋构型显著影响双中子星并合的动力学、抛射物性质与核合成产物；自旋对齐可增强极向流出物的准直性与中微子再处理效应，产生独特的电磁信号（如$^{56}Ni$衰变信号），但典型短伽马射线暴仍需其他机制或更极端条件解释。

Abstract: We present three-dimensional general relativistic magnetohydrodynamics simulations of equal-mass binary neutron star mergers with varied neutron star spin configurations and second-moment neutrino transport, following the formation and early evolution of long-lived remnants. We compare a fiducial irrotational binary with binaries having spins that are aligned or antialigned with the orbital angular momentum, and examime how spin affects the merger dynamics, magnetic field evolution, outflows, and nucleosynthesis. Compared to the fiducial case, the aligned spin configuration releases more cold, neutron-rich tidal ejecta in the equatorial plane, which enables the development of a more tightly collimated polar outflow erupting from the remnant and inner accretion disk. Conversely, the case with spins antialigned with the orbit experiences a more violent collision at merger, disrupting magnetic amplification, loading the environment with debris, and impeding the propagation of magnetically driven winds. Strong neutrino reprocessing of the polar outflow in the irrotational and aligned spin cases produces $2.4\times 10^{-3}\,M_\odot$ of proton-rich ($Y_e \geq 0.49$) material, resulting in the synthesis of light r-process elements including $^{56}Ni$, whose subsequent decay potentially sends a unique electromagnetic signal from long-lived remnants. However, the outflows remain too dense and slow to be consistent with typical short gamma-ray bursts.

</details>

### [11] [Experiments on Settling of Granular and Cohesive Material in Low Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30395)
*Matthias Keulen,Timo Giese,Kolja Joeris,Jonathan Kollmer*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本研究通过落塔实验模拟低重力环境，测量了三种不同粒度和粗糙度的颗粒样品（细玄武岩、粗玄武岩、玻璃珠）在不同人工重力下的沉降体积与堆积密度，发现低重力下堆积密度降低、体积增大，且细玄武岩对重力变化最敏感，表明颗粒体积变化不仅依赖于粒径，还受粗糙度与均匀性影响，并为弱引力环境下的理论模型提供了实验验证数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 行星或小行星等岩石天体的表土（regolith）在不同于地球重力的条件下沉降，颗粒物质（granular material）的行为难以在不同重力下直接缩放。当颗粒间黏附力（cohesive inter-particle forces）与重力相当时，系统高度复杂，亟需模拟与实验来预测其行为。

Method: 利用ZARM落塔提供的零重力（zero g）环境，结合高精度线性平移台（linear stage）人工施加150、250、500、750和1000 mm/s²的模拟重力（覆盖从大行星到接近月球重力范围），观察三种颗粒样品（细玄武岩1–200 μm、粗玄武岩2–5 mm、玻璃珠750–1000 μm）的沉降过程并测量其堆积密度（packing density）。

Result: 低重力下颗粒样品体积更高、堆积密度更低；细玄武岩对重力变化最敏感，在250 mm/s²时体积增加+19.6%；粗玄武岩次之，在150 mm/s²时体积增加+12.2%；玻璃珠最不敏感，在250 mm/s²时体积仅增加+4.25%。

Conclusion: 颗粒沉降体积变化不仅受粒径（particle size）影响，还与颗粒粗糙度（roughness）和均匀性（uniformity）有关；实验结果为理论工作提供了真实实验数据验证，并强调了低重力环境下黏附力（cohesive force）的重要作用。

Abstract: The regolith of rocky bodies, such as planets or asteroids, generally settles under gravity conditions different from those of Earth. The behavior of granular material is not easily scalable for different gravities. To predict these highly complex systems where cohesive inter particle forces can be comparable to gravitational forces, we need simulations and experiments. We did experiments on settling of three different granular samples in varying reduced gravities and examined their packing densities. We used a high precision linear stage to artificially induce reduced gravities inside the zero $g$ environment provided by the ZARM drop tower and observe the settling of our samples. The three samples were fine basalt with particle diameters of $1\text{-}200\,μ$m, coarse basalt with $2\text{-}5\,$mm and glass beads with $750\text{-}1000\,μ$m. The artificial gravities were $150,\,250,\,500,\,750$ and $1000\,$mm/s$^2$ and therefore ranged from large asteroid gravity to almost moon gravity. We saw the granular samples have higher volumes in lower gravities and therefore lower packing densities, we also saw the fine basalt be the most sensitive to changes in gravity, up to $+19.6\,\%$ in volume for $250\,$mm/s$^2$, followed by the coarse basalt particles, up to $+12.2\,\%$ for $150\,$mm/s$^2$ and the glass beads packing density being the least sensitive to changes in gravity, up to $+4.25\,\%$ for $250\,$mm/s$^2$. With these experiments we show change in volume is not solely dependent of particle size but also roughness and uniformity, we provide real life experimental data to validate theoretical works and highlight the role of cohesive forces in low gravity environments.

</details>

### [12] [Non-Abelian Dirac oscillator in a uniform Yang--Mills background: spin--isospin mixing and singlet--triplet splitting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30403)
*Abdelmalek Boumali*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了与平面狄拉克振子（Dirac oscillator）耦合的 \(U(2)=U(1)\times SU(2)\) 杨-米尔斯（Yang-Mills）背景场，通过泡利约化（Pauli reduction）框架对角化非阿贝尔场强算子，得到了双重简并对齐分支和两个混合分支的本征值，并澄清了符号约定、极限情形及与完整一阶狄拉克对角化的区别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索平面狄拉克振子在含有非阿贝尔（non-Abelian）规范背景场下的能谱结构，特别是通过构造特定的Dossa–Avossevou型规范组态，研究阿贝尔磁场 \(B\)、非阿贝尔空间振幅 \(\beta\) 和非阿贝尔标量振幅 \(\rho\) 对谱的联合影响。

Method: 采用泡利约化（Pauli-reduced）形式，将非阿贝尔场强算符表示为 \(\mathbb{C}^{2}_{\mathrm{spin}}\otimes\mathbb{C}^{2}_{\mathrm{iso}}\) 上的常算符，包含对角内部塞曼（internal-Zeeman）项 \(\sigma^{3}T^{3}\) 和非对角自旋-同位旋耦合项 \(\sigma^{1}T^{1}+\sigma^{2}T^{2}\)。通过对该算符进行对角化得到本征值。

Result: 对角化得到三个本征值：对齐分支 \(\lambda_{\mathrm{FM}}=g^{2}\beta^{2}/(4m)\)（双重简并），以及两个混合分支 \(\lambda_{S}=-g^{2}\beta(\beta-2\rho)/(4m)\) 和 \(\lambda_{T}=-g^{2}\beta(\beta+2\rho)/(4m)\)。对齐的内部塞曼尺度在 \(\beta\) 上呈二次型，而单态-三重态（singlet–triplet）分裂在 \(\beta\rho\) 上呈线性。

Conclusion: 修正后的公式明确了符号约定，验证了主要极限情形，区分了泡利约化谱与完整一阶狄拉克（Dirac）对角化的结果，并澄清了数值插图的物理含义。

Abstract: We investigate a planar Dirac oscillator coupled to a spatially uniform \(\utwo=\uone\times\su\) Yang--Mills background. The gauge configuration, adapted from the Dossa--Avossevou construction, contains an Abelian magnetic field \(B\), a non-Abelian spatial amplitude \(β\), and a non-Abelian scalar amplitude \(ρ\). Within the Pauli-reduced formulation, the non-Abelian field strength produces a constant operator on \(\mathbb{C}^{2}_{\mathrm{spin}}\otimes\mathbb{C}^{2}_{\mathrm{iso}}\). This operator contains a diagonal internal-Zeeman contribution proportional to \(σ^{3}T^{3}\) and an off-diagonal spin--isospin term proportional to \(σ^{1}T^{1}+σ^{2}T^{2}\). Its diagonalization gives a doubly degenerate aligned branch and two mixed branches with eigenvalues \[ λ_{\mathrm{FM}}=\frac{g^{2}β^{2}}{4m},\qquad λ_{S}=-\frac{g^{2}β(β-2ρ)}{4m},\qquad λ_{T}=-\frac{g^{2}β(β+2ρ)}{4m}. \] Consequently, the aligned internal-Zeeman scale is quadratic in \(β\), whereas the singlet--triplet separation is linear in \(βρ\). The revised formulation makes the sign conventions explicit, verifies the main limiting cases, distinguishes the Pauli-reduced spectrum from a full first-order Dirac diagonalization, and clarifies the physical meaning of the numerical illustrations.

</details>


### [13] [Axions Create Singularities on Extremal Horizons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30411)
*Gary T. Horowitz,Maciej Kolanowski,Grant N. Remmen,Jorge E. Santos*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文指出，轴子（axion）会导致极端黑洞（extremal black holes）具有奇异视界（singular horizons），这一效应在黑洞旋转且带有任意小的非零电荷时几乎普遍成立。随着轴子质量增大，该奇异性与更高导数修正引发的奇异性相关。在远离极端条件时，该效应会在近极端视界附近产生异常大的潮汐力（tidal forces），导致有效理论失效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究轴子对极端黑洞视界奇点结构的影响，并考察轴子质量与耦合参数变化下奇异性出现的条件及其与已知高阶导数修正奇异性之间的关系。

Method: 通过理论分析，研究轴子场与旋转带电黑洞的相互作用，考察不同轴子质量与耦合强度下视界奇点的存在性，并与爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦方程（Einstein-Maxwell equations）的高阶导数修正效应进行对比。

Result: 轴子在几乎所有参数范围内都会导致旋转且带有任意小非零电荷的极端黑洞出现奇异视界；当轴子质量较大时，该奇异性与高阶导数修正引起的奇异性一致。在非极端情形下，近极端视界附近会产生异常大的潮汐力，导致有效理论失效。

Conclusion: 轴子效应普遍破坏极端黑洞视界的正则性，并在近极端区域引发有效理论的崩溃，表明轴子-引力耦合对黑洞解的结构具有深远影响。

Abstract: We show that axions cause extremal black holes to have singular horizons. This is true for almost all values of the axion mass and coupling provided the black hole is rotating and has some arbitrarily small nonzero charge. When the axion mass becomes large, these singularities are related to the recently discovered singularities induced by higher-derivative corrections to the Einstein-Maxwell equations. Away from extremality, this effect produces anomalously large tidal forces in the vicinity of near-extremal horizons, causing breakdown of the effective theory.

</details>


### [14] [Logarithm of charge ratio in black hole entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30417)
*Muktajyoti Saha,Ashoke Sen,P. Shanmugapriya*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本研究从宏观和微观两方面计算了BPS黑洞熵中的对数修正项，发现在𝒩=4和𝒩=8超对称弦紧化中两者完美匹配，并强调了正确选择紫外截断、路径积分测度、场变量及系综的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: BPS黑洞熵的对数修正常包含涉及电荷大比值（large ratios of charges）的项，而电电荷远大于磁电荷时弦耦合（string coupling）的吸引子值很小，有望从宏观侧使用弱耦合弦理论计算此类对数修正。本文旨在系统验证宏观与微观计算结果的一致性。

Method: 作者在平坦时空（flat space-time）中、在四维𝒩=2、𝒩=4和𝒩=8超对称弦紧化（supersymmetric string compactifications）背景下，对保留四个超荷的黑洞进行宏观对数修正计算。计算中考虑了四项关键效应：1）使用正确的紫外截断（ultra-violet cut-off，弦尺度而非普朗克尺度）；2）正确的路径积分测度（ultra-local measure，含适当的膨胀子依赖度量）；3）正确的路径积分变量（Kalb-Ramond 2-形式而非对偶轴子）；4）正确系综（从巨正则到微正则）。此外，验证了所用测度与弦场论的BV形式（BV formalism）一致。

Result: 对于𝒩=4和𝒩=8理论，宏观计算结果与已知的微观结果完全吻合（perfect agreement）。本文还确认所采用的路径积分测度与弦场论BV形式主义导出的测度一致。

Conclusion: 宏观计算中需正确选择紫外截断尺度、路径积分测度、场变量（Kalb-Ramond 2-形式）及系综（微正则系综），才能与微观结果相匹配。这为弦理论中黑洞熵的对数修正提供了自洽性检验。

Abstract: Logarithmic correction to BPS black hole entropy, computed from microscopic description, often contains terms involving large ratios of charges, besides the logarithmic terms involving the overall scale of the charges. If the electric charges are much larger than the magnetic charges, then the attractor value of the string coupling is small and one might hope to use weakly coupled string theory to compute logarithmic corrections involving ratios of charges from the macroscopic side. We compute these for black holes in flat space-time, preserving four supercharges, in $\mathcal{N} = 2$, $\mathcal{N}=4$ and $\mathcal{N}=8$ supersymmetric string compactifications in four dimensions. We find perfect agreement with the microscopic results in $\mathcal{N}=4$ and $\mathcal{N}=8$ theories, for which the microscopic results are known. Various stringy and statistical mechanical effects become important in this analysis, including 1) use of the correct ultra-violet cut-off (string scale instead of Planck scale), 2) correct path integral measure (ultra-local measure with appropriate dilaton dependent metric), 3) use of the correct path integral variable (Kalb-Ramond 2-form instead of the dual axion) and 4) change of ensemble (from grand canonical to microcanonical). We also verify that the measure we use is consistent with what follows from the BV formalism of string field theory.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在共形场论（CFT）描述中，复上同调由Ramond-Ramond基态张成，Hodge分解由U(1)×U(1) R-荷决定，理性结构由BPS边界态提供，偏振由开弦Witten指标诱导。Hodge轨迹由保持N=(2,2)超共形代数且在谱流生成元上可逆作用的非平凡拓扑缺陷范畴TDL的存在来识别。

Result: 在Hodge轨迹上的特殊点，范畴TDL展现出额外的算术结构，允许嵌入具有复乘（Complex Multiplication）的数域（number fields）的有限乘积，从而对理论的边界态施加了更强的约束。

Conclusion: 该构造具有一般性，并在椭圆曲线和K3曲面两种情形下得到了详细验证，表明该sigma模型类比为弦论中Hodge轨迹的研究提供了统一的框架。

Abstract: We propose a sigma-model analogue of Hodge loci in the moduli space of geometric Calabi-Yau compactifications, characterized by the emergence of non-trivial rational Hodge endomorphisms, using generalized symmetries. In the CFT description, the complex cohomology is spanned by Ramond-Ramond ground states, the Hodge decomposition is determined by the $U(1)\times U(1)$ R-charges, and the rational structure is provided by BPS boundary states, with polarization induced by the open string Witten index. Hodge loci are identified by the existence of a non-trivial category $TDL$ of topological defects preserving the $N=(2,2)$ superconformal algebra and acting invertibly on the spectral-flow generators. At special points on these loci, the category $TDL$ exhibits additional arithmetic structure and admits embeddings of finite products of number fields with Complex Multiplication, leading to stronger constraints on the boundary states of the theory. Although the construction is general, we analyze in detail the cases of elliptic curves and $K3$ surfaces.

### [16] [Spectral Admissibility of Real Observers in Euclidean de Sitter Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30423)
*Ricardo Espíndola,Ahmed Farag Ali*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文针对欧几里得德西特（Euclidean de Sitter）路径积分中观测者（observer）的经典半可容许性（semiclassical admissibility）问题，提出了一种基于形式域判据（form-domain criterion）的数学框架，用于判定哪些观测者扇区能够与德西特鞍点耦合为真正的度规观测者，并构造了一个满足该判据的局域化带隙时钟探测器（localized gapped clock-detector）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Maldacena的构造表明，引入一个合适的实观测者能够重整化精细态计数问题，但在此之前需要回答一个先行的经典半可容许性问题：哪些观测者扇区能够与德西特鞍点偶合为真正的度规观测者（genuine metric observers），而非沦为旁观者（spectators）或产生红外奇异的反作用（infrared-singular backreaction）。

Method: 在S^D上，通过规范固定（gauge fixing）和零模投影（zero-mode projection）后，观测者的二次影响由舒尔补（Schur complement）决定。论文建立了一个形式域判据：若观测者核（observer kernel）为正且混合度规-观测者源（mixed metric-observer source）在施加Δ_{ΦΦ}^{-1/2}后有界，则诱导的度规修正是所选通道上的有界二次型扰动（bounded quadratic-form perturbation）。在有隙情形下，利用Δ_{ΦΦ}≥m_*^2 1给出范数界；度规耦合的软模（soft modes）则产生随1/ε增长的修正。论文证明了充分性定理，并构造了一个具有内部振荡子的局域化带隙时钟探测器，在涂抹世界线（smeared worldline）上满足该判据。

Result: 建立了半经典可容许观测者的数学判据：在任意具有强制性形式（coercive form）Q_{gg}^P ≥ δ_P ‖h‖^2的稳定通道上，当‖Δ_{ΦΦ}^{-1/2} 𝔧_P‖_{op}^2 < δ_P时，高斯鞍点（Gaussian saddle）保持可控。构造的局域化带隙时钟探测器满足该判据，并给出了可计算的界限及S^4上相对于圆球TT尺度的基准（benchmark）。论文指出，共形通道（conformal channel）仅作为不定（indefinite）或等值线定义（contour-defined）的扇区处理，有界性不意味着正定性（positivity）。

Conclusion: 该判据识别了半经典可容许的观测者类别。相位抵消（phase cancellation）只有在该类与相关共形或负模扇区（negative-mode sector）重叠，并与独立的等值线或态计数方案（contour or state-counting prescription）结合时才会发生。

Abstract: The Euclidean de Sitter path integral contains the familiar phase associated with conformal negative modes. Maldacena's construction shows that a suitably included real observer can reorganize the refined state-counting problem. This paper does not rederive that cancellation. It addresses the prior semiclassical admissibility question: which observer sectors couple to the de Sitter saddle as genuine metric observers without becoming spectators or producing infrared-singular backreaction? On $S^D$, after gauge fixing and zero-mode projection, the observer's quadratic influence is governed by a Schur complement. We formulate a form-domain criterion: if the observer kernel is positive and the mixed metric-observer source is bounded after applying $Δ_{ΦΦ}^{-1/2}$, the induced metric correction is a bounded quadratic-form perturbation on the chosen channel. In the gapped case, $Δ_{ΦΦ}\geq m_*^2\mathbf{1}$ gives $\|K^\dagger Δ_{ΦΦ}^{-1} K\|_{\rm op} \leq \|K\|_{\rm op}^2/m_*^2$; metric-coupled soft modes produce corrections growing as $1/\varepsilon$. We prove a sufficiency theorem: on any stable channel with coercive form $Q_{gg}^P \geq δ_P \|h\|^2$, the Gaussian saddle remains controlled whenever $\|Δ_{ΦΦ}^{-1/2} \mathfrak{j}_P\|_{\rm op}^2 < δ_P$. We construct a localized gapped clock-detector with internal oscillators on a smeared worldline that satisfies the criterion with a computable bound and gives explicit $S^4$ benchmark versus the round-sphere TT scale. The conformal channel is treated only as an indefinite or contour-defined sector; boundedness does not imply positivity. The criterion identifies the semiclassically admissible observer class. Phase cancellation follows only when this class overlaps the relevant conformal or negative-mode sector and is combined with an independent contour or state-counting prescription.

</details>

Method: 通过分析自举法在势能包含不同类型函数（如多项式与指数项）时的失效情况，指出歧义性问题；并提出三种可能的解决方案（three possible resolutions）。

Conclusion: 自举法存在未被充分认识的歧义性问题，需要通过作者提出的三种方案加以解决。

Abstract: The bootstrap method for quantum mechanics is a powerful tool for computing the energy eigenvalues of a Hamiltonian. However, we point out that this method suffers from an ambiguity problem: it fails to yield the correct spectrum when the potential contains different types of functions, such as polynomial and exponential terms. ### [18] [Vertex Operators in Superstring Theory from Integral Forms and Descent Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30759)

TL;DR: 本文基于超黎曼曲面（super Riemann surfaces）上的积分形式（integral forms），为超弦理论（superstring theory）中的顶点算子（vertex operators）发展了一种几何表述。通过推导下降方程（descent equations），建立了超几何对象与鬼超场（ghost superfields）之间的对应关系，并将反图像改变算子（inverse picture-changing operators）纳入统一的下降结构（universal descent structure），所有算子在BRST上同调（BRST cohomology）中均有良好定义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从已积分的NS-NS顶点算子出发，推导连接不同鬼数和图像数的下降方程；将微分形式$dz-θdθ$与$dθ$分别识别为鬼超场及其超导数；引入反图像改变算子以跨越不同图像扇区（picture sectors）；建立高鬼数算子的超场构造（superfield construction）。

Result: 建立了超几何对象与鬼超场之间的对应关系，实现了超鬼结构（superghost structure）的几何化；反图像改变算子生成了跨图像扇区的新的下降序列；高鬼数算子的超场构造需要比玻色情形（bosonic case）更多的额外项。

Conclusion: 所有算子被组织成一个统一的下降结构，并在BRST上同调中具有良好定义，从而为超弦理论中顶点算子的几何基础提供了系统而一致的框架。

Abstract: We develop a geometric formulation of vertex operators in superstring theory based on integral forms on super Riemann surfaces. Starting from the integrated NS-NS vertex operator, we derive descent equations that relate operators with different ghost and picture numbers. A key result is a correspondence between supergeometric objects and ghost superfields, in which the one-form $dz-θdθ$ and the even differential $dθ$ are identified with the ghost superfield and its superderivative. This provides a geometric realization of the superghost structure. We further extend the construction by incorporating inverse picture-changing operators, which generate new descent sequences across different picture sectors. We also introduce a superfield construction of higher-ghost-number operators, for which additional terms are required compared to the bosonic case. All operators are organized into a universal descent structure and are well-defined in BRST cohomology.

### [19] [A Boolean-Lattice Perspective for All-Loop Two-Site Cosmological Wavefunction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30797)
*Yanfeng Hang,Cong Shen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明了两站点（two-site）宇宙学波函数系数（wavefunction coefficients）的移位树分解（shifted-tree decomposition）与管状构造（tubing construction）本质上是同一布尔格（Boolean lattice）恒等式的两种不同实现，并通过有限差分算子的乘积、极大链展开（maximal-chain expansion）以及立方体积分（cubical integral）给出了代数与几何两种互补的证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者旨在将此前提出的两站点移位树分解公式（arXiv:2410.17192）推广到任意圈阶（loop order）的泡泡状图族（bubble-like family），并揭示该公式与管状构造之间的深层数学联系。

Method: 方法包括：将移位树分解的非平凡中心部分化简为移位对角除子（shifted diagonal divisors）的交错子集和（alternating subset sum），该和由内部能量（internal energies）对应的布尔格自然组织；将其重写为有限差分算子（finite-difference operators）的乘积作用在种子除子（seed divisor）上；从有限差分形式出发，先得到布尔格上的顶点展开（vertex expansion），再推导出极大链展开；最后分别通过代数（telescoping relation）和几何（立方体积分与单纯形分解）两种路径证明该恒等式。

Result: 得到两个主要结果：（1）移位树分解的中心部分等价于一个基于内部能量布尔格的极大链展开公式；（2）恢复两站点公共前因子（prefactor）后，该极大链展开恰好重现了圈级波函数系数的管状表示（tubing representation）。

Conclusion: 移位树分解与管状构造是同一个布尔格恒等式的两种实现，从而为全圈阶两站点公式提供了具体的几何解释。

Abstract: We revisit the shifted-tree decomposition formula proposed in our previous work arXiv:2410.17192 for two-site cosmological wavefunction coefficients. For the two-site bubble-like family at arbitrary loop order, we show that the nontrivial central part of the decomposition reduces to an alternating subset sum over shifted diagonal divisors. This subset sum is naturally organized by the Boolean lattice associated with the internal energies, and can be rewritten as a product of commuting finite-difference operators acting on a seed divisor. The finite-difference form first gives a vertex expansion on the Boolean lattice and then leads to an equivalent maximal-chain expansion over complete filtrations from the empty subset to the full set of internal energies. We prove this maximal-chain formula in two complementary ways. Algebraically, the identity follows from a telescoping relation for products of shifted divisors. Geometrically, the finite-difference expression is represented by a cubical integral over the Boolean cube, while the maximal-chain expansion gives its simplex decomposition. After restoring the common two-site prefactor, this maximal-chain expansion reproduces the tubing representation of the loop-level wavefunction coefficient. Thus the shifted-tree decomposition and the tubing construction are two realizations of the same Boolean-lattice identity, providing a concrete geometric interpretation of the all-loop two-site formula.

### [20] [Towards Bulk Locality: A Systematic Construction of Contact Interactions from Chord Diagrams](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30970)
*Hao Dai,Yi-Li Wang,Yu-Ge Chen,Li-Guo Qin,Li-Jun Tian*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于任意周期格点大小的Fock空间通量模型构建一般性框架，阐明晶格维度如何控制探针构型（probe configuration）与体接触顶点（bulk contact vertex）；发展系统匹配方案（systematic matching scheme），并利用弦路径积分形式计算三至六点接触关联函数。

Result: 成功重现了包含对数奇异性（logarithmic singularities）在内的一大类AdS₂标量接触Witten图，证明弦图在完全一般性（full generality）下为体接触相互作用提供了微观描述。

Abstract: Chord diagrams encode boundary correlators in the double-scaled holographic Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev model, but currently capture only a limited class of bulk interactions that yield pure power-law correlators. In this article, we investigate a general construction based on Fock-space flux models with arbitrary periodic lattice size, clarifies how lattice dimensions control probe configurations and bulk contact vertices. Developing a systematic matching scheme and using the chord path integral formalism, we compute three- to six-point contact correlators and reproduce a broad class of AdS$_2$ scalar contact Witten diagrams, including those with logarithmic singularities. The results demonstrate that chord diagrams, in full generality, provide a microscopic description of bulk contact interactions and thereby establish a principled framework for reconstructing bulk locality from boundary data.

### [21] [Brane flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31181)
*Georgios Papadopoulos,Kostas Skenderis*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文基于有效D膜作用量（effective D-brane actions），将里奇流（Ricci flow）推广到包含n-形式场强（n-form field strength）的流理论，并进一步推广至带有陈-西蒙斯项（Chern-Simons term）的引力作用量，证明了在适当场依赖体积固定条件下流的单调性，以及稳态流孤子（steady flow solitons）均为梯度孤子（gradient solitons）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的里奇流及其广义形式（generalised Ricci flows）无法涵盖带有高阶形式场强（n≥0）的理论，且对于带有陈-西蒙斯项的引力系统的流行为缺乏系统分析。

Method: 基于有效D膜作用量，将里奇流推广到包含n-形式场强的理论；借鉴Perelman的方法，引入场依赖的固定体积条件以证明流的单调性；对带有陈-西蒙斯项的引力作用量，调整了Perelman方案的适配方式，构造了新的泛函（functional）。

Result: 证明了在合适的场依赖体积固定条件下流是单调的；所有稳态流孤子都是梯度孤子，这在一定条件下意味着存在一个使其他场保持不变的基灵矢量场（Killing vector field）；对于带有陈-西蒙斯项的情形，同样证明了流的单调性以及稳态流孤子均为梯度孤子。

Conclusion: 该推广统一了里奇流与广义里奇流，并拓展至陈-西蒙斯型引力系统；梯度孤子的特例包括NS5膜和D5膜，相应的固定体积分别为T-对偶不变体积（T-duality invariant volume）及S-对偶体积（S-dual volume）；稳态孤子的性质对孤子几何（geometry of solitons）具有重要推论。

Abstract: Based on effective D-brane actions, we present a generalisation of the Ricci flow that includes the flow of a theory with a $n$-form field strength for $n\geq 0$. This is a generalisation of both the Ricci flows and the generalised Ricci flows. Following Perelman, we show that flows that keep a suitable field-dependent volume fixed are monotonic. We also show that all steady brane flow solitons are gradient solitons and use this to demonstrate that on some occasions this implies the existence of a Killing vector field that leaves all the other fields invariant. Particular cases of gradient solitons are NS5 and D5 branes, and the volume which is kept fixed in these cases is the T-duality invariant volume (NS5 brane) or its S-dual (D5 brane). We also generalise the above analysis to gravitational actions coupled to form gauge potentials that also exhibit a Chern-Simons type term. We find an alteration is required in the adaptation of Perelman's modification to this case, which yields a new functional that also exhibits a Chern-Simons term. Under suitable assumptions, we proceed to prove the monotonicity of the flow and that all steady flow solitons are gradient solitons. We also explore the consequences of the last statement on the geometry of solitons.

### [22] [Higher-Derivative Corrections to Reissner--Nordström Black Holes from Worldline QFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31331)
*Siddarth Ajith,Ravisankar Rajagopal,Nur Rifat,Diana Vaman,Kent Yagi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文推导了在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦作用量中添加高阶导数 $RF^2$ 项（黎曼张量与麦克斯韦场强平方的缩并）后，Reissner-Nordström 黑洞的修正。采用世界线量子场论方法得到领头阶后闵可夫斯基修正，并通过求解修正的场方程以闭合形式验证了结果（对牛顿常数 $G$ 至所有阶）。讨论了修正黑洞的第一定律并计算了熵。极值黑洞温度的非负性恰好对应弱引力猜想（weak gravity conjecture）的满足，该条件排除了 Drummond-Hathrell 理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高阶导数 $RF^2$ 项在有效场论（effective field theory）框架下自然出现，研究其对 Reissner-Nordström 黑洞的修正是理解广义相对论在量子引力效应下的有效描述的重要步骤。

Method: 采用世界线量子场论（wordline QFT）方法计算领头阶后闵可夫斯基（post-Minkowskian）修正；同时通过求解修正的爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦场方程获得闭合形式解，该解对牛顿常数 $G$ 成立至所有阶。

Result: 得到了 $RF^2$ 项对 Reissner-Nordström 黑洞的修正；极值黑洞温度的非负性等价于弱引力猜想（weak gravity conjecture）的成立；该温度条件排除了 Drummond-Hathrell 理论。

Conclusion: $RF^2$ 高阶导数项对黑洞解和热力学性质的修正与弱引力猜想存在深层联系，后者可作为排除某些有效场论（如 Drummond-Hathrell 理论）的理论判据。

Abstract: In this paper we derived the corrections to the Reissner-Nordström black hole when higher-derivative $RF^2$ terms (contractions of the Riemann tensor with the Maxwell field strength squared) are added to the Einstein-Maxwell action. Such terms arise naturally in the context of effective field theories. We used wordline QFT methods to obtain the leading order post-Minkowskian corrections. We verified these results by solving the modified Einstein-Maxwell field equations in closed form, to all orders in Newton's constant $G$. We discussed the first law and computed the entropy of the perturbed black holes. The extremal black hole temperature is non-negative precisely when the weak gravity conjecture is satisfied. This condition on the extremal black hole temperature rules out Drummond-Hathrell theory.

</details>


### [23] [Two roles of Alexander in two Kashaev phases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31588)
*Dmitry Galakhov,Alexei Morozov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文指出复兴理论（resurgence theory）的关键特征是非微扰行为的歧义性，并以陈-西蒙斯理论（Chern-Simons theory）的Kashaev极限为典型示例，揭示了Alexander多项式在经典A-多项式和Jones微扰展开中的双重对立角色，最终通过准经典极限下两个不同分支的共存消解了这一悖论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复兴理论中的非微扰歧义性需要通过具体可解模型加以阐明；陈-西蒙斯理论中的Wilson圈平均在双标度极限（large representation and small coupling）下的行为，有望推广至任意杨-米尔斯理论（Yang-Mills），但其中Alexander多项式扮演了看似矛盾的两种角色，这一谜题需要澄清。

Method: 采用可精确求解的模型，重点分析陈-西蒙斯理论在Kashaev极限（即双标度极限）下的Wilson圈平均；运用准经典/WKB近似（quasiclassical/WKB approximation）进行理论处理，并对比经典A-多项式（classical A-polynomials）与Jones多项式在微扰展开中的行为。

Result: 经典A-多项式与Alexander多项式（Alexander polynomials）具有共同的根，而Jones多项式在微扰展开中趋于Alexander多项式的逆（Δ⁻¹）；量子A-多项式具有特殊形式，为两种行为的共存提供了自洽性；准经典极限下存在两个不同分支（相）：一个具有非平凡经典作用量，导出经典A-多项式和双曲体积（hyperbolic volumes）；另一个经典作用量为零，导出逆Alexander多项式。

Conclusion: Alexander多项式在经典A-多项式和Jones微扰展开中的对立角色并非矛盾，而是源于准经典极限下两个不同分支（相）的共存；这一发现为理解复兴理论中的非微扰歧义性提供了新的视角，并可推广至一般杨-米尔斯理论。

Abstract: The crucial feature of resurgence theory is the ambiguity of non-perturbative behavior, reflected either in the different choices of integration contours or in the existence of several solutions to Ward identities. This is well illustrated by considering exactly solvable models, of which the prominent example is Chern-Simons theory. Its important chapter, which should have a direct generalization to arbitrary Yang-Mills, is the consideration of Wilson averages in the double-scaling limit of large representation and small coupling. For historical reasons, we call it a Kashaev limit. It possesses a natural interpretation in terms of quasiclassical/WKB approximation, which is, however, somewhat peculiar and thus sheds new light on the old story. The crucial point is the appearance of Alexander polynomials $Δ$ in two seemingly opposite roles: the classical $A$-polynomials have common roots with $Δ$, while Jones polynomials tend to $Δ^{-1}$ in the perturbative expansion. The consistency is provided by the peculiar form of the quantum $A$-polynomial, and the resolution of the puzzle is the co-existence of two different branches (phases) in the quasiclassical limit -- with non-trivial and with vanishing classical actions. The first leads to classical $A$-polynomials and hyperbolic volumes, the second -- to inverse Alexanders.

</details>

### [24] [Superconductor-"Metal" Transition of One-dimensional Interacting Bosons with Ohmic Quantum Dissipation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30746)
*Miguel A. Cazalilla*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了一维晶格上具有在位相位耗散（dissipation）的相互作用玻色子（库珀对）系统的相图，通过与附近扩散性正常金属电极的约瑟夫森隧穿描述耗散。在公度填充下，系统存在两种量子相：具有长程相位相干的耗散玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（D-BEC）或超导体，以及具有指数衰减相位关联的耗散莫特绝缘体（D-Mott）或“金属”。从微观“玻色子液滴”图像出发，推导了用于描述准一维导线超导体-金属转变的耗散含时金兹堡-朗道理论，并证明了D-Mott/D-BEC转变属于Wilson-Fisher普适类（dynamical exponent z≈2）。文章还分析了小掺杂下D-Mott相的稳定性及大掺杂下D-BEC相的基态特性，并与一维玻色子莫特绝缘体阵列在光学晶格中的退禁闭转变进行了比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解一维系统中耗散对量子相变的影响，特别是相互作用玻色子系统在耦合到耗散性电极时的相图（phase diagram）结构及临界行为。

Method: 结合多种解析技术，包括微扰论（perturbation expansion）、映射到赝自旋链（pseudospin chain）并结合玻色化（bosonization）方法，以及从微观液滴图像推导耗散含时金兹堡-朗道（Ginzburg-Landau）理论。

Result: 发现了D-BEC/superconductor和D-Mott/metal两种量子相；推导了Sachdev等人提出的唯象耗散含时金兹堡-朗道理论的微观基础；表明D-Mott/D-BEC转变属于Wilson-Fisher普适类（universality class），动态临界指数z≈2；给出了D-Mott相在有限掺杂下的可压缩性（compressibility）的一阶修正。

Conclusion: 该系统的量子相变具有明确的普适类归属，且D-BEC相在任意小的非零耗散下仍可成为大掺杂区的基态。此外，该转变与一维玻色子莫特绝缘体阵列在光学晶格中的退禁闭转变（deconfinement transition）既有相似性也有差异。

Abstract: The phase diagram of a system of interacting bosons (Cooper pairs) hoping on a one-dimensional (1D) lattice with onsite phase dissipation describing the Josephson tunneling to a nearby diffusive normal-metal electrode is studied. Starting from the system at commensurate lattice filling, it is shown by a combination of analytical techniques that the phase diagram contains two quantum phases: A dissipative Bose-Einstein condensate (D-BEC) or superconductor with long-range phase coherence, and a dissipative Mott insulator (D-Mott) or "metal" with exponentially decaying phase correlations in space and local imaginary-time correlations decaying as the local pairing correlations of the electrode. The D-Mott/metal phase can be described as a 1D array of dissipative boson puddles, weakly coupled by Josephson tunneling. The puddle size roughly corresponds to the length scale beyond which phase slips suppress phase coherence. The dissipative time-dependent Ginsburg-Landau theory phenomenologically used by Sachdev, Werner, and Troyer [Phys. Rev. Lett. {\bf 92} 237003 (2004)] for the superconductor-metal transition in quasi-1D wires is derived from this microscopic puddle picture. Thus, the criticality of the D-Mott/D-BEC transition is shown to belong to the Wilson-Fisher universality class with dynamical exponent $z\approx 2$. At small doping, the D-Mott/metal phase remains stable due to its finite compressibility, which is computed to leading order in a perturbation expansion of the dissipation strength and the inter-puddle Josephson coupling. At larger doping, using a mapping to a pseudospin chain combined with bosonization, the D-BEC/superconductor phase is the ground state for non-vanishing but arbitrarily small dissipation. Similarities and differences with deconfinement transition of an array 1D bosonic Mott insulators in anisotropic optical lattices are also discussed.

</details>


### [25] [Spin Hall effect in two-dimensional materials with inverted bands and Mexican-hat dispersion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30881)
*Bagun S. Shchamkhalova,Vladimir A. Sablikov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有“墨西哥帽”色散（Mexican hat dispersion）和环形费米面（ring-shaped Fermi surface）的二维拓扑绝缘体（two-dimensional topological insulators）中的自旋霍尔效应（spin Hall effect），发现由二阶散射过程产生的外禀自旋霍尔电流（extrinsic spin-Hall current）可显著超过由贝里曲率（Berry curvature）引起的内禀贡献，并且由于墨西哥帽色散，该电流表现出非常规的费米能量依赖性，甚至可能改变符号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在具有墨西哥帽色散和环形费米面的二维拓扑绝缘体中，能带反转导致的电子态结构独特，电子在不同等能轮廓间的跃迁以及能带态的量子度量（quantum metric）对输运性质有重要影响。然而，这类材料中自旋相关的散射机制及外禀自旋霍尔效应的具体行为尚不清楚，需要系统研究。

Method: 研究了由二阶散射过程（second-order scattering processes）实现的自旋依赖斜散射（spin-dependent skew scattering），分析了外禀自旋霍尔电流与内禀自旋霍尔电流的对比，并考察了自旋霍尔电流随费米能量（$E_F$）的变化关系。

Result: 外禀自旋霍尔电流可显著大于由贝里曲率引起的内禀自旋霍尔电流；由于墨西哥帽色散，外禀自旋霍尔电流随费米能量呈现非常规依赖：在某一费米能量处达到最大值，随后随费米能量增加而下降，甚至可能改变符号。

Conclusion: 这种复杂行为反映了多种因素能量依赖性的相互竞争，包括轮廓间与轮廓内跃迁概率以及两个轮廓中不同的电子速度。

Abstract: We study the spin Hall effect in two-dimensional topological insulators with "Mexican hat" dispersion and a ring-shaped Fermi surface which are formed due to the band inversion. Electron transitions between different isoenergetic contours and the quantum metric of band states play an important role in the transport properties of such materials, since they largely determine the spatial distribution of the electron charges screening the impurity potential and the scattering probability [Phys.B, 719, 417942 (2025)]. Here we study a spin-dependent skew scattering, which is enabled by the second-order scattering processes, and show that the extrinsic spin-Hall current (SHC) can significantly exceed the intrinsic SHC arising from the Berry curvature. Furthermore, due to Mexican-hat dispersion, the SHC exhibits a very unusual dependence on the Fermi energy ($E_F$). The extrinsic SHC reaches a maximum at some $E_F$, then decreases with increasing $E_F$ and can even change a sign. This complicated behavior reflects an interplay of energy dependencies of such important factors as probabilities of inter- and intra-contour transitions, as well as different electron velocities in two contours.

</details>


### [26] [Pure Spin Photocurrent in Altermagnetic Photovoltaic Battery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30909)
*Qiang Li,Shibo Fang,Zongmeng Yang,Xingyue Yang,Jianhua Wang,Rui Peng,Lin Zhu,Shuhua Wang,Dexing Liu,Min Zhang,Dahua Ren,Mai Zhang,Han Zhang,Yee Sin Ang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一种由两个交变磁电极夹一层非磁性半导体构成的交变磁自旋光伏电池（altermagnetic spin photovoltaic battery），基于第一性原理量子输运模拟证明该器件可在无净磁化条件下产生纯自旋光电流，且自旋向上和自旋向下光电流大小相等、符号相反，为交变磁结构中光驱动纯自旋电流的产生提供了现实可行的路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统铁磁体（ferromagnets）和反铁磁体（antiferromagnets）在自旋电子学应用中存在局限，而交变磁体（altermagnets）具有无净磁化但依赖动量的自旋劈裂（momentum-dependent spin splitting）特性，有望提供新的自旋电子学功能平台。本文旨在利用交变磁体的独特性质实现光驱动的纯自旋电流（pure spin current）生成。

Method: 采用第一性原理量子输运模拟（first-principles quantum-transport simulations），构建V2Te2O/ZnSe/V2Te2O异质结，其中两个交变磁电极的奈尔矢量（Néel vectors）方向相反，中间层为非磁性半导体ZnSe，通过光照驱动自旋相关输运。

Result: 该交变磁结在两种电极奈尔矢量相反时，可产生纯自旋光电流（pure spin photocurrent），自旋向上与自旋向下光电流大小相等、符号相反。该效应在线偏振光（linearly polarized light）和圆偏振光（circularly polarized light）下均能保持，并可通过光子能量（photon energy）和偏振角（polarization angle）进行调控。

Conclusion: 研究结果证明交变磁结可作为一种可行的光驱动纯自旋电流发生器，为超越传统铁磁和反铁磁材料的自旋电子学器件设计提供了新的实现途径。

Abstract: Altermagnets, featuring momentum-dependent spin splitting without net magnetization, provide a promising platform for spintronic functionalities beyond conventional ferromagnets and antiferromagnets. Here, we propose an altermagnetic spin photovoltaic battery consisting of a nonmagnetic semiconducting layer sandwiched between two altermagnetic electrodes. Using first-principles quantum-transport simulations, we show that a V2Te2O/ZnSe/V2Te2O junction supports a pure spin photocurrent for opposite Néel vectors in the two altermagnetic electrodes, with spin-up and spin-down photocurrents equal in magnitude and opposite in sign. The effect persists under both linearly and circularly polarized light and remains tunable with photon energy and polarization angle. Our results establish a realistic route toward light-driven pure spin-current generation in altermagnetic junctions.

</details>


### [27] [Interplay of Cl Substitution and He$^{+}$ Irradiation in CrSBr$_{1-x}$Cl$_{x}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31134)
*Satyam Sahu,Adeel Bukhari,Arijit Kayal,Valerie Černá,Bing Wu,Aljoscha Söll,Gregor Hlawacek,Zdeněk Sofer,Martin Kalbáč,Matěj Velický,Otakar Frank*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过极化分辨拉曼光谱（polarization-resolved Raman spectroscopy）分析了Cl取代和He⁺辐照对二维磁性半导体CrSBr振动响应的影响，发现两种缺陷工程均显著重构了拉曼光谱并增强了电子-声子耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维磁性半导体为研究无序、晶格动力学和共振光-物质相互作用提供了有前景的平台，其中CrSBr具有强面内各向异性和显著的共振增强拉曼散射，因此有必要探索缺陷工程对其振动响应的影响。

Method: 采用极化分辨拉曼光谱（polarization-resolved Raman spectroscopy），在近共振1.96 eV激发条件下，对Cl取代和He⁺辐照处理的CrSBr样品进行振动响应测量，并结合功率依赖测量分析非线性拉曼响应。

Result: Cl取代激活了与局域对称性破缺相关的新声子模；He⁺辐照引入了缺陷相关的散射通道并增强了声子展宽；两者的联合效应导致拉曼光谱发生强各向异性重构，并在近共振激发下改变了非线性拉曼响应。功率依赖测量显示，本征和取代诱导的声子模均呈现稳健的超线性标度（superlinear scaling）行为。

Conclusion: 即使在缺陷工程样品中，共振增强的电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）仍然持续存在，表明CrSBr在调控缺陷的同时能够保持其共振光学特性。

Abstract: Two-dimensional magnetic semiconductors provide a promising platform for exploring the interplay between disorder, lattice dynamics, and resonant light--matter interactions. Among them, CrSBr exhibits strong in-plane anisotropy and pronounced resonance-enhanced Raman scattering. Here, we investigate the effects of Cl substitution and He$^{+}$ irradiation on the vibrational response of CrSBr using polarization-resolved Raman spectroscopy. Cl substitution activates additional phonon modes associated with local symmetry breaking, while He$^{+}$ irradiation introduces distinct defect-related scattering channels and enhanced phonon broadening. The combined effects of alloy disorder and externally introduced defects lead to strong anisotropic reconstruction of the Raman spectra and modification of the nonlinear Raman response under near-resonant 1.96 eV excitation. Power-dependent measurements reveal robust superlinear scaling of both intrinsic and substitution-induced phonon modes, indicating persistent resonance-enhanced electron--phonon coupling even in defect-engineered samples.

### [28] [The geometry of the CISS effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31166)
*P. Hedegård,A. Kazimir,C. Lamers,L. T. Baczewski,T. N. H. Nguyen,C. Tegenkamp*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究通过扫描隧道显微镜系统性地测量了手性分子与金属基底界面的磁电阻效应，观察到磁电阻信号随磁化方向、分子手性和分子取向的改变而发生反转。提出将分子关联为一个轴矢量（axial vector）来解释实验现象，并指出该轴矢量对应的轴向磁极化（axial magnetic polarization）而非电极化（electric polarization）是产生界面磁矩的关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性诱导自旋选择性（CISS）效应的微观起源尚未明确，尤其是在分子与金属接触界面的磁电阻信号反转机制缺乏统一理论解释。

Method: 利用扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy, STM）结合精心挑选的手性分子和锚定基团，系统性开展了系列磁电阻（magnetoresistance）实验。

Result: 观察到磁电阻信号随磁化方向、分子手性和分子取向的改变而发生反转。将分子视为一个轴矢量（axial vector），结合基底磁化矢量（vector）和分子取向矢量，可以统一解释所有观测结果，包括那些未观察到CISS相关磁电阻的零结果实验。

Conclusion: 分子自身的电极化（polar electrical polarization）不直接参与CISS磁电阻效应，而轴向磁极化矢量算符（axial magnetic polarization vector operator）是更合理的候选机制，它在分子与金属引线界面处产生磁矩（magnetic moment）的过程中起到关键作用。

Abstract: Using scanning tunneling microscopy, and a careful selection of chiral molecules and anchoring groups, we systematically carried out a series of magnetoresistance experiments. We observed a reversal of the signal upon changing the magnetization direction, the molecular chirality, and the molecular orientation. The orientation of the molecules and the magnetization of the substrate are vectors, and by associating an axial vector with the molecule, the observations can be explained. Other recent experiments, among them null experiments showing no CISS related magnetoresistance can be explained using our framework. The physical interpretation is, that the polar electrical polarization of the molecule cannot play a direct role, while the axial magnetic polarization vector operator is a much more realistic candidate. This vector plays an important role in the creation of a magnetic moment in the interface between molecule and metallic lead.

</details>


### [29] [Surface lone-pair polarization probed by quantum-geometric transport in tellurium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31197)
*Nathanael N. Batista,Wendel S. Paz,Manuel Suárez-Rodríguez,Pierpaolo Fontana,Victor Velasco,Marcus V. O. Moutinho,Chang Niu,Peide D. Ye,Marco Gobbi,Fèlix Casanova,Luis E. Hueso,Caio Lewenkopf,Marcello B. Silva Neto*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用量子几何输运（quantum-geometry transport）探测三角晶系碲（trigonal tellurium）中表面孤对电子极化（surface lone-pair polarization），建立了表面极化场与线性及非线性输运系数的微观联系，并指出整流电压与表面极化直接成正比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 孤对电子（lone pair）是分子和固体中极性的微观来源，但其在晶体中的集体行为常被对称性掩盖或局限于表面，缺乏有效的探测手段。

Method: 通过量子几何输运方法，分析表面孤对电子极化作为反演奇偶性的偶极分量对布洛赫波包（Bloch wavepacket）质心及速度的量子几何修正；构建最小三组分晶格模型描述极化织构（polar texture）。

Result: 线性输运系数探测净极化场的二阶矩（second moment），非线性输运系数探测其一阶矩（first moment）；碲薄片中的整流电压直接正比于表面孤对电子极化强度。

Conclusion: 该工作为理解和设计基于碲同素异形体的极化驱动量子几何电子器件提供了微观路径。

Abstract: Stereochemically active lone pairs are ubiquitous microscopic sources of polarity in molecules and solids, but their collective behavior in crystals is often hidden by symmetry or confined to surfaces. Here we show that quantum-geometry transport provides a sensitive probe of surface lone-pair polarization in trigonal tellurium. This surface polarization appears microscopically as an inversion-odd dipolar component of the crystal potential, which shifts the center of mass of Bloch wavepackets and produces quantum-geometric corrections to their velocity. We describe this lone-pair polar texture through a minimal three-component lattice model, and we show that the resulting linear and nonlinear transport coefficients probe, respectively, the second and first moments of the net polarization field. Because rectified voltages in tellurium flakes are directly proportional to the surface lone-pair polarization, our results provide a microscopic route to understanding and engineering polarization-driven, quantum-geometric electronic devices based on tellurium allotropes.

</details>


### [30] [Valley-polarized Orbital and Spin Magnetism Induced by Femtosecond Optical Pulses in Two-Dimensional Semiconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31263)
*M. S. Mrudul,Peter M. Oppeneer*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用含时密度矩阵形式（time-dependent density-matrix formalism）理论研究了二维有隙狄拉克系统中的自旋与轨道磁性的超快产生，揭示了二者在光-物质耦合机制、时间动力学以及对退相干的敏感性上的根本差异，并指出轨道磁矩对飞秒磁性调控的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过渡金属二硫属化物等二维六方半导体具有谷选择性光学选择定则（valley-selective optical selection rules），其能带的谷对比磁性织构（valley-contrasting magnetic texture）为超快磁性调控提供了新的可能性。然而，自旋与轨道磁矩在激光驱动下的产生机制与动力学行为的差异尚不清楚，亟需系统理论分析。

Method: 采用含时密度矩阵形式（time-dependent density-matrix formalism），对具有自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的二维有隙狄拉克系统（two-dimensional gapped Dirac system）进行理论计算，模拟圆偏振激光脉冲在共振和多光子共振条件下产生的非平衡磁化。

Result: 通过调节驱动光子的能量和偏振，可以分别控制诱导的自旋与轨道磁矩。轨道磁矩直接耦合外电场，表现出更快的动力学及显著的拉比振荡（Rabi-like oscillations）；自旋响应则通过自旋-轨道耦合逐渐演化。此外，轨道动力学对电子-空穴退相干（electron-hole dephasing）的敏感度显著高于自旋响应。

Conclusion: 轨道磁矩在飞秒时间尺度磁性调控中扮演关键角色，未来相关技术需充分考虑轨道贡献。该研究为理解二维材料中自旋与轨道磁性的超快光控提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate the ultrafast generation of spin and orbital magnetism in a two-dimensional gapped Dirac system with spin-orbit coupling. This system is representative of two-dimensional hexagonal semiconductors, such as transition-metal dichalcogenides that exhibit valley-selective optical selection rules arising from the valley-contrasting magnetic texture of their band structure. Using a time-dependent density-matrix formalism, we demonstrate that circularly polarized laser pulses generate nonequilibrium magnetization under both resonant and multiphoton resonant conditions. We show that the induced spin and orbital magnetic moments can be distinctly controlled via the photon energy and polarization of the driving field. Furthermore, spin and orbital dynamics originate from fundamentally different light-matter coupling mechanisms, leading to qualitatively dissimilar temporal behaviors. The orbital magnetic moment couples directly to the external electric field, resulting in faster dynamics and pronounced Rabi-like oscillations, whereas the spin response develops gradually through spin-orbit coupling. Consequently, orbital dynamics is significantly more sensitive to electron-hole dephasing than the spin response. Our results highlight the importance of properly accounting for orbital contributions in future technologies that utilize femtosecond control of magnetism.

### [31] [Feasibility study of continuous electronic Pomeranchuk cooling with a flavor-degenerate Wigner crystal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31307)
*Robin J. Dolleman,Ammon Fischer,Lennart Klebl,Alexander Rothstein,Dante M. Kennes,Bernd Beschoten,Florian Libisch,Christoph Stampfer*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出并模拟了一种片上冷却循环方案，利用平带材料中电子液体（EL）与维格纳晶体（WC）之间的熵差，通过电流驱动实现连续冷却，使电子温度降至亚毫开尔文（sub-millikelvin）水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在纳米电子器件中实现亚毫开尔文电子温度可揭示新输运现象、延长量子相干时间并提升量子计量精度，但持续维持这一低温状态长期构成挑战。

Method: 在具有局域栅极的器件中通入电流，通过调节栅下载流子密度形成WC相；载流子从电子液体（EL）相转变为WC相时熵增加而吸热，滑移的WC将热量沿器件传输，再在载流子转变回EL相时释放热量，从而建立稳态温度梯度。

Result: 模拟显示，在足够低的电流密度（通常低于1 nA/μm）下可实现净冷却；在4 mK浴温下，栅极区域内的冷却功率可达8.4 aW/μm。该方法适用于具有低能味简并（谷和/或轨道）且无序度低的平带材料。

Conclusion: 该方案可在合适条件下使电子温度远低于1 mK，为实现该温区的连续片上冷却提供了一条有前景的路径。

Abstract: Achieving sub-millikelvin electron temperatures in nanoelectronic devices could unveil new transport phenomena, extend quantum coherence times, and enhance the precision of quantum metrology. However, maintaining such low temperatures continuously remains a long-standing challenge. Here, we propose and simulate an on-chip cooling cycle that harnesses the entropy difference between an electron liquid (EL) and a Wigner crystal (WC) in flavor-degenerate flat-band materials. Cooling is driven by a current through a device with a locally gated region. Within this region, the charge carrier density is tuned such that a WC forms beneath the gate. As carriers transition from an EL to WC phase, their entropy increases, extracting heat and the sliding WC advects this heat along the device. The heat is then released when carriers transition back to the EL phase, which establishes distinct hot and cold regions and a steady temperature gradient over the device. Simulations show net cooling for sufficiently low current densities, typically below $1~\mathrm{nA}/μ\mathrm{m}$, whereas Joule heating dominates at higher currents. Within the gated region, we estimate cooling powers of up to $8.4~\mathrm{aW}/μ\mathrm{m}$ at a bath temperature of $4~\mathrm{mK}$. Our approach can achieve electron temperatures well below $1~\mathrm{mK}$ under suitable conditions, promising a route towards continuous on-chip cooling in this temperature regime. Our approach applies to any flat-band material with low-energy flavor degeneracy (valley and/or orbital) and low disorder, including gapped Bernal-stacked bilayer graphene, rhombohedral-stacked multilayer graphene, and magic-angle twisted bilayer graphene.

</details>


### [32] [Nonperturbative renormalization of Haldane pseudopotentials from the exact two-electron spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31537)
*G. -Q. Hai,M. T. Matsubara,L. Cândido,B. G. A. Brito*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过精确求解磁场中双电子相对运动问题，提出了一种非微扰方法来定义重整化哈登伪势（renormalized Haldane pseudopotentials）$V^*_{|m|}$，并引入动力学修正项$Δ_{|m|}=V^*_{|m|}-V_{|m|}$，从而在分数量子霍尔效应的有效相互作用理论中系统性地纳入非微扰朗道能级混合（Landau-level mixing）效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的分数量子霍尔（fractional quantum Hall）体系有效相互作用通过将库仑相互作用投影到最低朗道能级（lowest Landau level）来获得，忽略了向更高朗道能级的虚跃迁，这在高朗道能级混合强度下会失效。因此，需要一种非微扰方法来获得更精确的有效相互作用参数。

Method: 从磁场中双电子精确能谱出发，超越最低朗道能级近似求解相对运动问题，定义重整化伪势$V^*_{|m|}$，并计算动力学修正项$Δ_{|m|}=V^*_{|m|}-V_{|m|}$作为系统非微扰处理的量化结果。

Result: 动力学修正$Δ_{|m|}$始终为负，且强烈依赖于相互作用强度和相对角动量（relative angular momentum）；在弱耦合下精确结果复现了微扰朗道能级混合极限，而在强混合区域显著偏离低阶微扰展开结果。

Conclusion: 该方法为在分数量子霍尔系统有效相互作用理论中纳入非微扰朗道能级混合效应提供了微观框架，尤其在强相互作用体系（如ZnO/MgZnO异质结构）中，短程相互作用通道（short-range interaction channels）发生强烈重整化，显著改变了有效相互作用的层级结构。

Abstract: Haldane pseudopotentials $V_{|m|}$ provide the effective interaction parameters governing correlated states in the fractional quantum Hall regime. In conventional formulations, these quantities are obtained by projecting the Coulomb interaction onto relative-angular-momentum states within the lowest Landau level, thereby neglecting virtual transitions to higher Landau levels. Here, we formulate a nonperturbative description of effective interactions directly from the exact two-electron spectrum in a magnetic field. By solving the relative-motion problem beyond the lowest-Landau-level approximation, we define renormalized pseudopotentials $V^*_{|m|}$ from the exact eigenenergies and introduce dynamical corrections $Δ_{|m|}=V^*_{|m|}-V_{|m|}$. The corrections remain systematically negative and depend strongly on both interaction strength and relative angular momentum, reflecting dynamical correlation effects associated with higher-state virtual admixture. The exact results reproduce the perturbative Landau-level-mixing limit at weak coupling while exhibiting substantial deviations in the strong-mixing regime, signaling the breakdown of low-order perturbative expansions. In particular, the short-range interaction channels relevant to Laughlin-type correlations undergo strong renormalization, leading to substantial modification of the effective interaction hierarchy in strongly interacting systems such as ZnO/MgZnO heterostructures. The present formulation establishes a microscopic framework for incorporating nonperturbative Landau-level-mixing effects into effective interaction theories of quantum Hall systems.

</details>

### [34] [Rényi divergences and binary state discrimination error exponents for fermionic quasi-free states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31379)
*Milán Mosonyi,Gábor Maróti-Zareczky*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对二元独立同分布（i.i.d.）量子态区分问题中的误差概率权衡关系，在非独立同分布（non-i.i.d.）情形下，研究了平移不变且规范不变的准自由态（translation-invariant and gauge-invariant quasifree states）的一系列正则化Rényi散度（regularized Rényi divergences），给出了显式公式，并分析了不同模式数下的渐近经典行为与非交换性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非独立同分布（non-i.i.d.）量子态区分问题中，误差指数通常由正则化Rényi散度（regularized Rényi divergences）表达，但这些散度一般不具显式公式。本文旨在为一大类具有物理重要性的状态——双无限费米子链上的平移不变且规范不变的准自由态——提供多种正则化Rényi散度的显式解析表达式。

Method: 研究了双无限费米子链上的平移不变且规范不变的准自由态（translation-invariant and gauge-invariant quasifree states），给出了包括$(α,z)$型、对数欧几里得型（log-Euclidean）、最大型（maximal）、测量型（measured）及新近引入的积分型（integral）Rényi散度在内的多种正则化Rényi散度的显式公式。同时，将[Bunth等人2023年工作]的构造推广到每个格点具有多个模式的情形。

Result: 当每个格点仅有一个模式时，系统渐近地表现为经典行为，所有不同类型的正则化Rényi散度取值相等；而当每个格点有多个模式时，非交换性（non-commutativity）在正则化下持续存在，且对于固定$α$，正则化Rényi $(α,z)$-散度随不同参数$z$取不同值。此外，推广后的构造可获得一大类呈现超指数衰减（super-exponential decay）区分误差概率的状态。

Conclusion: 本文为平移不变且规范不变的准自由态提供了多种正则化Rényi散度的显式公式，揭示了单模情形下的渐近经典行为与多模情形下非交换性的持续存在，并构建了一类具有超指数误差衰减特性的状态，为量子态区分的误差指数分析提供了新的工具与见解。

Abstract: The trade-off relations between the two types of error probabilities in binary i.i.d. quantum state discrimination can be expressed by single-copy formulas in terms of the Petz-type and the sandwiched Rényi divergences of the two states representing the two hypotheses. In the non-i.i.d. setting, the error exponents can usually be expressed in terms of regularized Rényi divergences, which do not admit explicit formulas in general. Here, we consider a class of states, translation-invariant and gauge-invariant quasifree states on doubly infinite fermionic chains, and give explicit formulas for a wide range of regularized Rényi divergences between such states, including $(α,z)$, log-Euclidean, maximal, measured, and the recently introduced integral Rényi divergences. We show that the case where there is a single mode at each lattice site becomes asymptotically classical, with all the different types of regularized Rényi divergences being equal, while in the case of multiple modes per site, non-commutativity persists under regularization, and for any fixed $α$, the regularized Rényi $(α,z)$-divergences give different regularized values for different $z$ parameters in general. We also generalize a previous construction from [Bunth, Maróti, Mosonyi, Zimborás, Lett.~Math.~Phys.~113:(7), 2023] to the case of multiple modes per lattice site to obtain a large class of states exhibiting super-exponential decay of the discrimination error probabilities.

### [35] [Eigenstate chaos in the presence of non-Abelian symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30798)
*Siddharth Jindal,Pavan Hosur*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过非阿贝尔对称性分辨方法，将本征态热化假说（ETH）推广至具有紧致李群（如SU(2)）对称性的混沌本征态，建立了非阿贝尔微正则熵与纠缠熵之间的联系，并发现了依赖于全局卡西米尔荷的对数修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来对非对易守恒荷（non-commuting conserved charges）物 理以及非阿贝尔本征态热化假说（non-Abelian ETH）的兴趣日益增长，亟需将ETH推广至由一般紧致李群（compact Lie group）描述的对称性系统。

Method: 应用非阿贝尔对称性分辨（non-Abelian symmetry resolution）方法，发展非阿贝尔微正则熵（non-Abelian microcanonical entropy），并将其与混沌本征态的纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）建立联系。

Result: 微正则熵与对称性分辨纠缠熵（symmetry-resolved entanglement entropy）密切相关，后者相比常规纠缠熵存在普适的对数修正；修正行为依赖于全局卡西米尔荷（global Casimir charge，如总自旋）：有限荷密度下存在对数增强，零密度下纠缠熵无修正但微正则熵和对称性分辨纠缠熵出现对数减小。

Conclusion: 该研究工作为非阿贝尔本征态热化（non-Abelian eigenstate thermalization）提供了新的理论视角和定量结果。

Abstract: The eigenstate thermalization hypothesis (ETH) posits that energy eigenstates encode local properties of the microcanonical ensemble. Motivated by recent interest in the physics of non-commuting conserved charges and the non-Abelian ETH, we study chaotic eigenstates in the presence of symmetries described by general compact Lie groups, such as SU(2). By applying non-Abelian symmetry resolution, we develop a non-Abelian microcanonical entropy and relate this entropy to the entanglement entropy of chaotic eigenstates. We find that microcanonical entropy is closely related to the symmetry-resolved entanglement entropy, which differs from conventional entanglement entropy by a universal logarithmic correction. Our results depend on the global Casimir charge, e.g. total spin. At finite charge density, we find a logarithmic enhancement to conventional entanglement entropy. At zero density, we find no such correction to entanglement entropy, but a logarithmic reduction to microcanonical entropy and symmetry-resolved entanglement entropy. We discuss the implications of our approach for non-Abelian eigenstate thermalization.

### [36] [Dually tunable YBCO coplanar waveguide resonators based on helium-ion-generated Josephson inductances](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30425)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用高温铜氧化物超导体 YBa₂Cu₃O₇ (YBCO) 制备共面波导谐振腔，并利用聚焦氦离子束对 YBCO 进行可控局部辐照，以集成约瑟夫森电感（Josephson inductances）和量子干涉仪（quantum interferometers）。

Result: 获得了强可通量调谐的微波谐振器，展现出周期性的干涉振荡（interferometer oscillations）及叠加的夫琅禾费调制模式（Fraunhofer-like modulation pattern）；在高达 14 K 的温度下仍具有 promising 特性。

Conclusion: 该器件通过磁场单独调节每个约瑟夫森结的临界电流（critical current），实现了谐振频率与磁通响应度的独立调控，有望在宽频率范围内构建对外部磁噪声低灵敏度的可调谐微波电路。

Abstract: Superconducting microwave circuits with and without Josephson inductances are the Swiss Army knife for many experiments and technologies from quantum information science to astrophysical particle detectors. Despite a large variety of existing circuit types, thin film materials and Josephson junction technologies, a flexible and reliable platform for high-magnetic-field and high-temperature applications is yet to be found. In this manuscript, we investigate coplanar waveguide cavities made of the high-temperature cuprate superconductor YBa$_2$Cu$_3$O$_7$ (YBCO), integrated with Josephson inductances and quantum interferometers that are generated by the controlled local irradiation of the YBCO with a focused helium ion beam. We obtain strongly flux-tunable microwave resonators, which not only display periodic interferometer oscillations of resonance frequency and decay rate, but also a superimposed Fraunhofer-like modulation pattern. The latter originates from the magnetic field tuning of the individual Josephson junction critical currents due to the out-of-plane junction barriers. It allows adjusting resonance frequency and flux responsivity independently of each other, potentially enabling tunable microwave circuits with low sensitivity to external magnetic-field noise over a broad range of frequencies. Finally, we investigate the temperature dependence of the cavities, show that they have promising characteristics up to 14$\,$K, and present a model for the junction-induced cavity losses.

### [37] [Geometric dependence of critical-current variation in Al/AlO${\rm _x}$/Al Josephson junctions: a model-based analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30768)
*K. Kakuyanagi,N. Teran,H. Toida,S. Saito*
