Motivation: 实现约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）临界电流的均匀分布对于超导量子电路（superconducting quantum circuits）的大规模集成至关重要，因此需要定量识别导致临界电流变异的主导因素。

Method: 利用室温隧道电阻（room-temperature tunnel resistance）统计量分析Al/AlO_x/Al结临界电流的变异性，基于结的几何结构和沉积条件对变异来源进行建模，并比较各模型因素的贡献大小。

Result: 模型分析表明，铝膜厚度波动是所考虑因素中的主导变异来源；采用30°沉积角进行Dolan桥双角度沉积（Dolan-bridge double-angle deposition）制备双层结，可在9.75 mm方形区域内实现相对标准偏差1.2%，在1.5 mm方形区域内达到0.5%。

Conclusion: 优化沉积角度能够显著改善约瑟夫森结临界电流的均匀性，为超导量子电路的大规模集成提供了可行的工艺方案。

Abstract: Achieving uniform critical current across Josephson junctions is essential for the large-scale integration of superconducting quantum circuits. In this work, we statistically analyzed the variation of the critical current of Al/AlO${\rm _x}$/Al junctions using room-temperature tunnel resistance statistics, and identified the dominant contribution among the modeled sources of the variation based on their dependence on geometry and deposition conditions of junctions. Our model-based analysis reveals that fluctuations in the Al film thickness play the dominant role among the modeled contributing factors. Based on this analysis, we found that, in Dolan-bridge double-angle deposition, adopting a deposition angle of 30-degree for bilayer junctions significantly improves uniformity, yielding a relative standard deviation of 1.2% (0.5%) across a 9.75 mm (1.5 mm) square region.

</details>


### [38] [(Non-)Traversable Quantum Phase Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31472)
*Federico Balducci,Paul M. Schindler,Andrea Solfanelli,Marin Bukov*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于基态流形几何距离的量子相变新分类——可穿越（traversable）与不可穿越（nontraversable）量子相变，利用反绝热驱动（counterdiabatic driving）框架动态连接两相，揭示了该分类与已知分类（如序参量、重整化群不动点）的独立性，并讨论了其在态制备和绝热量子计算复杂性中的意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子相变表现为多体系统基态的突变，但这一突变是否必然排除两相之间的连续动力学连接仍是一个开放问题。现有分类（如基于序参量或重整化群不动点）未涉及这一几何方面的动力学可连接性。

Method: 利用反绝热驱动框架，显式构造了能够动态连接两个相的动力学方案（dynamical protocol）。通过分析热力学极限下基态流形之间的几何距离，将量子相变划分为可穿越（有限几何距离）和不可穿越（无穷几何距离）两类。

Result: 发现多类已知相变属于可穿越类，包括满足超标度关系（hyperscaling）的对称性破缺相变以及具有增强连续对称性的非连续相变。同时，存在不可穿越的量子相变，即使借助非局域反绝热驱动也无法动态穿越，因为需要发散振幅和频率；这类包括呈现平均场普适性（mean-field universality）的连续相变以及由亚稳极小竞争导致的非连续相变。

Conclusion: 该几何分类超越了已知的分类体系，独立于局域序参量和重整化群不动点，并对态制备（state preparation）的复杂性和绝热量子计算（adiabatic quantum computation）具有直接意义。

Abstract: Quantum phase transitions manifest as an abrupt change in the ground state of a many-body system; yet it is an open question whether this sudden change necessarily precludes a continuous dynamical connection between the two phases. We introduce a classification of quantum phase transitions based on this geometric aspect of the ground-state manifold, that differs from known classifications. By leveraging the framework of counterdiabatic driving, we explicitly construct schedules that dynamically connect one phase to another. This strategy allows us to uncover a large class of quantum phase transitions, where the states on both sides are separated only by a finite geometric distance in the thermodynamic limit. We term such transitions traversable, since exact counterdiabatic driving links the two phases via a finite dynamical protocol in the thermodynamic limit. We show that multiple known transitions fall into this class -- e.g., symmetry-breaking transitions obeying hyperscaling and discontinuous transitions with an enhanced continuous symmetry. We further show the existence of quantum phase transitions that cannot be crossed dynamically even with the help of nonlocal counterdiabatic driving, as they would require divergent amplitudes and frequencies. Geometrically, these nontraversable transitions correspond to an infinite distance separating the two phases of matter; we show that the class comprises continuous transitions exhibiting mean-field universality, and discontinuous transitions arising from the competition between metastable minima. Our geometric classification goes beyond the known taxonomy, is independent of local order parameters and renormalization group fixed points, and has direct implications for the complexity of state preparation and adiabatic quantum computation.

</details>

### [39] [Model-Agnostic Signal Discovery with Machine Learning: Bridging the Gap Between Theory and Practice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31103)
*Oz Amram,Marco Letizia,Mikael Kuusela*

Main category: physics.data-an

TL;DR: 本文综述了基于人工智能（AI）的无模型搜索策略（model-agnostic search strategies），该策略提供了一种与传统的依赖特定假设的搜索方式互补的新范式，优先考虑广泛的探索而非针对性的分析，旨在提升复杂科学数据中新现象的发现潜力，尤其适用于理论指导匮乏的领域。文章讨论了这些方法的概念框架、潜在陷阱以及验证与解释策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的新现象搜索高度依赖特定模型（model-dependent）和具体假设，导致搜索范围受限，无法全面覆盖可能的信号空间。为弥补这一不足，本文旨在综述基于AI的无模型搜索策略，提供一种互补范式，以在不依赖理论先验的情况下增强实验的总体发现能力。

Method: 本文为一篇综述性文章，系统梳理了基于AI的无模型搜索策略的主要类别及其背后的概念框架（conceptual framework），并讨论了这些方法的验证（validation）与解释（interpretation）策略。

Result: 文章识别出基于AI的无模型搜索策略是一种新兴的互补范式，已在高能物理（high-energy physics）领域率先提出。这些方法优先进行广泛探索，能够弥补传统依赖特定假设的搜索方式的局限性，尤其适用于理论指导较少的探索性研究场景。

Conclusion: 基于AI的无模型搜索策略有潜力显著提升现代实验的发现潜力。本文可作为从业者和对该领域感兴趣的研究人员了解这些策略的有用参考，为后续的方法开发和实际应用提供了概念基础与使用注意事项。

Abstract: Searches for new phenomena in complex scientific data are predominantly model-dependent, optimized for specific hypotheses, and therefore limited in their coverage of the space of possible signals. Recently, new AI-based model-agnostic search strategies, many of which have been pioneered in high-energy physics, have been proposed which provide a complementary paradigm, prioritizing broad exploration over tailored analyses. These techniques offer an opportunity to enhance the overall discovery potential of modern experiments, especially in regimes where theoretical guidance is scarce. In this document, we review the conceptual framework behind the main classes of AI-based model-agnostic strategies. We discuss the potential pitfalls of these methods, and strategies for their validation and interpretation. We aim for this document to serve as a useful reference both for practitioners and for researchers interested in learning more about these model-agnostic search strategies.

</details>

### [40] [Effects of the Symmetry energy slope on the exotic content of the neutron stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30554)
*Luiz L. Lopes*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 通过改变对称能斜率（$L$），研究了中子星内部奇异成分（超子与Δ共振态）的含量变化及其对宏观与微观量的影响。结果表明，$L$ 对超子丰度影响微弱，但对 Δ 共振态有强烈抑制作用；奇异成分在低 $L$ 值下更为显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索中子星内部奇异物质（如超子（hyperons）和Δ共振态（Δ resonances））的含量如何随对称能斜率（symmetry energy slope, $L$）变化，并评估这种变化对宏观与微观可观测量的影响。

Method: 采用两种不同的参数化方案（L3$ωρ$ 和 BigApple），并结合三种中子星核心组分假设（核子+超子、核子+Δ共振态、核子+超子+Δ共振态），通过改变对称能斜率 $L$ 进行系统性数值分析。

Result: 改变对称能斜率 $L$ 几乎不影响超子的丰度，但较大的 $L$ 值会显著抑制 Δ 共振态的产生；奇异成分在低 $L$ 值下比高 $L$ 值下更明显；两种参数化方案之间既存在差异也存在相似性。

Conclusion: 对称能斜率 $L$ 对中子星内部奇异组分的影响具有组分依赖性：对超子影响弱，对 Δ 共振态影响强；低 $L$ 值更有利于奇异物质出现。

Abstract: By varying the symmetry energy slope ($L$), I investigate how the exotic content within the interiors of neutron stars changes and how it affects both macroscopic and microscopic quantities. Using two different parametrizations (L3$ωρ$ and BigApple), and three different possibilities about the neutron star core (nucleons+hyperons, nucleons+deltas, nucleons+hyperons+deltas), I show that, for the models analyzed in this work, changing the slope barely changes the amount of hyperons, but it can strongly suppress the $Δ$ resonances for large values of $L$. I also show that, in general, the presence of exotic content will be more evident for lower values of $L$ than for large ones. Differences and similarities between the two parametrizations are also analyzed.

</details>

Szelc,N. Taniuchi,K. Terao,C. Thorpe,D. Torbunov,D. Totani,M. Toups,A. Trettin,Y. -T. Tsai,J. Tyler,M. A. Uchida,T. Usher,B. Viren,J. Wang,L. Wang,M. Weber,H. Wei,A. J. White,S. Wolbers,T.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用 $^{208}$Tl 衰变产生的 2.614 MeV γ 射线在 MicroBooNE 探测器中发生成对产生（pair production）过程产生的单能信号，对重构能量分辨率进行表征。

Result: 测得能量分辨率为 (7.52 ± 0.78 (统计) ± 0.92 (系统))%，该结果与 MicroBooNE 模拟预测值 (9.70 ± 0.65 (统计))% 在 1.6 σ 水平上一致。

Conclusion: 本研究是首次在 MeV 能标下对 LArTPC 能量分辨率进行测量，为未来使用 LArTPC 探测器的实验提供了利用单能信号进行能量校准（energy calibration）的方法路径。

Abstract: A detailed understanding of the capabilities and fidelity of low-energy reconstruction is crucial for taking advantage of MeV-scale neutrino physics opportunities in liquid argon time projection chambers (LArTPCs). This study presents a measurement of the resolution of reconstructed energy in the MicroBooNE LArTPC at $\approx 1.5$ MeV. The characterization is performed using monoenergetic signals generated by $2.614$ MeV $γ$-rays from $^{208}$Tl decays undergoing pair production in the detector. The resolution is found to be ($7.52 \pm 0.78 \text{(stat)} \pm 0.92 \text{(syst)}$)%. This value is consistent with the MicroBooNE simulation prediction of ($9.70 \pm 0.65 \text{(stat)}$)% at the $1.6 σ$ level. This study represents the first ever measurement of LArTPC energy resolution at the MeV scale and provides a pathway for monoenergetic energy calibrations in future experiments using LArTPC detectors.

### [42] [Novel Strip-like Readout Geometries in Resistive AC-coupled Silicon Detectors (RSD / AC-LGAD)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31235)
*L. Leander Grimm,Lorena Hahn,Brendan Regnery,Luca Menzio,Roberta Arcidiacono,Nicolo Cartiglia,Alexander Dierlamm,Markus Klute,Michael Moll*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文首次利用瞬态电流技术（TCT）表征了意大利FBK生产的第二批电阻型硅探测器（RSD/AC-LGAD）中具有新型读出焊盘形状的传感器。测量结果表明，这些介于条状与像素状之间的新型设计具有优异的一维空间分辨率，证实了条状RSD在未来跟踪系统中的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 下一代粒子对撞机（如EIC、FCC-ee、CEPC、FCC-hh）需要兼具优异时间与空间分辨率的探测器，以实现4D跟踪器。但在远离对撞点的区域，条状读出几何结构比像素状更受欢迎，因其可减少读出通道数量。现有RSD传感器多为像素状，缺乏针对条状混合读出形状的系统性表征。

Method: 使用瞬态电流技术（Transient Current Technique, TCT）对FBK第二批生产的RSD传感器中具有非常规读出焊盘形状（介于条状与像素状之间的混合设计）进行首次表征。

Result: 测量结果表明这些新型焊盘设计实现了出色的一维空间分辨率。

Conclusion: 新型条状RSD传感器在未来跟踪系统中具有巨大应用潜力。

Abstract: Resistive Silicon Detectors (RSD/AC-LGAD) are novel silicon detectors capable of both precise spatial and temporal resolution. Such sensors will be essential for the next generation of particle colliders (EIC, FCC-ee, CEPC, FCC-hh) and would enable the possibility of a 4D tracker. RSD sensors are typically fabricated with a pixel-like geometry that provides excellent spatial resolution in the x and y directions. However, in regions further from the interaction point, high spatial resolution in one direction (strip-like geometry) is often preferred to reduce the number of readout channels. For example, strip AC-LGADs are now the default option for the US electron ion collider (EIC). The second production of RSD sensors by Fondazione Bruno Kessler includes sensors with unconventional readout pad shapes that act as a mixture between strip-like and pixel-like readout. This work presents the first characterization of these new pad designs using the Transient Current Technique (TCT). The measurements demonstrate exceptional one-dimensional spatial resolution, confirming the potential of novel strip-like RSDs for future tracking systems.

### [43] [Deep-learning-based low-energy trigger algorithms for the Hyper-Kamiokande experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31391)
*Katharina Lachner,Saúl Alonso-Monsalve,Benjamin Richards,Davide Sgalaberna*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文详细研究了深度学习触发算法在大型水切伦科夫探测器（如Hyper-Kamiokande）低能中微子事件（<7 MeV）中的应用，比较了监督分类器和两种基于噪声的异常检测方法（自编码器和MPDR）。监督模型对3 MeV单电子的信号识别效率达76.7%，远超传统计数触发（26.4%），GPU推理延迟低于毫秒级，满足实时运行需求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代机器学习技术在粒子物理学中因强大的模式识别能力而日益重要，尤其是在实时数据采集中面临严格的运行时间约束。本文针对大型水切伦科夫探测器（如Hyper-Kamiokande）的低能中微子事件（低于7 MeV），探索基于深度学习（deep learning）的触发（trigger）算法以提升信号识别效率。

Method: 本文设计了定制化神经网络监督分类器（custom neural-network supervised classifiers），并采用两种仅基于探测器噪声训练的异常检测方法（anomaly-detection approaches）：纯自编码器（pure autoencoder）和基于流形投影—扩散恢复（Manifold Projection–Diffusion Recovery, MPDR）的能量模型（energy-based model）。所有方法均在大型水切伦科夫探测器框架下进行评估。

Result: 监督模型对3 MeV动能单电子的信号识别效率为76.7%，显著优于传统基于击中计数的触发（hit-count-based trigger）的26.4%；MPDR方法达到31.8%。GPU上的运行时评估显示，每窗口推理延迟（per-window inference latency）远低于毫秒量级，表明实时操作可行。

Conclusion: 基于深度学习的方法在低能中微子触发任务中大幅超越传统触发算法，监督模型表现最优，MPDR异常检测方法也优于基线。GPU推理延迟满足实时数据采集要求，为未来大型水切伦科夫实验（如Hyper-Kamiokande）的低能触发系统提供了可行技术方案。

Abstract: Modern machine learning techniques have become increasingly important in particle physics because of their powerful pattern-recognition capabilities, including in real-time data acquisition where stringent runtime constraints apply. This paper details the performance of deep-learning-based trigger algorithms for a large water Cherenkov detector such as Hyper-Kamiokande aimed at low-energy neutrino events (below 7 MeV). The performance of custom neural-network supervised classifiers is shown alongside two anomaly-detection approaches trained solely on detector noise: a pure autoencoder and an energy-based model based on Manifold Projection--Diffusion Recovery (MPDR). The supervised model shows signal identification efficiencies of 76.7% for single electrons of 3 MeV kinetic energy, significantly exceeding signal efficiencies obtained from a traditional hit-count-based trigger of 26.4%, as does the MPDR approach with 31.8%. Runtime evaluations on GPU yield per-window inference latencies well below the millisecond scale, indicating that real-time operation is feasible.

</details>

### [44] [Conservation-Based Feedback-Circuit Decomposition for Linear Forced Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30505)
*Ming Cai*

Main category: physics.ao-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于守恒的反馈电路分解方法，适用于一般线性受迫系统。该方法通过独立本征电路增益及其受迫变换向量，完整解析地表示受迫系统的瞬态与平衡解，且收敛性不受增益大小或不稳定模式存在的影响，为科学与工程中耦合线性系统的受迫响应分析提供了新的基础数学工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有线性系统分析主要依赖特征值和特征向量（eigenvalues and eigenvectors）方法处理初值问题，但对于一般线性受迫系统（forced systems），缺乏类似的通用解析框架。本文旨在填补这一空白，提供一种系统的分解方法以统一描述受迫系统的瞬态与平衡行为。

Method: 提出一种基于守恒的反馈电路分解（conservation-based feedback-circuit decomposition）方法。该方法定义了一组独立的“本征电路增益”（intrinsic circuit gains）及其对应的“受迫变换向量”（forcing-transformation vectors）。通过有限周期受迫变换核（finite-cycle forcing-transformation kernel）向平衡受迫变换核（equilibrium forcing-transformation kernel）的收敛过程，解析地表示瞬态与平衡解。

Result: 本征电路增益的符号决定了连续反馈循环（successive feedback cycles）呈单调收敛还是振荡收敛到变换后的受迫作用；受迫变换向量则决定了变换后受迫作用的结构。无论电路增益的幅度是否大于1，或系统中是否存在不稳定模式（unstable modes），收敛性均能得到保证。

Conclusion: 该反馈电路分解方法为理解和预测科学与工程中广泛耦合线性系统的受迫响应，提供了一种新的基础性数学工具，兼具通用性与解析性。

Abstract: We present a conservation-based feedback-circuit decomposition specifically for general linear forced systems. In a role parallel to that of eigenvalues and eigenvectors for initial-value problems, the complete set of independent intrinsic circuit gains and their associated forcing-transformation vectors provide a complete analytical representation of both transient and equilibrium forced solutions. The sign of intrinsic circuit gains determines whether successive feedback cycles exhibit monotonic or oscillatory convergence to transformed forcing, while the forcing-transformation vectors determine the structure of transformed forcing. The exact transient and equilibrium solutions are represented analytically through the convergence of the finite-cycle forcing-transformation kernel to the equilibrium forcing-transformation kernel, which is guaranteed regardless of whether the magnitudes of circuit gains exceed one or unstable modes exist in the system. The feedback-circuit decomposition provides a new generic foundational mathematical tool for understanding, predicting, and controlling forced responses in a broad range of coupled linear systems across science and engineering.

</details>


### [45] [A mathematical framework for dynamic emergent constraints in climate science](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30684)
*Francesco Ragone,Valerio Lucarini*

Main category: physics.ao-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于线性响应理论（linear response theory）为气候科学中的动态涌现约束（dynamic emergent constraints）建立了一个数学框架，揭示了传统动态涌现约束是更一般“积分动态涌现约束（integral dynamic emergent constraints）”的特例，并通过气候模型模拟验证了该框架的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 气候科学中的涌现约束（emergent constraints）通过建立可观测物理量之间的经验关系来降低气候变化预测的不确定性（climate change projection uncertainties），但其数学基础尚不牢固。作者希望为动态涌现约束提供严格的数学理论基础。

Method: 利用线性响应理论的最新成果，推导出积分动态涌现约束的一般关系式：预测量的响应可表示为预测子的响应与预测子-预测量对的代理格林函数（proxy Green's function）的卷积。该框架将传统动态涌现约束作为特例纳入，并明确了代理格林函数的因果性（causality）和观测时间尺度是约束成立的条件。以MPI-ESM气候模型的全球变暖模拟为应用案例，研究不同可观测量的动态涌现约束。

Result: 传统动态涌现约束被证明是更一般的积分动态涌现约束的特例；建立了动态涌现约束成立的数学条件（因果性与时间尺度）；在MPI-ESM气候模型模拟中成功应用该框架分析了不同可观测量的约束关系。

Conclusion: 该工作为动态涌现约束理论奠定了坚实的数学基础，并提出了在气候数据中识别此类约束存在必要条件的分析方案（protocol）。

Abstract: Emergent constraints in climate science are empirical relations that link the response to a forcing of a physical observable to the properties of other observables, with the aim of reducing climate change projection uncertainties. Here we use recent results in linear response theory to develop a mathematical framework for dynamic emergent constraints, a class of emergent constraints linking the response of different observables to the same forcing. We show how traditional dynamic emergent constraints are a special case of more general relations, that we call integral dynamic emergent constraints. These relations allow to compute the response of a predictand as the convolution of the response of a predictor and the proxy Green's function of the predictand-predictor pair. The conditions for the existence of integral emergent constraints are related to the causality of the proxy Green's function and the time scales at which the system is observed. We apply this framework to global warming simulations with the MPI-ESM climate model, to study dynamic emergent constraints between different observables. These results allow to put the theory of dynamic emergent constraints on firm mathematical ground, and suggest a protocol to identify necessary conditions for the existence of such relations in climate data.

</details>

### [46] [Time-reversed stochastic inflation in the quantum well](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31323)
*Chiara Animali,Baptiste Blachier,Nanoka Okada,Christophe Ringeval,Tomo Takahashi,Koki Tokeshi*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文通过时间反演随机暴胀（time-reversed stochastic inflation）方法，在平坦有界势（量子阱）中精确求解了随机暴胀过程，发现场的行为可分为与半无限平坦势不可区分和增强随机性两类，所得的曲率扰动分布在小涨落时退化为半无限结果，而大涨落则呈现指数衰减尾部，其衰减速率是标准前向随机暴胀的两倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准前向随机暴胀（forward stochastic inflation）从初始状态向暴胀终点演化，但观测者天然附着于暴胀结束的超曲面（end-of-inflation hypersurface），因此需要建立从终点回溯到初始状态的时间反演视角，以正确描述可观测宇宙的统计性质。

Method: 采用时间反演随机暴胀框架，在平坦有界势（quantum well）中精确求解随机演化方程，从暴胀终点逆向计数e-fold数回溯到初始状态，以此分析场的统计行为和曲率扰动分布。

Result: 在给定暴胀寿命下，场的行为要么与半无限平坦势结果不可区分，要么进入增强随机性（enhanced stochasticity）区域，完全抹去初始状态的记忆。曲率扰动的小涨落分布退化为半无限结果，而大涨落则呈现指数尾部，且正负值均出现，其衰减速率是标准前向方法的两倍。

Conclusion: 时间反演与标准前向随机暴胀在曲率扰动尾部行为上存在显著差异，这种差异可能对依赖尾部的敏感现象（如原初黑洞形成 primordial black hole formation）产生重要影响。

Abstract: Time-reversed stochastic inflation solves the stochastic evolution of the inflationary universe backward in time, by counting the number of e-folds from the end of quantum diffusion towards some initial state. The point of view of observers attached to the end-of-inflation hypersurface is thus enforced. In this work, we exactly solve time-reversed stochastic inflation in a flat and bounded potential, the so-called quantum well. At given lifetime, the field behaviour is found to be either indistinguishable from the one obtained in a semi-infinite flat potential, or, subject to enhanced stochasticity where any memory of the initial state is erased. The derived distribution of curvature perturbations reduces to the semi-infinite result for small fluctuations while it develops exponential tails for the large ones. Such tails arise for both positive and negative values, and decay twice as fast as the one obtained in the standard forward stochastic inflation. These differences may have important consequences for tail-sensitive phenomena, such as primordial black hole formation.

</details>


### [47] [Gravitational Waves from hybrid defects as probe of Flavor symmetry breaking: Machine-Learning Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31600)
*Anish Ghoshal,Ilia Gogoladze,Amit Tiwari*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出一种由规范U(1)_F味对称性及随后的离散Z_2对称性自发破缺产生的、由宇宙弦束缚畴壁网络所激发的随机引力波背景（SWGB）信号，并基于多层感知器（MLP）机器学习代理实现快速推断与信号特征识别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用全数值方法计算由宇宙弦束缚畴壁（string-bounded-wall）网络产生的引力波谱；在此基础上，利用基于多层感知器（multilayer perceptron, MLP）的机器学习代理（machine-learning surrogate）对谱进行快速推断，并用于探测器特定信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio, SNR）的高效计算。

Result: 该引力波谱在微赫兹至赫兹频率范围内的红外波段呈现与标准宇宙弦（standard cosmic-string）情况不同的独特频率斜率；对于高U(1)_F破缺能标，信号可被LISA、ET和SKA等未来引力波探测器探测到。

Conclusion: 该混合缺陷网络可产生可区分的引力波特征，且引力波探测与实验室中的味观测量（Flavor observables）之间存在一定的互补性。

Abstract: We present a novel possibility that a network of domain walls bounded by cosmic strings generates a stochastic gravitational wave background (SWGB) signal originating from the spontaneous breaking of a gauged $U(1)_F$ flavor symmetry and the subsequent breaking of discrete $Z_2$ symmetry that accommodates dark matter. The gravitational wave (GW) spectrum produced by the string-bounded-wall network can be detected for high $U(1)_F$ breaking scales in forthcoming GW detectors including LISA, ET and SKA. The GW signal exhibits a distinctive frequency slope, in the infrared, compared to the standard cosmic-string case, in the frequency range between micro-hertz and hertz. We develop a possible strategy to distinguish and characterize GW spectrum of the hybrid defect from from other defects, such as stable cosmic strings, via employing the exact calculation with a machine-learning surrogate, based on a multilayer perceptron (MLP), trained on spectra obtained from the full numerical treatment. This is then used for rapid inference in the detector-specific signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) computation which also makes the process fast and efficient. We also discuss some possible complementarity between GW searches and Flavor observables in the laboratory.

### [48] [New quantum information perspectives in the axion--photon and neutrino systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30419)
*Aaditya Datar,Arun M. Thalapillil,Palak Thareja*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文从量子信息论（quantum information theory）角度重新审视轴子-光子混合（axion–photon mixing），证明其双粒子纠缠特性，并系统分析纠缠熵、并发度（concurrence）、负性（negativity）、量子互信息、量子失谐（discord）及纠缠容量等量子信息度量，同时对比中微子振荡中的对应现象；进一步研究了Mandelstam–Tamm与Margolus–Levitin量子速度极限（quantum speed limits），以及纠缠量子速度极限，揭示了轴子-光子转换中的量子资源与极限时间尺度，从而将轴子现象学（axion phenomenology）、中微子振荡（neutrino oscillations）与量子信息理论联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子增强型轴子探测实验（quantum-enhanced axion searches）的兴起，使人们需要从量子信息理论的角度理解轴子-光子混合过程中的纠缠特性与量子资源，现有研究对这一方向尚未深入探讨。

Method: 采用两能级单激发子空间（two-level single-excitation sector）模型描述轴子-光子振荡，计算纠缠熵、并发度、负性、量子互信息、量子失谐及纠缠容量等量子信息度量，并分析Mandelstam–Tamm与Margolus–Levitin量子速度极限，以及针对纠缠的量子速度极限。

Result: 最大轴子-光子纠缠与共振或强混合转换（strong-mixing conversion）密切相关；正交化（orthogonalisation）仅在轴子-光子共振或中微子最大混合时发生；远离这些极限时，Margolus–Levitin界在最大转换处饱和，而Mandelstam–Tamm界普遍较弱；纠缠量子速度极限分为失谐主导（detuning-dominated）与磁场混合主导（magnetic-mixing-dominated）两个区域，且在一段周期内饱和后变弱。

Conclusion: 研究识别了轴子-光子转换中的量子资源与极限时间尺度，建立了轴子现象学、中微子振荡与量子信息理论之间的联系。

Abstract: In this work, we broach a quantum information-theoretic treatment of axion--photon mixing. Motivated by an emerging class of quantum-enhanced axion searches, we analyse the two-level single-excitation sector of axion--photon oscillations, demonstrating how the coupled dynamics naturally generate bipartite axion--photon mode entanglement. We study in detail the ensuing aspects of entanglement entropy, concurrence, negativity, quantum mutual information and discord, and capacity of entanglement, and the corresponding neutrino analogues wherever novel and previously unaddressed. In particular, we highlight the characteristic features that connect maximal axion--photon entanglement to resonant or strong-mixing conversion, and the distinct thresholds for the extremal values attained by the quantum information measures. We study aspects of the Mandelstam--Tamm and Margolus--Levitin quantum speed limits for both the axion--photon and neutrino systems. While orthogonalisation occurs only at axion--photon resonance, or at maximal neutrino mixing, where the two bounds coincide, away from these limits, the Margolus--Levitin bound is saturated at maximal conversion, while the Mandelstam--Tamm bound is generally weaker. We also study an entanglement quantum speed limit for axion--photon conversion, that separates into detuning-dominated and magnetic-mixing-dominated regimes, and find that it is saturated for a period and then the bound becomes weak. The results in this work identify the quantum resources and limiting timescales intrinsic to axion--photon conversion, and connect axion phenomenology, neutrino oscillations and quantum information theory.

</details>


### [49] [Searching for Lepton Flavor Violating decays of the Higgs Boson into $μτ$, $eτ$, and $eμ$ final states at FCC-ee](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30971)
*P. Sriling,N. Srimanobhas,P. Uttayarat,R. Uttho,V. Wachirapusitanand*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文评估了未来正负电子对撞机FCC-ee在240 GeV质心能量、积分亮度5 ab⁻¹下，探测125 GeV希格斯玻色子以及一个110–200 GeV范围内的新CP偶希格斯玻色子的轻子味 violating (LFV) 衰变（h→μτ, h→eτ, h→eμ）的灵敏度，并与低能ℓ→ℓ'γ搜索的约束力进行了比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轻子味 violating (LFV) 过程在标准模型（Standard Model）中微乎其微，因此任何观测信号都将是超越标准模型（beyond the Standard Model, BSM）新物理的强有力证据。FCC-ee作为下一代正负电子对撞机，具有极高的亮度和清洁的末态，为高精度探测希格斯玻色子的LFV衰变提供了独特机遇。

Method: 研究基于蒙特卡洛模拟，考虑e⁺e⁻→ℓℓh过程，重点分析希格斯轫致辐射（Higgs-strahlung）和矢量玻色子融合（vector boson fusion）两种产生通道，并利用多轻子末态进行信号-本底区分，设定95%置信度（CL）上限。

Result: 在95%置信水平下，对125 GeV希格斯玻色子各LFV衰变道的分支比上限分别为：h→μτ为5.92×10⁻⁴，h→eτ为6.27×10⁻⁴，h→eμ为7.48×10⁻⁵。对于e–τ和μ–τ通道，FCC-ee灵敏度优于低能ℓ→ℓ'γ搜索；而对于e–μ通道，低能搜索提供了更强的约束。

Conclusion: FCC-ee在探测希格斯玻色子的e–τ和μ–τ LFV衰变方面具有超越当前低能实验的灵敏度潜力，但在e–μ通道中低能搜索仍占优势。该研究为未来对撞机在味物理（flavor physics）领域的探索提供了重要的灵敏度参考。

Abstract: We investigate the projected sensitivity of the FCC-ee in probing the LFV decay of the 125 GeV Higgs boson, $h\toμτ$, $h\to eτ$, and $h \to eμ$ at center-of-mass energy of 240 GeV with an integrated luminosity of 5 ab$^{-1}$. With the clean multi-lepton final states, we consider the Higgs production modes that contribute to $e^+e^- \to \ell\ell h$, in particular, the Higgs-strahlung and the vector boson fusion production channels. The 95\% CL upper limits on branching ratio are found to be $5.92 \times 10^{-4}$, $6.27 \times 10^{-4}$, and $7.48 \times 10^{-5}$ for the channels $h\toμτ$, $h\to eτ$, and $h \to eμ$, respectively. In addition, we also consider the LFV decay of a new CP-even Higgs boson with mass in the range of $110-200$ GeV. The projected FCC-ee sensitivities are then compared to those from low energy searches for $\ell\to\ell'γ$ decay. We find that the FCC-ee sensitivity for the LFV decays of the Higgs in the $e-τ$ and $μ-τ$ channels is superior to the low-energy constraints. However, in the $e-μ$ case, the low energy search offers stronger constraints.

### [50] [Revisiting Unidentified Charged-Hadron Fragmentation Functions with Modern COMPASS SIDIS Multiplicities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31325)
*HAPS Collaboration,Maryam Soleymaninia,Hamzeh Khanpour,Hubert Spiesberger,Majid Azizi,Michael Klasen,Hadi Hashamipour*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了HAPS-hFF1.0，这是一项使用单举电子-正电子湮灭（SIA）数据和COMPASS半举深度非弹性散射（SIDIS）多重数数据进行的非标识带电强子碎裂函数（FFs）全局QCD分析。提取在次领头阶（NLO）和次次领头阶（NNLO）下完成，结果表明现代COMPASS SIDIS数据能够与SIA数据一致描述，并为轻夸克和反夸克的碎裂函数提供了电荷分离约束。NLO与NNLO对比显示夸克部分稳定，而胶子碎裂函数的约束仍较弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非标识带电强子碎裂函数（fragmentation functions, FFs）是描述部分子碎裂为带电强子的关键非微扰对象，现有全局FF提取对SIDIS数据的利用不足，特别是缺乏现代COMPASS实验提供的电荷分离约束，导致轻夸克与反夸克FF的味结构（flavor structure）不够精确。

Method: 采用全局QCD拟合方法，同时使用单举电子-正电子湮灭（single-inclusive electron-positron annihilation, SIA）数据和COMPASS实验2025年质子靶测量数据及2026年附录修订的等标量靶（isoscalar-target）SIDIS多重数数据，在NLO和NNLO两个微扰阶次下提取非标识带电强子FF。

Result: 现代COMPASS SIDIS多重数能够与SIA数据实现一致描述，并为轻夸克和反夸克FF提供了重要的电荷分离约束；NLO与NNLO提取结果对比表明夸克部分子（quark sector）的确定较为稳定，而胶子FF（gluon FF）在当前SIA+SIDIS分析中受到的直接约束仍较弱。

Conclusion: 研究突显了现代COMPASS SIDIS多重数数据对非标识带电强子碎裂精确研究以及未来全局FF确定的重要性。HAPS-hFF1.0副本已以标准LHAPDF格式公开发布。

Abstract: We present \texttt{HAPS-hFF1.0}, a new global QCD analysis of unidentified charged-hadron fragmentation functions (FFs) using single-inclusive electron-positron annihilation (SIA) data together with the modern COMPASS semi-inclusive deep-inelastic scattering (SIDIS) multiplicities. The COMPASS input consists of the 2025 proton-target measurement and the revised isoscalar-target multiplicities provided in the COMPASS addendum 2026. The extraction is performed at both next-to-leading order (NLO) and next-to-next-to-leading order (NNLO), allowing us to study the perturbative stability of the QCD fit and the impact of the updated SIDIS information on the flavor structure of the FFs. We find that the modern COMPASS multiplicities can be consistently described together with the SIA data and provide important charge-separated constraints on the light-quark and antiquark FFs. The comparison between the NLO and NNLO extractions indicates a stable quark-sector determination, while the gluon FF remains less directly constrained in the present SIA+SIDIS analysis. Our results highlight the importance of the modern COMPASS SIDIS multiplicities for precision studies of unidentified charged-hadron fragmentation and for future global FF determinations. The resulting \texttt{HAPS-hFF1.0} replicas are publicly available in standard LHAPDF format.

### [51] [CJ26 Global QCD Analysis with Large-$x$ Jefferson Lab 6 and 12 GeV Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31424)
*Alberto Accardi,Matteo Cerutti,Cynthia E. Keppel,Shujie Li,J. F. Owens,Sanghwa Park,Peter Risse*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: CJ26 是 CTEQ-JLab 全球 QCD 分析的最新版本，首次纳入了 JLab 6 GeV 和 12 GeV 的全部散射测量数据，显著提升了在大 $x$ 区域对 $n/p$ 结构函数比和 $d/u$ 价夸克比的确定精度，并提供了相应的 NLO 部分子分布函数（PDF）和结构函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过去的大 $x$ 区域量子色动力学（QCD）分析受限于数据覆盖不足，难以有效区分高扭效应（higher-twist effects）与离壳核子修正（off-shell nucleon corrections）。作者希望利用 JLab 12 GeV 数据提供的更高 $Q^2$ 杠杆来分离这些效应，从而更精确地确定核子结构函数比和价夸克比。

Method: 研究采用 CTEQ-JLab 全球 QCD 分析框架（CJ26），首次完整纳入了 JLab 6 GeV 深度非弹性散射（DIS）测量数据和已发表的 JLab 12 GeV 测量数据。通过利用 12 GeV 数据在更高 $Q^2$ 范围内的杠杆作用，将高扭效应与离壳核子修正进行区分，并在分析中考虑了实验关联系统不确定性的关键作用。

Result: $n/p$ 结构函数比的不确定性降低了 30-50%，$d/u$ 价夸克比的不确定性降低了 5-10%。分析显示了实验关联系统不确定性在实现该精度中的关键作用，并生成了 NLO 精度的 PDF 和结构函数结果，以 LHAPDF 格式提供。

Conclusion: CJ26 分析通过整合 JLab 6 GeV 和 12 GeV 的完整 DIS 测量数据，在大 $x$ 区域实现了对核子结构函数比和价夸克比的高精度确定。作者将结果以 LHAPDF 格式公开，供更广泛的物理社区使用。

Abstract: We present CJ26, the new CTEQ-JLab global QCD analysis that incorporates for the first time the complete suite of JLab 6 GeV DIS measurements and the first published JLab 12 GeV measurements. Focused on the large-$x$ region, the analysis utilizes the increased $Q^2$ leverage of the 12 GeV data to uniquely disentangle higher-twist effects from off-shell nucleon corrections. This leads to a highly accurate determination of the $n/p$ structure function ratio and the $d/u$ valence quark ratio, with uncertainties reduced by 30-50% and 5-10%, respectively. We highlight the critical role of experimental correlated systematic uncertainties in achieving this precision and provide the resulting NLO PDFs and structure functions in LHAPDF format for general use.

</details>


### [52] [Quark-Lepton Color-Flavor Unification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30413)
*Antonio Delgado,Seth Koren*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一个 SU(12) × SU(2)_L × U(1)_R 大统一模型，通过夸克色-味与轻子味的统一，利用规范瞬子动态生成底夸克与τ轻子汤川耦合，同时解决强CP问题并实现跷跷板机制。模型仅需两个新标量不可约表示，并引入离散规范对称性实现质子绝对稳定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统大统一理论通常需要引入大量新费米子并面临强CP问题与质子衰变困难。本文旨在构建一个 flavor-full 的大统一替代方案，通过夸克色-味与轻子味的统一，在最小化新费米子引入的前提下，同时解决强CP问题、汤川耦合层级问题及质子稳定性问题。

Method: 模型从紫外（ultraviolet）的一个共享汤川耦合（yukawa）出发，该耦合统一描述上型夸克与中微子。利用规范化的夸克色-味与轻子味瞬子（gauged instanton）动态生成底夸克和τ轻子的汤川耦合。对称性破缺仅需两个新标量不可约表示（scalar irreps），路径包括夸克色-味解构（deconstruction）与红外重统一（infrared reunification）。模型还利用非可逆手征对称性破缺（non-invertible chiral symmetry-breaking）来构建丰富的广义对称性（generalized symmetries）与拓扑缺陷（topological defects）。

Result: 标准模型规范群在此理论中表示为 G_SM = [SU(3)_C × SU(2)_L × U(1)_Y × Z^X_18] / (Z_3 × Γ × Z_3)，其中 Γ 属于 {1, Z_2} 是电弱全局结构。新引入的离散规范对称性 X = B - 3(L_i + L_j - L_k) 是 SM 中 Z^{B+L}_18 全纯对称性的 flavor-full 升级，能实现质子绝对稳定（absolute proton stability）。在红外（infrared），连续群与离散群之间的共享商结构（shared quotient）将 SM 的一形式与二形式全局对称性（one-form and two-form global symmetries）联系起来。

Conclusion: 该模型以 flavor-full 的方式实现了大统一，利用规范瞬子动态生成汤川层级，解决了强CP问题，并通过离散规范对称性保障质子绝对稳定。非可逆手征对称性破缺与广义对称性的涌现为理解 SM 的拓扑结构提供了新视角。

Abstract: We present an $SU(12) \times SU(2)_L \times U(1)_R$ model unifying $SU(9)$ quark color-flavor with $SU(3)$ lepton flavor as a flavorful alternative to conventional theories of unification. We begin in the ultraviolet with a single yukawa shared by the unified up-type quarks and neutrinos, and no further new fermions. We show that gauged quark color-flavor and lepton flavor instantons dynamically generate the bottom and tau yukawas, which implements a massless quark solution to the strong CP problem and sets up a flavored type-I seesaw mechanism. Only two new scalar irreps are needed for the symmetry-breaking steps, which include quark color-flavor deconstruction and then infrared reunification, and the Standard Model gauge group in this theory emerges as \[G_{\rm SM} = \frac{SU(3)_C \times SU(2)_L \times U(1)_Y \times \mathbb{Z}^X_{18}}{\mathbb{Z}_{3} \times Γ\times \mathbb{Z}_3},\] where $Γ\in \lbrace 1, \mathbb{Z}_2 \rbrace$ is the electroweak global structure and there is a discrete gauge symmetry $X = B - 3(L_i + L_j - L_k)$ which brings additional $\mathbb{Z}_3$ global structure to the SM. This gauge symmetry acts as a flavorful upgrade of the $\mathbb{Z}^{B+L}_{18}$ anomaly-free global symmetry of the SM and stabilizes the proton absolutely. Non-invertible chiral symmetry-breaking is crucial to our model, and we discuss the rich spectrum of emergent generalized symmetries and topological defects appearing at various stages. In the infrared, the novel shared quotient between continuous and discrete groups links the one-form and two-form global symmetries of the Standard Model.

### [53] [Factorizing quarkonium production matrix elements using effective field theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30441)
*Marston Copeland,Ivan Vitev*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用有效场论（effective field theory）和Hubbard-Stratonovich变换，在NRQCD框架内将夸克偶素（quarkonium）产生矩阵元因子化为色单态（color-singlet）复合场矩阵元与态无关的真空胶子关联函数，从而验证并扩展了不同S波矢量夸克偶素态之间的长距离矩阵元（LDME）关联，并恢复了横向动量依赖（TMD）因子化框架中产生算符的普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: NRQCD（非相对论量子色动力学）中夸克偶素产生截面的计算涉及复杂的产生矩阵元，传统方法难以将其与普适的、态无关的物理量（如波函数与真空胶子关联函数）直接联系起来，从而限制了理论的可预测性。本文旨在通过有效场论技术实现该因子化，以揭示不同态之间长距离矩阵元（long-distance matrix elements, LDMEs）的内在联系，并提升横向动量依赖（transverse momentum dependent, TMD）因子化框架下NRQCD的预言能力。

Method: 采用有效场论（effective field theory）方法，对NRQCD中的产生矩阵元进行因子化处理。具体而言，通过应用Hubbard-Stratonovich变换，在速度幂次计数（velocity power counting）的首阶（leading order），证明混合vNRQCD/pNRQCD（速度NRQCD/势NRQCD）拉格朗日量中软（soft）与超软（ultrasoft）部分可以从重夸克与反夸克场中解耦。该解耦过程使得产生矩阵元被分离为色单态（color-singlet）复合场矩阵元（可写为原点波函数）与态无关的色电（chromo-electric）及色磁（chromo-magnetic）胶子场真空关联函数。

Result: 验证了最初基于pNRQCD推导的不同S波矢量夸克偶素态之间长距离矩阵元（LDMEs）的强有力关联。发现了色八重态（color-octet）P波机制的新的算符贡献，该贡献满足类似的关系集合。此外，该方法成功将TMD因子化框架中出现的产生矩阵元——即TMD软过渡函数（soft transition functions）——因子化为态无关的胶子关联函数。这恢复了TMD产生算符的部分普适性，并显著提升了NRQCD在TMD框架中的预测能力。

Conclusion: 本文工作表明，通过有效场论与Hubbard-Stratonovich变换，夸克偶素产生矩阵元可以系统地因子化为普适的、态无关的胶子关联函数与波函数。这一结果不仅深化了对不同夸克偶素态之间LDMEs关联的理解，更重要的是为TMD因子化框架下NRQCD的应用提供了更强的可预测性和普适性。

Abstract: We use effective field theory to factorize production matrix elements that appear in quarkonium cross sections in NRQCD. By applying a Hubbard-Stratonovich transformation we show that the soft and ultrasoft sectors of NRQCD can be decoupled from the heavy quark and antiquark fields in a hybrid vNRQCD/pNRQCD Lagrangian at leading order in the velocity power counting. This enables us to separate quarkonium production matrix elements in terms of matrix elements of color-singlet composite fields, which we can write as the wavefunction at the origin, and state independent vacuum correlators of chromo-electric and chromo-magnetic gluon fields. This approach verifies powerful connections between the LDMEs of different S-wave vector quarkonium states, originally derived using pNRQCD. Additionally, we find new operator contributions for the color-octet P-wave mechanism, which satisfy a similar set of relationships. Finally, this approach allows us to factorize the production matrix elements that appear in the transverse momentum dependent factorization framework, known as TMD soft transition functions, in terms of state independent gluon correlators. This work restores some universality for TMD production operators and dramatically improves the predictive power of NRQCD in the TMD framework.

### [54] [CoLoRFulNNLO for color-singlet processes: An update on NNLOCAL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31221)
*S. Van Thurenhout,V. Del Duca,C. Duhr,L. Fekésházy,F. Guadagni,P. Mukherjee,G. Somogyi,F. Tramontano*

TL;DR: 本文报告了NNLOCAL蒙特卡罗程序的更新进展，该程序实现了CoLoRFulNNLO完全局域减除方案在强子对撞中色单态产生过程的扩展，并通过LHC全微分截面计算进行了验证。

Method: 基于量子色动力学QCD的标准红外IR因子化公式构建对项counterterms，并对未分辨发射unresolved emissions的相空间进行全解析积分。方法具有通用性generic，数值稳定性控制良好。

Result: 通过计算大型强子对撞机LHC的NNLO修正全微分截面fully differential cross sections，验证了方法的有效性。

Abstract: We give an update on the status of NNLOCAL, a parton-level Monte Carlo program implementing the extension of the completely local subtraction scheme CoLoRFulNNLO to color-singlet production in hadron-hadron collisions. The construction of the counterterms in our scheme is generic, being based on the standard IR factorization formulae of QCD. Furthermore, the integration of the counterterms over the phase space of unresolved emissions is performed fully analytically, allowing for good control of the numerical stability of our predictions. We validate our method by computing NNLO corrections to fully differential cross sections for the LHC.

### [55] [Thermodynamics of the Isospectral family of holographic vector mesons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31280)
*Miguel Angel Martin Contreras,Saulo Diles,Alfredo Vega*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 基于软墙AdS/QCD模型的等谱族（isospectral family），研究了 ρ 介子的热行为。发现基态电磁衰变常数 f₁ 是控制 ρ(770) 介子熔化温度 T_m 的关键标度，且 T_m 随 f₁ 单调递增。通过等谱参数将 f₁ 固定在实验值（226 MeV），得到熔化温度 T_m = 157 MeV 以及从禁闭到退禁闭的光滑过渡（smooth crossover）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在 AdS/QCD 全息对偶（holographic duality）框架下，热密介质中的矢量介子行为（如 ρ 介子的熔化和色禁闭–退禁闭相变）对理解夸克胶子等离子体（QGP）和夸克偶素解离（quarkonium dissociation）至关重要。现有模型中基态衰变常数对熔化温度的调控作用尚不清晰，本文旨在利用等谱族方法系统性地分离这一影响。

Method: 采用软墙AdS/QCD（softwall AdS/QCD）模型的等谱族方法，在有限温度（finite temperature）和有限化学势（finite chemical potential）条件下，计算不同族成员的谱函数（spectral functions）。通过等谱变换（isospectral transformation）独立调整基态电磁衰变常数 f₁，而不改变质量谱（mass spectrum），从而隔离 f₁ 对熔化温度 T_m 的影响。

Result: 基态 ρ(770) 的熔化温度 T_m 随 f₁ 单调增加；激发态呈现相同趋势，但随径向量子数（radial quantum number）增加而显著抑制。将 f₁ 固定在实验值 226 MeV 时，模型给出 T_m = 157 MeV，并呈现从禁闭到退禁闭的光滑过渡（smooth crossover）。热质量（thermal mass）在临界点附近轻微下降，宽度（width）单调增长。

Conclusion: 等谱变换提供了一种受控方式，可在不改变质量谱的前提下调整基态衰变常数，从而精确研究介质效应对矢量介子的影响。f₁ 被确认为控制夸克偶素解离的关键标度。

Abstract: We study the thermal behavior of the $ρ$ meson using the isospectral family of the softwall AdS/QCD model. By computing spectral functions at finite temperature and chemical potential for different members of this family, we isolate the effect of the ground-state electromagnetic decay constant $f_1$ on the melting temperature $T_m$ of the $ρ(770)$ meson. A clear monotonic increase of $T_m$ with $f_1$ is found, supporting the interpretation of $f_1$ as a key scale controlling quarkonium dissociation. For excited states, the same qualitative trend appears but is strongly suppressed as the radial quantum number increases. Using the isospectral parameter to fix $f_1$ to its experimental value ($226$ MeV) yields a holographic model whose spectral function gives a melting temperature $T_m = 157$ MeV and a smooth crossover from confinement to deconfinement. The thermal mass shows a mild decrease near the critical point, while the width grows monotonically. Our results demonstrate that the isospectral transformation provides a controlled way to adjust ground-state decay constants without altering the mass spectrum, enabling precise studies of medium effects on vector mesons.

</details>

### [56] [Mean-squared displacements of rough particles in polydisperse granular gases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30474)

Method: 通过理论分析或数值模拟，在均匀冷却态下考察多分散颗粒气体的扩散系数和均方位移，并系统研究它们与法向和切向恢复系数的依赖关系。

Result: 颗粒的迁移率（motility）受到其机械性质和表面特性的强烈影响。

We study their dependence on the normal and tangential restitution coefficients. We show that the motility of particles is strongly affected by their mechanical properties and surface characteristics.

### [57] [Wetting as an emergent property of water: reformulating Young equation on molecular grounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30661)
*Nicolas Loubet,Gustavo Appignanesi*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过提出分子润湿系数（molecular wetting coefficient, ωₘ），将杨氏方程（Young equation）在分子层面重新表述，揭示了水润湿现象的分子起源，并建立了润湿、粘附、空化与纳米限域填充之间的统一能量学框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 杨氏方程虽能很好地宏观描述润湿现象，但其分子起源（尤其是水的润湿）两百多年来一直未能明确，因此需要建立分子层面的理论解释。

Method: 将水润湿问题重新表述为分子润湿系数 ωₘ，该系数量化了界面如何补偿水分子中氢键缺陷（hydrogen-bond defects）相对于体相水的固有能量成本。在连续且广泛的亲水性（hydrophilicity）谱上，对化学多样性的实验与模型表面进行测试。

Result: 当用 ωₘ 表达时，宏观接触角（contact angles）在跨越多类表面后坍缩为一条单一的通用主曲线（universal master curve）。该分子重述在能量学基础上闭合了杨氏方程与杨-杜普雷方程（Young-Dupre relation）。

Conclusion: 润湿是水作为溶剂的内在涌现性质（emergent property），而非表面特有属性。该工作提供了一个可迁移的分子框架，可校准能量学直觉并指导水性界面的理性设计，同时建立了润湿、粘附、空化与纳米限域填充间的统一物理联系。

Abstract: Young equation provides a remarkably successful macroscopic description of wetting, yet its molecular origin (particularly for water) has remained elusive for over two centuries. Here we make the molecular basis of aqueous wetting explicit by reformulating it in terms of a molecular wetting coefficient, omega m, which quantifies how an interface compensates the intrinsic energetic cost of hydrogen-bond defects relative to bulk water. Across a broad and continuous spectrum of hydrophilicities, spanning chemically diverse experimental and model surfaces, macroscopic contact angles collapse onto a single universal master curve when expressed through omega m. This molecular reformulation closes Young and Young-Dupre relations on energetic grounds, establishing a unified and predictive physical link between wetting, adhesion, cavitation, and nanoconfined filling. By anchoring interfacial behavior to waters intrinsic hydrogen-bond energetic scales, our results reveal wetting as an emergent property of water itself, rather than a surface-specific attribute and provide a transferable molecular framework that recalibrates energetic intuition and guides the rational design of aqueous interfaces. (This document is the unedited Author version of a Submitted Manuscript subsequently accepted for publication in J. Am. Chem. Soc. For the published version, which includes a more complete molecular-thermodynamics grounding of the method see the published version)

</details>


### [58] [Living Helices in Fluctuating Polymer Chains: Cooperative Nucleation, Dynamics, and Lifetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30868)
*Biman Bagchi*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一个粗粒度统计力学理论，通过三态合作模型和平均首通时间（mean first-passage time）框架，解释了聚合物链中瞬态、有限且动态演化的“活螺旋”（living helices）的成核机制、稳定性与寿命，并预测其形成时间在纳秒至亚微秒量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 聚合物链中的螺旋片段通常是瞬态、有限且动态演化的，但其起源与稳定性尚未被完全理解。本文旨在填补这一理论空白，解释此类“活螺旋”如何在涨落聚合物系统中涌现。

Method: 提出一个最小粗粒化（coarse-grained）统计力学理论，采用具有合作相互作用（cooperative interactions）的三态模型，将成核过程描述为多步机制：先形成受约束的前核（pre-nucleus），再通过合作稳定促进有限螺旋片段增长。动力学方面，将螺旋尺寸演化建模为随机过程（stochastic process），利用平均首通时间（mean first-passage）框架推导形成时间和寿命的解析表达式。

Result: 自由能景观（free-energy landscape）自然倾向于形成边缘稳定的螺旋，其尺寸由合作增益与刚度（stiffness）、扭转应变（torsional strain）及溶剂涨落（solvent fluctuations）带来的非线性惩罚之间的竞争决定。对于柔性聚合物和多肽片段等代表性参数，理论预测特征时间尺度在纳秒到亚微秒范围。

Conclusion: 分析支持将活螺旋视为有限、可移动的激发态（mobile excitations），其稳定性受合作性、边界运动（boundary motion）以及溶剂诱导涨落（solvent-induced fluctuations）共同控制。

Abstract: Helical segments in polymer chains are often transient, finite, and dynamically evolving, yet their origin and stability remain incompletely understood. Here we develop a minimal coarse-grained statistical-mechanical theory that explains how such living helices emerge in fluctuating polymer systems. Using a three-state model with cooperative interactions, we show that helix formation proceeds through a multistep nucleation mechanism. An initial constrained pre-nucleus forms first, followed by cooperative stabilization that promotes the growth of finite helical segments. The resulting free-energy landscape naturally favors marginally stable helices whose size is determined by a competition between cooperative gains and nonlinear penalties arising from stiffness, torsional strain, and solvent fluctuations. By formulating the dynamics as a stochastic process in segment size, we derive analytical expressions for both formation times and lifetimes within a mean first-passage framework. For representative parameters relevant to flexible polymers and peptide segments, the theory predicts characteristic timescales in the nanosecond to sub-microsecond range. The present analysis supports a view of living helices as finite, mobile excitations whose stability is controlled by cooperativity, boundary motion, and solvent-induced fluctuations.

</details>


### [59] [Limits of the Non-Linear Generalized Langevin Equation: Cross-Correlations, Irreversibility and Desynchronization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31297)
*Bernd Jung,Gerhard Jung*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过简化模型系统研究了广义朗之万方程（GLE）中非线性力与记忆效应结合所导致的分析不一致性及其数值后果，指出非线性力会破坏涨落-耗散定理并使噪声变得位置依赖且不可逆，在弱非线性下可通过迭代优化或微观一致噪声部分缓解，但强非线性下迭代重构失败且出现去同步化，从而为非线性GLE在软物质粗粒化建模中的适用性提供了实用指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义朗之万方程（generalized Langevin equation, GLE）广泛应用于生物分子动力学等复杂软物质系统的粗粒化建模，但近期理论研究表明，非线性力与记忆效应的结合会引入基本的分析不一致性。本文旨在通过数值实验探究这些理论问题的实际后果，并明确非线性GLE在什么情况下可以准确应用。

Method: 采用一个简化模型系统，对非线性力与记忆效应结合下的广义朗之万方程进行数值模拟，分析非线性力引起的噪声-力交叉关联，并比较迭代记忆优化与微观一致噪声两种改进策略在不同非线性强度下的表现。

Result: 非线性力会与噪声产生交叉关联，修改涨落-耗散定理（fluctuation-dissipation theorem），使噪声变得位置依赖且不可逆，导致常用的可逆高斯噪声无法捕捉微观涨落的关键特征。弱非线性下，迭代记忆优化或使用微观一致噪声可部分解决问题，后者还能意外地使GLE轨迹与底层微观动力学同步；但在强非线性（如高势垒或势能肩部）条件下，迭代重构失效并出现去同步化。

Conclusion: 非线性GLE在弱非线性条件下可通过适当方法实现准确应用，但在强非线性情形下无法正确再现微观动力学。该研究为非线性GLE在软物质粗粒化（coarse-grain）建模中的实际应用提供了明确的适用性判据和指导。

Abstract: The generalized Langevin equation (GLE) is widely used to model complex soft-matter systems, including biomolecular dynamics, by incorporating memory effects and colored noise into coarse-grained descriptions. However, recent results suggest that combining memory with non-linear forces, ubiquitous in soft matter, introduces fundamental analytical inconsistencies. Here, using a simplified model, we investigate the practical numerical consequences of these analytical results. We show that non-linear forces generate cross-correlations with the noise, modifying the fluctuation-dissipation theorem and rendering the noise position-dependent and irreversible. This implies that the commonly assumed reversible Gaussian noise in GLE simulations fails to capture essential features of the microscopic fluctuations. For weak non-linearities, these issues can be partially resolved either by using an iterative optimization of memory or by using microscopically consistent noise, which unexpectedly synchronizes GLE trajectories with the underlying microscopic dynamics. For stronger non-linearities like high barriers or shoulders in the external potential, however, iterative reconstruction fails and we observe desynchronization, indicating that the non-linear GLE no longer correctly reproduces the microscopic dynamics. Our results show in which situations non-linear GLEs can be accurately applied and when they fail, thus providing practical guidance for their application to coarse-grain soft-matter systems.

</details>


### [60] [Spontaneous flows and interfacial instabilities in oxygen-sensitive living active matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31355)
*Azam Gholami,Sangram Gore,Sai V. R. Ambadipudi,Iraj Gholami,Albert J. Bae*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过实验与模型结合，展示了自生氧梯度如何通过趋氧性（oxytaxis）和极性主动流体（polar active fluid）机制，引发并失稳微游泳体（如眼虫 Euglena gracilis）的致密悬浮液，形成环形集体旋转与冠状突起结构；揭示了化学梯度对主动流体（active fluid）界面与流动的环境调控路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在生命系统中，主动流体的行为常受到生物消耗或产生的环境场调控；本研究旨在揭示自生化学梯度（如氧梯度）如何组织并失稳主动流体，从而为环境调控主动物质（active matter）的流动与界面提供机制性理解。

Method: 实验采用外周开口的圆形腔室，通过氧气交换与细胞消耗构建径向氧梯度；观察眼虫 Euglena gracilis 悬浮液的自组织过程。同时构建氧耦合的极性主动流体模型，模拟氧调控细胞运动方向与速度，以及偶极主动应力（dipolar active stress）驱动界面失稳的动力学。

Result: 初始均匀的悬浮液通过氧依赖的趋氧性自发形成致密细胞环，随后环产生集体旋转并失稳为长寿命的冠状突起结构；模型重现了这一序列，表明氧趋氧性形成环状主动界面，而冠状突起源于活动驱动的界面不稳定性（activity-driven interfacial instability）。

Conclusion: 结果揭示自生化学梯度可定位并激活主动流体，为通过环境场调控主动物质流动与界面行为提供了新途径。

Abstract: Active fluids generate motion and stress internally, but in living systems this
  activity is often regulated by environmental fields that the organisms consume
  or produce. Here we show that oxygen gradients organise and destabilise dense
  suspensions of the flagellated microswimmer \textit{Euglena gracilis}. In
  circular chambers open to air at the periphery, oxygen exchange and cellular
  consumption generate a radial chemical gradient. An initially homogeneous
  suspension spontaneously forms a dense cellular ring through oxygen-dependent
  motility and bidirectional oxytaxis. The ring then develops collective
  rotation and destabilises into a long-lived corona of protrusions. We reproduce
  this sequence with an oxygen-coupled polar active-fluid model in which oxygen
  controls both the direction and speed of cell motion, while dipolar active
  stresses drive the instability of the dense interface. The simulations show
  that oxygen taxis creates the annular active interface, but the subsequent
  corona is an activity-driven interfacial instability. Our results reveal how a
  self-generated chemical gradient can position and activate a living fluid,
  providing a route to environmental control of active-matter flows and
  interfaces.

### [61] [Nonequilibrium scaling of drag forces in counterdriven fluid mixtures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31479)
*Jonas Köglmayr,Florian Sammüller,Matthias Schmidt*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本论文通过功能标量论（power functional scaling）和自适应布朗动力学模拟，研究了反向驱动二元流体混合物稳态中由微观相互作用产生的非平衡有效阻力场，建立了从近平衡线性响应到远非平衡平方根渐近行为的交叉规律，并通过局部功能泛函近似验证了空间非平衡结构形成的再现性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的动力学密度泛函理论（dynamical density functional theory）无法描述非平衡阻力场从近平衡到远非平衡区的完整交叉行为，因此需要建立一种超越该理论的普适标度（scaling）框架。

Method: 采用功能标量论（power functional scaling）的论证方法，结合自适应布朗动力学（adaptive Brownian dynamics）计算机模拟；提出一个代数表达式同时涵盖近平衡线性响应（linear response）与远非平衡平方根渐近（square root asymptotics）两种极限情况，并适用于交叉区（crossover regime）。

Result: 基于标度律（scaling law）的局部功能泛函近似（local power functional approximation）能够再现非均匀驱动系统中的空间非平衡结构形成；模拟结果作为基准验证了该近似的准确性。

Conclusion: 该交叉行为超越了动力学密度泛函理论，揭示了驱动流体中普遍存在的非平衡标度规律，为理解反向驱动二元混合物中的非平衡阻力场提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We address the effective nonequilibrium drag force field that emerges from the microscopic interparticle interactions in steady states of counterdriven binary fluid mixtures. Using power functional scaling arguments for adaptive Brownian dynamics computer simulation results, we establish quantitatively the crossover between near-equilibrium linear response and far-nonequilibrium square root asymptotics. An algebraic expression captures both limiting cases and remains applicable in the crossover regime. Using simulation results as benchmarks, we verify that a local power functional approximation based on the scaling law reproduces the spatial nonequilibrium structure formation in inhomogenously driven systems. The crossover scenario transcends dynamical density functional theory and it sheds light on general nonequilibrium scaling of driven fluids.

### [62] [Discovering Thermodynamically Admissible Dissipation Potentials via Grammar-Based Symbolic Regression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31532)
*Federico Califano,Jacopo Ciambella*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于符号回归（symbolic regression）的框架，在广义标准材料（Generalized Standard Materials, GSM）形式体系下，从数据中自动发现满足热力学约束（凸性和非负性）的耗散势（dissipation potential），从而保证非弹性材料本构定律的热力学允许性（thermodynamic admissibility）。该框架在合成数据和真实实验数据上均得到验证，能复现动态模量的振幅依赖软化行为，且优于线性Zener基线模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前数据驱动的非弹性材料本构模型方法虽然可能通过物理编码架构（physics-encoded architectures）提供形式上的热力学保证，但往往牺牲了可解释性（interpretability）。因此，需要一种既能严格满足热力学允许性要求（如Clausius-Duhem不等式导出的凸性和非负性），又能保持模型可解释性的数据驱动方法。

Method: 在广义标准材料（GSM）形式体系内，从Clausius-Duhem不等式出发，将对偶耗散势（dual dissipation potential）必须满足的热力学要求（凸性和非负性）形式化地表述为一般子微分（subdifferential）设定下的约束条件，涵盖率相关（viscoelastic）和粘塑性（viscoplastic）耗散机制。候选势函数由一种基于组合扩展的保凸文法（composition-extended convexity-preserving grammar）生成，从而在构造层面保证热力学允许性。

Result: 在合成数据集（包括牛顿型、幂律型及Bingham粘塑性真实模型，含过程和测量噪声）上，以及合成弹性体（synthetic elastomer）的振荡剪切实验数据（多个应变幅值和频率）上得到验证。发现的耗散势能复现动态模量的振幅依赖软化（amplitude-dependent softening）行为，性能优于校准后的线性Zener基线模型。

Conclusion: 该符号回归框架能够在保证热力学允许性的前提下，从数据中自动发现具有可解释性的非弹性材料耗散势，为数据驱动本构建模提供了一种兼顾严格物理约束与模型可解释性的有效途径。

Abstract: Constitutive laws for inelastic materials must satisfy strict thermodynamic admissibility requirements, yet current data-driven approaches sacrifice interpretability, even when formal guarantees are provided by physics-encoded architectures. We propose a symbolic regression framework for the data-driven discovery of dissipation potentials governing the evolution of internal variables within the Generalized Standard Materials (GSM) formalism. Starting from the Clausius--Duhem inequality, we enforce the thermodynamic requirements, convexity and non-negativity, that the dual dissipation potential must satisfy to guarantee non-negative mechanical dissipation. These requirements are formulated in the general subdifferential setting, encompassing rate-dependent (viscoelastic) and viscoplastic dissipative mechanisms, including potentials with genuine elastic domains, within a unified framework. Candidate potentials are generated by a composition-extended convexity-preserving grammar that guarantees thermodynamic admissibility \emph{by construction}. The framework is validated on synthetic datasets spanning Newtonian, power-law, and Bingham viscoplastic ground truths under process and measurement noise, and on experimental oscillatory shear measurements of a synthetic elastomer across multiple strain amplitudes and frequencies, where the discovered potentials reproduce the amplitude-dependent softening of the dynamic moduli and outperform a calibrated linear Zener baseline.

*Quentin Berger,Shuta Nakajima*

TL;DR: 本文研究二维有向聚合物模型（directed polymer model）在高温柔乱（high-temperature regime）下的自由能（free energy），给出了尖锐的下界，并利用渗流论证（percolation argument）和“对数能量”（log-energy）有界性，最终结合已有结果得到了自由能随逆温参数β趋于零时的渐近行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维是临界维度（critical dimension），该模型在该维度下的自由能行为是关注焦点，特别是高温柔乱下的精确下界尚未明确。

Method: 采用受Lacoin（2010）启发的渗流论证（percolation argument），引入“对数能量”（log-energy）有界性这一关键性质，该性质量化了聚合物测度在扩散尺度上的正则性，并证明该性质可沿开放路径传播。

Result: 结合Berger, Caravenna, and Turchi (2025)的定理2.8，得到了自由能的渐近下界：−𝔣(β) ≍ exp(−π/σ²(β))，当β↓0时。

Conclusion: 给出了二维有向聚合物模型在高温柔乱下自由能的尖锐下界，揭示了自由能随逆温参数衰减的指数形式。

Abstract: We consider the directed polymer model on $\mathbb{Z}^d$, in an i.i.d.\ random environment $ω=(ω_{n,x})_{n\geq 0,x\in\mathbb Z^d}$, focusing on the critical dimension $d=2$. Our main contribution is to give a sharp lower bound on the free energy in the high-temperature regime. Our proof uses a percolation argument inspired by Lacoin (2010), for which we introduce a key property of bounded ``$\log$-energy'': this property quantifies the regularity of the polymer measures at diffusive scales and we show that it propagates along open paths. Writing $\mathfrak{f}(β)$ for the quenched free energy, and setting $λ(β):=\log \mathbb E[e^{βω_{1,0}}]$ and $σ(β)^2:=e^{λ(2β)-2λ(β)}-1$, our lower bound combined with Theorem 2.8 of Berger, Caravenna, and Turchi (2025) gives
  $$
  -\mathfrak{f}(β) \asymp \exp{\Big(- \fracπ{σ^2(β)}\Big)},\quad \text{ as $β\downarrow 0$.}
  $$

### [64] [Search at bounded speed with immigration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30629)
*Hwai-Ray Tung,Sean D Lawley*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究以有限速度移动的“迁入式”搜索者（immigrating searchers）的搜索时间，在快速迁入极限下，建立了第k次搜索时间的完整概率分布与各阶矩的数学表达式，并将其应用于随机搜索的经典模型与数值模拟中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多生物物理搜索过程中，搜索者随时间逐步进入（迁入）搜索域。现有搜索时间估计在快速迁入条件下因假设搜索者无限速运动而产生非物理结果，因此亟需建立考虑有限迁移速度的搜索时间理论。

Method: 在快速迁入（fast immigration）极限下，推导第k次搜索时间的完整概率分布及所有矩（moments）的解析表达式，这些表达式归结为单个搜索者在早期时间概率分布的泛函。随后将结果应用于几种典型的随机搜索（stochastic search）模型，并分析不同“扩散（diffusion）”模型对搜索时间的影响。

Result: 严格数学结果表明，快速迁入极限下第k次搜索时间的概率分布与矩可由单搜索者早期时间分布完全刻画。应用于经典随机搜索模型后，揭示了搜索者动态细节对搜索时间的影响条件与方式，理论预测与数值模拟（numerical simulations）吻合。

Conclusion: 所提出的理论框架为有限速度迁入式搜索提供了物理合理的搜索时间估计，弥合了现有无限速假设下非物理结果的缺陷，并为理解生物物理搜索过程中微观动态细节的角色提供了新视角。

Abstract: Many biophysical search processes employ searchers which enter or "immigrate" into the domain progressively over time. Existing search time estimates can become unphysical for fast immigration since they imply that searchers move at infinite speed. In this paper, we investigate search times of immigrating searchers that move at bounded speed. In the fast immigration limit, we determine the full probability distribution and all the moments of the $k$th search time in terms of the early time probability distribution of a single searcher. We apply these rigorous mathematical results to several canonical models of stochastic search. We further analyze different models of "diffusion" and use these results to investigate when and how the minutiae of searcher dynamics affect search times. We compare our theory to numerical simulations.

### [65] [A Boundary--Residue Incidence Coalgebra for Associahedral Scattering Forms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30390)
*Ioannis P. Zois*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文引入了一种与正几何（positive geometry）的面偏序集（face poset）相关联的边界-余项关联余代数（boundary--residue incidence coalgebra），并将其应用于结合面体（associahedron）散射形式。通过该结构，证明了树图等级联平面因子化通道（nested planar factorisation channels）与规范形式（canonical form）留数（residue）之间的关联，并推广至圈图（loop-level）与非平面情形，最后与细胞状时空（cellular spacetime）的关联余代数进行了比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受Connes--Kreimer余积（coproduct）在费曼图（Feynman graphs）上的递归留数结构与规范形式递归留数结构之间类比的启发，旨在为正几何中的散射振幅因子化提供一种代数框架。

Method: 定义了与正几何面偏序集关联的边界-余项关联余代数；在Stasheff结合面体（associahedron \(K_n\)）情形下，证明了该关联余积记录了树图级标量振幅（tree-level scalar amplitude）的所有中间嵌套平面因子化通道；对于圈图情形，将面偏序集替换为对应圈几何的边界偏序集（boundary poset）；在非平面情形，在对数奇点分层（logarithmic singularity strata）层面定义关联余代数。

Result: 在结合面体上，面标签为(n+1)边形非交叉剖分（non-crossing dissection）的子多边形所对应的规范形式留数，分解为更低维结合面体上规范形式的外积（exterior product）。以五边形结合面体\(K_4\)（对应五点平面标量振幅）为例展示了该构造。圈图情形以单圈环面体（halohedron）作为标量例子给出。

Conclusion: 有限正则CW复形（regular CW complex）的面偏序集可重构其重心细分（barycentric subdivision）及底层多面体，而正几何中相同的关联机制组织了规范形式留数。这建立了一种**关联优先（incidence-first）**的桥梁，连接了细胞状时空拓扑与正几何振幅因子化，且无需假设度量或因果数据由拓扑决定。

Abstract: We introduce a boundary--residue incidence coalgebra associated with the face poset of a positive geometry and apply it to associahedral scattering forms. The construction is motivated by the analogy between the Connes--Kreimer coproduct on Feynman graphs and the recursive residue structure of canonical forms. For the Stasheff associahedron \(K_n\), whose faces are indexed by non-crossing dissections of an \((n+1)\)-gon, we prove that the incidence coproduct records all intermediate nested planar factorisation channels of the corresponding tree-level scalar amplitude. The residue of the canonical form on a face labelled by a dissection factorises as the exterior product of canonical forms on the lower associahedra associated with the resulting subpolygons. We illustrate the construction explicitly for the pentagon associahedron \(K_4\), corresponding to the five-point planar scalar amplitude. We then formulate a loop-level extension: whenever a planar loop integrand is represented by a positive geometry, the associahedral face poset is replaced by the boundary poset of the corresponding loop geometry. The one-loop halohedron gives a concrete scalar example, while in the non-planar case we define the associated incidence coalgebra at the level of logarithmic singularity strata. Finally, we compare the boundary--residue coalgebra with the cellular incidence coalgebra of a triangulated or regular CW spacetime. The face poset of a finite regular CW complex reconstructs its barycentric subdivision, and hence its underlying polyhedron, while in positive geometry the same incidence mechanism organises canonical-form residues. This yields an incidence-first bridge between cellular spacetime topology and positive-geometric amplitude factorisation, without assuming that metric or causal data are determined by topology.

### [66] [BV pushforward as a quasi-isomorphism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30558)
*Alberto S. Cattaneo,Pavel Mnev*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了BV理论中从全场空间到红外子空间的pushforward映射P*是BV复形的拟同构，通过同伦扰动引理构造了强形变收缩，并给出了两种证明及拟逆映射的显式表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在BV（Batalin-Vilkovisky）理论中，场空间被分为红外（infrared，IR）和紫外（ultraviolet，UV）两个子空间后，需要理解有效理论中可观测量与全场理论可观测量之间的关系，特别是验证红外pushforward映射P*保持BV复形结构。

Method: 利用同伦扰动引理（homological perturbation lemma）构造一个强形变收缩（strong deformation retraction），使P*成为其组成部分。给出两种证明路径：(i) 比较P*的费曼图（Feynman diagrams）与同伦扰动理论中的缆线图（cable diagrams）；(ii) 利用拓扑量子力学（topological quantum mechanics）及其AKSZ理论实现。

Result: 证明了P*是BV复形之间的拟同构（quasi-isomorphism），并给出了其拟逆映射i_int的显式公式。在拓扑量子力学视角下，i_int可写为路径积分（path integral）形式，其经典极限（classical limit）亦可研究。

Conclusion: 本文通过两种互补方法严格建立了BV有效理论中红外pushforward映射的拟同构性质，为全场理论与有效理论之间可观测量对应关系提供了系统的同伦代数框架。

Abstract: Given a BV theory on a space of fields split into two subspaces ("infrared" and "ultraviolet"), one has the BV pushforward map $P_*$, sending observables to observables of the effective theory on the infrared space. This note proves that $P_*$ is a quasi-isomorphism of BV complexes, by realizing it as a part of a strong deformation retraction constructed using the homological perturbation lemma. Two proofs are given: (i) comparing Feynman diagrams for $P_*$ with "cable diagrams" arising from homological perturbation theory and (ii) using topological quantum mechanics. This construction gives a formula for the quasi-inverse $i_\mathrm{int}$ of $P_*$ - the map lifting observables of the effective theory to the full theory. The topological quantum mechanics perspective - and its realization as an AKSZ theory - allows one to write $i_\mathrm{int}$ as a path integral (realizing cable diagrams for $i_\mathrm{int}$ as Feynman diagrams) and to study its classical limit.

</details>


### [67] [A sharp three-particle fractional Hardy inequality and an angular Selberg-type identity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30586)
*Rajesh Mahadevan,Franco Olivares,Andres Zuniga*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文建立了一个尖锐的三粒子分数阶哈代不等式，该不等式涉及显式的三体相互作用势，并证明其最优常数。通过新的塞尔伯格型奇异积分恒等式，论文进一步推导了多粒子分数阶哈代不等式和改良的库仑型不等式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在将多粒子哈代不等式推广到分数阶拉普拉斯算子（fractional Laplacian）情形，并揭示超越标准两体库仑相互作用的纯粹三体效应。

Method: 采用分数阶基态表示法（fractional ground-state representation method）处理三粒子相互作用，并结合对非局部相互作用项的显式评估；该评估依赖于一个新颖的塞尔伯格型奇异积分恒等式（Selberg-type singular integral identity），将Grafakos-Morpurgo的三重公式推广到非径向情形。

Result: 建立了在维数$d\geq 4-2s$下关于阶数$s\in(0,1)$的拉普拉斯算子的尖锐三粒子分数阶哈代不等式，其最优常数是两粒子分数阶哈代常数$C_{fH}(d,s)$。由此推导出$N\geq 3$的非平凡多粒子分数阶哈代不等式，并在$N>d+1$时得到一个常数严格增大的改良库仑型不等式。

Conclusion: 三体势$V_{s,3}$严格优于标准的逐对库仑型相互作用，捕捉了真正的三体效应；所得结果与Hoffmann-Ostenhof等人及Lundholm关于多粒子哈代不等式的工作在精神上一致。所建立的塞尔伯格型奇异积分恒等式在调和分析中可能具有独立意义。

Abstract: We establish a sharp three-particle fractional Hardy inequality for the Laplacian of order $s\in(0,1)$ in dimension $d\geq 4-2s$ (Theorem 1.1), involving an explicit intrinsically three-body interaction potential $V_{s,3}$. The inequality holds with the optimal two-particle fractional Hardy constant $C_{fH}(d,s)$, which is shown to be sharp relative to the fixed potential $V_{s,3}$. This potential $V_{s,3}$ strictly dominates the standard pairwise Coulomb-type interaction and captures genuine three-body effects. As a consequence, we derive a nontrivial many-particle fractional Hardy inequality for $N\geq 3$, and, in the regime $N>d+1$, obtain an improved Coulomb-type inequality with a strictly larger constant, agreeing in spirit with the results of Hoffmann-Ostenhof et al. [M. Hoffmann-Ostenhof, T. Hoffmann-Ostenhof, A. Laptev, and J. Tidblom, "Many-particle Hardy inequalities", J. Lond. Math. Soc. 77 (2008), no. 2, 99-115] and Lundholm [D. Lundholm, "Geometric extensions of many-particle Hardy inequalities", J. Phys. A: Math. Theor. 48 (2015), no. 17, 175203]. The proof relies on a fractional ground-state representation method adapted to three-particle interactions, combined with an explicit evaluation of the resulting nonlocal interaction term. This evaluation is achieved through a new singular integral identity of Selberg-type (Theorem 1.2), extending the three-fold formula of Grafakos-Morpurgo [L. Grafakos and C. Morpurgo, "A Selberg integral formula and applications", Pacific J. Math. 191 (1999), no. 1, 85-94] beyond the radial setting. This identity provides the analytic mechanism underlying the emergence of the three-body potential and may be of independent interest in harmonic analysis.

</details>


### [68] [Hubbard--Heisenberg Thermodynamic Comparison at Half Filling in a Fixed Staggered Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30663)
*Tadahiro Miyao*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，半满强耦合排斥性哈伯德模型（repulsive Hubbard model）在交错磁场（staggered magnetic field）作用下，其有限体积哈伯德-海森堡压力（Hubbard–Heisenberg pressure）估计在系统尺寸上一致成立，并进一步证明了磁化比较与电荷扇区抑制估计，从而在吉布斯态（Gibbs-state）层面定量验证了强耦合图像中海森堡尺度（Heisenberg scale）下有效反铁磁自旋自由度主导、电荷涨落被抑制的物理图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在半满条件下，强耦合排斥性哈伯德模型（Hubbard model）与有效海森堡模型（Heisenberg model）之间的关系是凝聚态理论的核心问题之一。尽管物理图像直观，但在有限系统尺寸和有限温度下对该对应关系进行严格定量的数学分析仍具有重要理论意义。本文旨在建立均匀一致的压力估计、磁化比较与电荷扇区抑制估计，以严格形式刻画该模型的强耦合行为。

Method: 采用强耦合幺正变换（strong-coupling unitary transformation），将单占据自旋扇区（singly occupied spin sector）与包含空位或双占据位点的扇区分离开来。在单占据扇区上，将有效哈密顿量与海森堡参考哈密顿量（Heisenberg reference Hamiltonian）进行比较；其余扇区则通过对变换后配分函数（partition function）按空位或双占据位点进行分解来控制。磁化比较通过有限体积压力的凸性（convexity）从压力比较中导出。

Result: 在交错磁场强度|h|≤h₀且βJ₀(U)≥ℓ₀的条件下，建立了系统尺寸一致的有限体积哈伯德-海森堡压力估计，并可在极限压力存在时传递到热力学极限（thermodynamic limits）。对于固定正交错磁场窗口I⊂(0,h₀]，推导出磁化比较。在|h|≤h₀的大正U海森堡尺度区域，证明了电荷扇区抑制估计：空位或双占据位点密度、双占据密度均很小，且交错电荷平方除以|Λ|²很小。

Conclusion: 结果为强耦合图像提供了定量的吉布斯态表述：半满排斥性哈伯德模型在海森堡尺度下由有效的反铁磁自旋自由度描述，而电荷涨落被抑制。这严格验证了物理直观，即在强耦合极限下，模型行为由自旋扇区的海森堡动力学主导。

Abstract: We study the repulsive Hubbard model at half filling in the strong-coupling regime, with a staggered magnetic field of strength \(h\). The analysis is carried out in the canonical half-filled ensemble, with temperature measured on the Heisenberg scale \(J_0(U)=4t^2/U\). Uniformly for \(|h|\le h_0\) and \(βJ_0(U)\ge \ell_0\), we prove finite-volume Hubbard--Heisenberg pressure estimates with errors uniform in the system size. These estimates pass to thermodynamic limits whenever the limiting pressures exist.
  The proof uses a strong-coupling unitary transformation which separates the singly occupied spin sector from sectors containing empty or doubly occupied sites. On the singly occupied sector, the effective Hamiltonian is compared with the Heisenberg reference Hamiltonian; the remaining sectors are controlled through a decomposition of the transformed partition function according to the set of empty or doubly occupied sites. For fixed positive staggered-field windows \(I\Subset(0,h_0]\), the magnetisation comparison is then derived from the pressure comparison by convexity of finite-volume pressures.
  We also prove charge-sector suppression estimates, uniformly for \(|h|\le h_0\): in the large positive-\(U\) Heisenberg-scale regime, the density of empty or doubly occupied sites and the double-occupancy density are small, and the squared staggered charge divided by \(|Λ|^2\) is small. Thus the results give a quantitative Gibbs-state formulation of the strong-coupling picture in which the half-filled repulsive Hubbard model is described, at the Heisenberg scale, by effective antiferromagnetic spin degrees of freedom, while charge fluctuations are suppressed.

</details>

### [70] [Numerical analytical continuation of multivariate hypergeometric functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31553)
*M. A. Bezuglov,B. A. Kniehl,A. I. Onishchenko,O. L. Veretin*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一个通用框架，用于高精度数值求解定义为主微分方程组的全纯系统（holonomic systems）解的多变量超几何函数（multivariate hypergeometric functions）。该方法借鉴并扩展了多圈费曼积分（multi-loop Feynman integrals）的处理技术，通过Laporta约化算法构建Pfaffian系统，并利用Frobenius方法实现局部幂级数解的精确计算与沿规定路径的数值传输。论文还系统分析了多值性与分支结构（branch structure），展示了如何通过Frobenius方法控制访问不同黎曼叶（Riemann sheets），并在解析延拓过程中追踪解的变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多变量超几何函数在数学物理多个领域中具有重要应用，但其高精度数值计算仍面临挑战。现有方法在处理此类函数的全纯系统与多值分支结构时缺乏通用性与系统性，亟需建立一种既能实现可控精度又能处理解析延拓的数值框架。

Method: 方法分为三步：首先，将多变量超几何函数视为全纯偏微分方程组的解，采用Laporta约化算法（Laporta reduction algorithm）从适当的微分关系系统中构造出Pfaffian系统（Pfaffian systems）。其次，基于Frobenius方法（Frobenius method）构建数值方案，在变量空间中沿规定路径计算并传输具有可控精度的局部幂级数解。最后，通过Frobenius方法系统分析多值性与分支结构，实现不同黎曼叶的受控访问，并追踪解析延拓过程中函数值的变化。

Result: 成功建立了适用于任意多变量超几何函数的高精度数值计算通用框架，实现了局部幂级数解的精确计算与沿指定路径的数值传输。同时，论文提供了系统分析多值性与分支结构的方法，使得在解析延拓过程中能够控制性地访问不同黎曼叶并追踪解的变化。

Conclusion: 该框架将多圈费曼积分领域的高级数值技术系统地推广至多变量超几何函数的计算中，为高精度数值评估与解析结构分析提供了统一且通用的解决方案。

Abstract: We present a general framework for the high-precision numerical evaluation of multivariate hypergeometric functions defined as solutions of holonomic systems of partial differential equations. Our approach adapts and extends methods originally developed for multi-loop Feynman integrals to the setting of hypergeometric functions of many variables. In particular, we construct Pfaffian systems for arbitrary multivariate hypergeometric functions by applying the Laporta reduction algorithm to suitable systems of differential relations. Next, we construct a numerical scheme based on the Frobenius method, which allows us to compute local power-series solutions with controlled precision and to transport them along prescribed paths in the space of variables. A central part of the paper is devoted to a systematic analysis of multivaluedness and branch structure: we show how the Frobenius method can be used to access different Riemann sheets in a controlled way and to track changes of the solution under analytic continuation around singular loci.

### [72] [$q$-Exponential Random Graphs: higher-order networks from simple constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31209)
*David Dobáš,Diego Garlaschelli,Petr Jizba*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本文在非香农（Shannon）熵框架下推广了指数随机图（ERGs），通过最大化Uffink熵族得到q-指数随机图，发现即使保持的约束条件不变，该高阶网络模型也能自然产生稀疏-稠密相变、丰富的同配性和聚类结构等香农框架下不存在的现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期发现，在没有额外信息偏爱香农熵的情况下，最无偏的推断构造应最大化更广义的Uffink熵族，而香农熵可能产生自由度间不合理的独立性假设。本文旨在研究当使用非香农熵时，最常见的独立边指数随机图（如Erdos-Renyi模型和配置模型）如何推广为具有依赖边的高阶q-指数随机图。

Method: 作者保持原有约束条件（链接数目和度序列）不变，将最大化对象从香农熵切换为Uffink熵族，从而将传统的指数随机图推广为q-指数随机图（q-Exponential Random Graphs），使边的独立性假设被解除，边之间产生依赖关系。

Result: 发现了原始ERGs中不存在但在高阶网络中典型的稀疏-稠密相变（phase transition），以及更丰富的同配性（assortativity）和聚类（clustering）特征——允许链接稀疏性与三角闭包（triadic closure）共存。

Conclusion: 高阶网络并不必然需要高阶约束条件，它们可以在比香农框架更无偏的框架下，从更简单的约束条件中自然涌现。

Abstract: Exponential Random Graphs (ERGs) are among the most widely used network models, derived as principled least-bias graph ensembles that maximize Shannon entropy under constraints on the expected values of given structural properties. However, it has been recently (re)discovered that, in the absence of additional information privileging Shannon entropy, the most agnostic inferential construction should maximize the broader class of Uffink entropies. The resulting entropy-maximizing distribution changes from the exponential (Boltzmann-Gibbs) to the so-called q-exponential one. Since maximizing Shannon entropy may produce an unjustified independence between degrees of freedom, here we investigate how the most popular ERGs with independent edges (namely, the Erdos-Renyi and configuration models) generalize to higher-order q-Exponential Random Graphs with dependent edges in the non-Shannon case, while keeping their defining constraints (number of links and degree sequence, respectively) unchanged. We find features, such as a phase transition between sparse and dense regimes, that are absent in the original ERGs but typical of higher-order networks, plus novel phenomena such as richer assortativity and clustering profiles, which allow for the coexistence of link sparsity and triadic closure. These results show that higher-order networks do not necessarily require higher-order constraints, as they naturally arise from simpler ones in a framework that is even more agnostic than Shannon's.

</details>

### [73] [Ni-O hybridization-driven electronic reconstruction across the superconducting dome in an infinite-layer nickelate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30752)
*Chi Sin Tang,Shengwei Zeng,Xing Gao,Zhaoyang Luo,Xiongfang Liu,Zhi Shiuh Lim,Saurav Prakash,Ping Yang,Caozheng Diao,Xinmao Yin,Changjian Li,Huajun Liu,Mark B. H. Breese,A. Ariando*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文利用X射线吸收谱（X-ray absorption spectroscopy）系统测量了无限层镍氧化物（infinite-layer nickelate）La1-xCaxNiO2中依赖掺杂（doping）和温度的未占据态（unoccupied states），发现超导发生在0.18≤x≤0.27区间。在x≈0.20–0.23附近观察到一个轨道选择性交叉（orbital-selective crossover）——Ni 3d主导态减少而O 2p杂化态增加，该过程与霍尔系数（Hall coefficient）符号反转及超导临界温度（superconducting critical temperature）随更高掺杂降低的现象一致，从而将输运异常与超导穹顶（superconducting dome）直接关联到可测量的Ni-O轨道重组（orbital reorganization）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无限层镍酸盐作为铜酸盐（cuprate）类似物引发了广泛关注，但其电子结构（electronic structure）随空穴掺杂（hole doping）如何演化仍无定论。本研究旨在通过直接测量未占据态随掺杂和温度的变化，揭示轨道重构与超导及输运性质之间的内在联系。

Method: 采用O K-edge和Ni L-edge X射线吸收谱（X-ray absorption spectroscopy, XAS）测量了La基无限层镍酸盐La1-xCaxNiO2中依赖掺杂和温度的未占据态，覆盖从非超导到超导再到过掺杂的完整区间。

Result: 超导出现在0.18≤x≤0.27范围内；在x≈0.20–0.23附近，Ni 3d主导态强度降低而O 2p杂化态强度升高，表明发生了Ni-O共价性（covalency）的轨道选择性交叉。该交叉与霍尔系数符号反转同时发生，并先于更高掺杂下超导临界温度的下降。

Conclusion: 输运异常和超导穹顶被直接归因于可测量的Ni-O轨道重组，这为建立统一的无限层镍酸盐轨道分辨相图（orbital-resolved phase diagram）提供了关键一步，也为通过杂化调控（hybridization control）工程化超导提供了实用路线。

Abstract: Superconductivity in infinite-layer nickelates has drawn wide interest as a cuprate analogue, yet how the electronic structure evolves with hole doping remains unsettled. Here we map the doping- and temperature-dependent unoccupied states of the La-based infinite-layer nickelate La1-xCaxNiO2 using O K-edge and Ni L-edge x-ray absorption spectroscopy. Superconductivity occurs for 0.18<=x<=0.27. Near x~0.20-0.23, low-energy spectral weight redistributes: Ni3d-dominated states decrease while O2p-hybridized states increase, indicating an orbital-selective crossover in Ni-O covalency. This crossover coincides with a sign reversal of the Hall coefficient and precedes the reduction of the superconducting critical temperature at higher doping. By directly linking transport anomalies and the superconducting dome to a measurable Ni-O orbital reorganization, our results provide a key step toward a unified, orbital-resolved phase diagram for infinite-layer nickelates and a practical route to engineer superconductivity via hybridization control.

### [74] [Bending-like stress induced by solder joint under uniaxial tensile testing in 2G-HTS tapes: Impact and optimization approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30760)
*Dean Liu,Yue Wu,Haoliang Xiang,Xiaofen Li,Caida Fu,Chiheng Dong,Yue Zhao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 第二代高温超导（2G-HTS）带材的可逆应力极限（reversible stress limit, Rrev）是关键的机电性能（electromechanical performance, EMP）指标，但实际测量中，电压引线焊点引起的应力集中（stress concentration）会显著影响Rrev的测量精度，亟需探明其干扰机制并发展优化方案。

Method: 采用集成实验与数值方法（integrated experimental and numerical methods）对焊点干扰机制进行机理分析（mechanistic analysis），并据此提出背面焊接（back-surface soldering）优化方案，通过实验验证其对于不同带材构型（tape configurations）的改善效果。

Result: 焊点引起的局部几何不均匀性在单轴拉伸下诱导出外部弯曲型应力（bending-like stress）；当焊点位于带材正面（靠近超导层一侧）时，超导层承受局部附加拉应力（additional tensile stress），导致临界电流（Ic）过早退化。采用背面焊接后，超导层处于局部压缩区（localized compressive zone）；对于铜层厚度5 μm的带材，Rrev从546 MPa提升至734 MPa（增幅42%），更接近真实值。

Conclusion: 提出的背面焊接优化方法可有效缓解多种带材构型下的测量误差，为2G-HTS带材机电性能（electromechanical performances, EMPs）的精确表征提供了关键见解。

Abstract: The reversible stress limit (\mathit{R}_{rev}) of second-generation high-temperature superconducting (2G-HTS) tapes is a critical performance indicator, typically characterized through uniaxial tensile testing. In practice, the accuracy of the measured Rrev value is often compromised by stress concentration induced by the voltage tap solder joint. The present study investigates the underlying interference mechanism using integrated experimental and numerical methods. Mechanistic analysis reveals that under uniaxial tensile loading, the local geometric inhomogeneity introduced by the solder joint induces an external, bending-like stress in the vicinity of the solder joint, transitioning from additional tensile stress in the zone adjacent to the joint to additional compressive stress in the zone remote from it. When the solder joint is attached to the front surface of the tape (the side closer to the superconducting layer), the superconducting layer experiences localized additional tensile stress, triggering premature damage and early \mathit{I}_{c} degradation. Consequently, an optimized back-surface soldering approach is proposed, which positions the superconducting layer in a localized compressive zone. Experimental validation demonstrates that the proposed approach effectively mitigates testing errors for various tape configurations. Notably, for the tape with a copper layer thickness of 5 μm, the measured \mathit{R}_{rev} increased from 546 MPa to 734 MPa, corresponding to a 42% increase, and moved closer to the actual value. The findings provide essential insights for the precision characterization of the electromechanical performances (EMPs) of 2G-HTS tapes.

</details>


### [75] [Terahertz Electrodynamics and Kinetic Inductance of Disordered Titanium-Vanadium Alloy Thin Films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30847)
*Shekhar Chandra Pandey,Shilpam Sharma,Ashish Khandelwal,M. K. Chattopadhyay*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con
