<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索无序超导体（disordered superconductors）在高频电动力学响应中的物理机制，并为下一代量子探测器和超导器件的开发提供材料与理论依据。

Method: 采用太赫兹时域光谱（terahertz time-domain spectroscopy, THz-TDS）技术，对无序Ti40V60合金薄膜进行测量，分析其复电导率（complex conductivity）、穿透深度（penetration depth）和超流体响应（superfluid response）。

Result: 结构无序可系统性地调控薄膜的感应响应，同时保持稳定的超导相（superconducting phase）；Ti40V60合金具备比传统氮化物超导体更简便可控的制备路线。

Conclusion: Ti40V60合金是制作动能电感探测器（kinetic inductance detectors）的潜力材料，并为强无序超导体的电动力学研究提供了重要见解。

Abstract: Disordered superconductors represent an important area in modern condensed matter physics, where superconductivity survives even in the presence of strong electron scattering and localization effects. Understanding how disorder modifies the high-frequency electrodynamic response is not only important from physics point of view, but is also essential for developing next-generation quantum detectors and superconducting devices. In this work, we investigate the terahertz electrodynamics of disordered Ti40V60 alloy thin films using terahertz time-domain spectroscopy (THz-TDS) to understand the relationship between disorder, quasiparticle dynamics, and kinetic inductance. By analysing the complex conductivity, penetration depth and superfluid response, we show that structural disorder can be systematically used to tune the inductive response while maintaining a robust superconducting phase. Unlike conventional nitride superconductors that require tightly controlled reactive growth conditions, Ti40V60 alloys provide a simpler and more adaptable route for tuning the superconducting energy scales directly through the deposition conditions. These findings establish Ti40V60 alloys as a promising material for kinetic inductance detectors and provide useful insights into the electrodynamics of strongly disordered superconductors.

### [76] [What controls the superconducting dome of electron-doped FeSe?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31459)
*Paul T. Malinowski,Chad J. Mowers,Yaoju Tarn,Darrell G. Schlom,Brendan D. Faeth,Kyle M. Shen*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy）合成、碱金属表面掺杂、真空电输运及角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy）等综合手段，首次完整绘制了电子掺杂FeSe的超导拱顶（superconducting dome），发现超导转变温度（Tc）与剩余电阻率（ρ₀）在全掺杂范围内存在稳健的标度关系，表明电子掺杂FeSe的超导拱顶主要由无序敏感性（disorder sensitivity）驱动，而非掺杂本身，这与其他非常规超导体（unconventional superconductors）存在本质区别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: FeSe的电子掺杂可大幅提升超导转变温度（Tc），但其完整的相图与超导拱顶（superconducting dome）尚未被系统探索，这与所有其他高温及非常规超导体（unconventional superconductors）形成鲜明对比。

Method: 研究结合了分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy）合成、碱金属（alkali）表面掺杂、真空电输运测量以及角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy）等多种实验手段，覆盖电子掺杂FeSe的整个超导拱顶（superconducting dome），并实现了重度过掺杂（heavily overdoped）区域的完全金属态，超导电性被抑制。

Result: 发现在整个超导拱顶（superconducting dome）范围内，超导转变温度（Tc）与剩余电阻率（ρ₀）之间存在稳健的标度关系（scaling），暗示Tc的演化受高温电子掺杂相中弹性散射率（elastic scattering rate）变化的强烈影响。

Conclusion: 电子掺杂FeSe的超导拱顶（superconducting dome）从根本上不同于其他非常规超导体（unconventional superconductors）——后者的超导拱顶主要由掺杂（doping）驱动，而FeSe电子掺杂相的超导拱顶可能主要由超导电性对无序（disorder）的敏感性所驱动。

Abstract: Superconducting domes are conspicuous features of the phase diagrams of most unconventional and high-temperature superconductors. The superconducting transition temperature ($T_{c}$) of FeSe can be dramatically enhanced with electron doping, but unlike all other high-temperature and unconventional superconductors, its full phase diagram and superconducting dome have yet to be fully explored. Here, we employ a combination of molecular beam epitaxy synthesis, alkali surface doping, in-vacuum electrical transport, and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy to investigate the entire superconducting dome of electron-doped FeSe, achieving a fully metallic state where superconductivity is suppressed in the heavily overdoped regime. We discover a robust scaling between $T_{c}$ and the residual resistivity ($ρ_{0}$) which holds across the entire superconducting dome, suggesting that the evolution of $T_{c}$ is heavily influenced by the evolution of the elastic scattering rate in the high-$T_{c}$ electron-doped phase. This in turn suggests that the superconducting dome in electron-doped FeSe appears to be fundamentally different than that of other unconventional superconductors where doping plays the primary role, and may be driven primarily by the sensitivity of the superconductivity to disorder.

### [77] [Kohn-Luttinger Superconductivity of Weyl Fermi Arcs in PtBi$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31501)
*Reuel Dsouza,Nikolaos Parthenios,Brian M. Andersen,Morten H. Christensen*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非中心对称Weyl半金属PtBi₂的实验观测表明，拓扑表面态——Weyl费米弧（Weyl Fermi arcs）——承载了非常规超导，且每个费米弧中心存在一个节点。该现象缺乏理论解释，本文旨在为这一实验观测提供理论机制。

Method: 采用Kohn-Luttinger方法（Kohn-Luttinger approach）计算电子介导的配对相互作用，聚焦于Weyl费米弧的表面态；并系统研究主导超导不稳定性对电子相互作用参数和化学势（chemical potential）的依赖关系。

Result: 在相图（phase diagram）的大片区域中，主导超导不稳定性（leading superconducting instability）具有i波对称性（i-wave symmetry），恰好呈现实验观测到的弧内节点（intra-arc node）。该i波态对模型参数变化表现出鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 研究结果为PtBi₂表面拓扑i波超导（topological i-wave superconductivity）的观测提供了可能的理论机制，并对Weyl半金属表面由排斥相互作用产生的超导不稳定性更广泛的研究图景具有启示意义。

Abstract: Recent experimental observations in the noncentrosymmetric Weyl semimetal PtBi$_2$ indicate unconventional superconductivity hosted by topological surface states -- Weyl Fermi arcs -- with a node at the center of each arc. Focusing on these Fermi arcs, we calculate the electronically mediated pairing interaction using a Kohn-Luttinger approach and find that, in a large region of the phase diagram, the leading superconducting instability has an $i$-wave symmetry featuring precisely such an intra-arc node. We study the dependence of the leading superconducting instabilities on electronic interaction parameters and chemical potential and show that the $i$-wave state is robust to changes in the model parameters. Our results provide a possible mechanism for the observation of topological $i$-wave superconductivity on the surface of PtBi$_2$ and may have implications for the broader landscape of superconducting instabilities arising from repulsive interactions on the surfaces of Weyl semimetals.

### [78] [Closed-form linear moments of the two-dimensional angular central Gaussian distribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31536)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管角度中心高斯（angular central Gaussian, ACG）分布的三角函数矩（trigonometric moments）和向量值矩（vector-valued moments）已有详细研究，但其在线性意义下的一阶矩 E[θ] 和二阶矩 E[θ²] 尚无显式闭式表达式。该空白在物理等领域需要将 θ 视为实值相位（real-valued phase）而非圆变量（circular variable）时尤为突出。

Method: 推导基于绕反正切函数（arctan z）分支割线（branch cut）的围道积分（contour integration），方法属于初等分析范畴。

Result: 均值的闭式表达为参数的简单反正切函数；二阶矩的闭式表达由二重对数（dilogarithm）的实部给出。

Conclusion: 本文填补了ACG分布线性矩的显式表达空白，为物理等领域中需将角度视为实值相位的应用提供了解析工具。

Abstract: The polar-angle marginal of a centred bivariate Gaussian distribution, obtained after integrating out the radial coordinate, gives the two-dimensional angular central Gaussian (ACG) distribution of Tyler. While its trigonometric and vector-valued moments have been studied in detail, to our knowledge there are no explicit closed-form expressions for the \emph{linear} moments $\mathbf{E}[θ]$ and $\mathbf{E}[θ^{2}]$ on the natural domain $θ\in\left]-π/2,π/2\right[$. Here \textit{linear} refers to the ordinary moments $\intθ^{k}f(θ)\,dθ$ of the angle regarded as a real-valued variable, in contrast to the circular (trigonometric) moments $\mathbf{E}[e^{ikθ}]$ customary in directional statistics. We provide such expressions: the mean is a simple arctangent of the parameters, while the second moment is given by the real part of a dilogarithm. The derivation, based on a contour integration around the branch cut of $\arctan z$, is elementary. These quantities naturally arise in physics, where $θ$ is interpreted as a real-valued phase rather than a circular variable.

### [79] [Richardson-Gaudin states of non-zero seniority III: The Perfect-Pairing limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31582)
*Paul A. Johnson*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于完美配对态（perfect-pairing state）及其低能激发的简化参考态方法，在保持与Richardson-Gaudin态方法同等数值精度的前提下，显著降低了强关联电子（strongly correlated electrons）计算的计算成本，其二阶Epstein-Nesbet微扰修正（second-order Epstein-Nesbet perturbative corrections）在价电子处理上达到了与完全活性空间自洽场（complete active space self-consistent field, CASSCF）相当的质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强关联电子系统传统上采用基于未配对电子数分组的Slater行列式组态相互作用（configuration interaction）方法，但计算成本呈指数增长。此前系列工作表明，基于Richardson-Gaudin态的单参考方法可在多项式成本下获得类似质量的结果，但仍有进一步简化的空间。

Method: 该方法将Richardson-Gaudin态大幅简化为完美配对态作为参考态，并在此基础上构建其低能激发态（low-lying excitations）。然后对价电子施加二阶Epstein-Nesbet微扰修正（second-order Epstein-Nesbet perturbative corrections），以逼近完全活性空间自洽场的计算质量。

Result: 简化后的完美配对态及其激发态在计算上大幅简化，计算成本显著降低，同时数值精度没有损失。其中二阶Epstein-Nesbet微扰修正对价电子的处理质量与完全活性空间自洽场（CASSCF）相当。

Conclusion: 采用完美配对态作为参考态并结合低能激发的方案，在保持计算精度的前提下实现了对Richardson-Gaudin态方法的大幅简化，为强关联电子系统的低成本高精度计算提供了一条有效路径。

Abstract: Strongly correlated electrons can be treated with a configuration interaction of Slater determinants grouped by number of unpaired electrons with exponential cost. The first two papers in this series demonstrated that single reference methods built from Richardson-Gaudin states gave results of similar quality at polynomial cost. In this contribution, the states are simplified substantially yielding the perfect-pairing state as a reference along with its low-lying excitations. The states are much simpler, the computational cost is substantially reduced, and there is no sacrifice in numerical accuracy. Second-order Epstein-Nesbet perturbative corrections for the valence electrons are similar in quality to the complete active space self-consistent field.

### [80] [Using graph neural networks to predict many-body interactions in amorphous materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30822)
*Mehryar Jannesari Ghomsheh,Donald L. Koch,Sarah Hormozi*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文利用经典密度泛函理论（DFT）研究无溶剂聚合物接枝纳米粒子（PGNs）模型软玻璃，发现等变消息传递图神经网络（NequIP）能够以低四个数量级的计算成本学习该体系的高维势能面，并通过图神经网络驱动的蒙特卡洛模拟成功重现实验观测的平衡结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非晶态材料（amorphous materials）中多体相互作用（many-body interactions）通常主导其复杂行为，但由于计算效率的原因，常被简化为成对加和（pairwise additive）框架。本文旨在建立更高效且准确的方法来捕捉多体相互作用，并揭示其对软玻璃体系结构的影响。

Method: 采用经典密度泛函理论（classical density functional theory, DFT）对无溶剂聚合物接枝纳米粒子（polymer-grafted nanoparticles, PGNs）进行建模；利用等变消息传递图神经网络（equivariant message-passing graph neural network, NequIP）学习该体系的高维势能面（potential energy landscape）；通过系统分析图神经网络超参数，探讨相互作用的范围（range）、各向异性（anisotropy）和有效体阶（effective body order）；执行图神经网络驱动的蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟。

Result: NequIP以四个数量级更低的计算代价复现经典DFT能量；图神经网络驱动的蒙特卡洛模拟在平衡态下揭示出局部偏好的二十面体类似结构（icosahedral-like structures）；尽管网络仅在高能、非平衡构型（out-of-equilibrium configurations）上训练，却能成功恢复与实验一致的平衡结构。

Conclusion: 等变图神经网络能够高效且准确地学习多体相互作用主导的复杂势能面，并在仅基于非平衡数据训练的条件下再现实验观测的平衡结构，为软玻璃等非晶态材料的多体作用建模提供了有力工具。

Abstract: Many-body interactions govern the complex behavior of many amorphous materials, from metallic glasses to biological tissues, yet are often replaced by pairwise additive frameworks for computational efficiency. Here, we use classical density functional theory (DFT) to study a model soft glass of solvent-free polymer-grafted nanoparticles (PGNs), where the absence of solvent forces grafted chains to uniformly fill the interstitial space, generating strong angular-dependent many-body interactions between the cores. We show that NequIP, an equivariant message-passing graph neural network (GNN), learns the high-dimensional, rugged potential energy landscape of the system and reproduces classical DFT energies across a range of PGN design parameters at four orders of magnitude lower cost. Systematic analysis of GNN hyperparameters offers physical insights into the range, anisotropy, and effective body order of interactions. GNN-driven Monte Carlo simulations reveal locally favored icosahedral-like structures at equilibrium, and strikingly, recover equilibrium structures in agreement with experiments, despite the network being trained only on high-energy, out-of-equilibrium configurations.

### [81] [Nonlinear Schrodinger Equations for Dense Bose Fluid and He4 Film at Low Temperatures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30704)
*Vladimir I. Kruglov*

Main category: cond-mat.other

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于Hartree-Fock含时平均场理论（Hartree-Fock time-dependent mean-field theory），采用任意分子间相互作用势（arbitrary intermolecular interaction potential），推导广义的非线性薛定谔方程（nonlinear Schrödinger equation）。

Result: 得到了广义的非线性薛定谔方程，其系数经适当重新定义后可描述低温稠密玻色流体。推导出描述二流体流体动力学中超流氦组分的薛定谔型方程，给出速度场的量子修正。针对超流氦4薄膜，推导出低温下的非线性薛定谔方程，该方程导出低温基本激发的声子-旋子（phonon-roton）色散关系。

Conclusion: 所推导的广义非线性薛定谔方程框架统一了稀薄玻色气体、稠密玻色流体及超流氦4薄膜的描述，并通过量子修正和声子-旋子色散关系验证了模型在低温超流现象中的有效性。

Abstract: We have derived the nonlinear Schrodinger equation generalizing the Gross-Pitaevskii (GP) equa tion for dilute Bose gas. The derivation is based on the Hartree-Fock time-dependent mean-field theory with an arbitrary intermolecular interaction potential. It is shown that obtained nonlinear Schrodinger equation with appropriate redefinition of coefficients can be used for description of dense Bose fluid at low temperatures. We also present the Schrodinger type equation describing the superfluid component of helium in two fluid hydrodynamics. This approach leads to quantum correction for superfluid component of velocity in two fluid hydrodynamics. We also have derived the nonlinear Schrodinger equation for superfluid He4 film at low temperatures. It is shown that this Schrodinger type equation for superfluid He4 film leads to phonon-roton dispersion relation for elementary excitation at low temperatures.

Motivation: 控制金刚石中的氮掺杂是推进氮-空位（NV）中心器件发展的关键，因此需要探索有效的掺杂控制方法。

Method: 利用(001)取向衬底上的小丘结构实现高密度、对齐的NV中心原位生长；通过阴极发光（cathodoluminescence）和纳米二次离子质谱（nanoSIMS）表征氮掺入；利用NV退相干（decoherence）分析测量NV/替代氮(P1)比例。

Result: 小丘侧壁的氮掺入量比平面薄膜高出高达1000倍；小丘与堆垛层错（stacking faults）和刃型位错（edge-type dislocations）相关，而非衬底螺位错；四个小丘侧壁各承载一种独特的NV取向；NV/替代氮(P1)比例为1.7-2%，是典型(001)取向生长的4倍。

Conclusion: 自发形成的小丘可作为密集、对齐NV形成的天然实验室，激励对(001)金刚石中面依赖的氮掺入和NV择优取向进行系统性研究。

Abstract: Controlling nitrogen doping in diamond is key to advancing nitrogen-vacancy (NV) center devices. We harness the hillock, a typically undesirable surface feature, to incorporate high densities of grown-in, aligned NV-centers on a (001)-oriented substrate. Enhanced cathodoluminescence at hillock sidewalls is correlated via nanoSIMS to up to 1000x greater nitrogen incorporation compared to the planar film. We find that these hillocks are associated with stacking faults and edge-type dislocations, consistent with an origin in surface preparation rather than substrate screw dislocations. Yet, the growth is orderly enough that each of the four hillock sidewalls hosts a distinct NV orientation. A 1.7-2% grown-in NV/substitutional nitrogen (P1) ratio, 4x higher than typical (001)-oriented growth, is measured via NV decoherence analysis. By revealing that spontaneously formed hillocks act as natural laboratories for dense, aligned NV formation, this work motivates systematic investigation of facet-dependent nitrogen incorporation and preferential NV alignment in (001) diamond.

In this review article, we provide a comprehensive overview of RA-SHG studies across a broad range of condensed matter systems. Here, we demonstrate a scalable, generalized fabrication strategy that enables the formation of high-crystallinity oxide moire superlattices with clean, chemically bonded interfaces and precisely controlled twist angles down to nominal values of 0.1 degree, achieving sub-degree twist-angle accuracy across large contiguous lateral dimensions approaching the millimeter scale. Using NaNbO3 as a model system, we show that the resulting interlayer coupling drives pronounced structural reconstruction that modifies both the phase structure and ferroelectric domain configuration. Synchrotron-based X-ray 3D reciprocal space mapping reveals the emergence of a single-phase state in twisted bilayers, in contrast to the mixed-phase structure observed in single-layer membranes prior to twist assembly. The structural signatures are further consistent with gradual lattice rotation distributed along the thickness direction that may accommodate interfacial shear strain, distinct from reconstruction observed in van der Waals moire systems, which primarily occurs through in-plane stacking rearrangement. This collective lattice response is correlated with twist-dependent nanoscale electromechanical modulations observed by piezoresponse force microscopy. These results establish a scalable materials platform for oxide twistronics and open new pathways towards integrating twist-engineered complex oxides into practical, macroscale device architectures.

### [87] [Simulations of dislocation dynamics on an atomic lattice: the effect of collision rules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30682)
*Tom Hudson,Akaraphon Jantaraphum,Patrick van Meurs*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文研究一维周期格点上位错的随机动力学，通过数值模拟对比了有/无碰撞湮灭规则的两个离散模型，发现含湮灭的模型收敛到相应的偏微分方程（PDE），而无碰撞规则的模型则表现出不一致的收敛行为，强调了位错碰撞处理在离散位错动力学模型中的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解离散位错动力学（discrete dislocation dynamics）中位错碰撞机制对宏观密度演化行为的影响，探究离散模型是否以及如何收敛到连续偏微分方程描述。

Method: 在一维周期格点域（one-dimensional periodic lattice domain）上建立两种位错随机动力学模型：一种不含碰撞规则（without a collision rule），另一种在相反取向位错相遇时予以湮灭（annihilates colliding dislocations if they have opposite orientation）。通过一系列数值模拟（numerical simulations）考察随位错数增加时两类模型的渐近行为（asymptotic behaviour）。

Result: 含湮灭的离散模型趋于一个描述密度演化并包含湮灭项的偏微分方程（PDE）；无碰撞规则的模型未展示出一致的收敛行为——在某些参数下密度趋于保守型PDE，而在另一些参数下密度演化却遵循含湮灭的PDE。

Conclusion: 离散位错动力学模型中，位错碰撞的处理方式对模型的宏观收敛行为至关重要，需谨慎设计碰撞规则才能获得正确的连续极限描述。

Abstract: The stochastic dynamics of dislocations on a one-dimensional periodic lattice domain are considered. Two models are studied: one without a collision rule, and one which annihilates colliding dislocations if they have opposite orientation. The behaviour of both models is investigated by means of a series of numerical simulations exploring the asymptotic behaviour of these models as the number of dislocations increases. From these simulations, evidence is obtained that the discrete model with annihilation tends to a PDE for the dislocation density that accounts for annihilation. However, the discrete model without a collision rule does not appear to exhibit consistent convergence behaviour; instead, it appears that the expected PDE with conserved dislocation density appears in the limit for some parameters, but that for other parameters the density appears to follow to the evolution of the PDE with annihilation. These findings provide evidence that a careful treatment of dislocation collisions is important in discrete dislocation dynamics models.

Result: 在亚10纳米（sub-10 nm）超薄薄膜中，成功实现了低于100 mV电压下的稳健铁电操作（robust ferroelectric operation）。

Abstract: Scaling ferroelectrics to nanometer thicknesses remains a central challenge for low-power, nonvolatile electronics, as leakage currents increasingly dominate with reduced dimensions. Alkali-based, lead-free ferroelectrics offer an environmentally sustainable alternative to lead-based systems, yet their scaling is severely limited by leakage arising from volatile alkali constituents. Here, we show that this intrinsic limitation can be transformed into an advantageous degree of freedom through defect engineering. By precisely modulating alkali deficiency during thin-film synthesis, we engineer clustered defect complexes that function as deep trap states, strongly suppressing leakage and enabling robust ferroelectric operation in ultrathin films down to the sub-10 nm regime at voltages below 100 mV. Our results establish defect-enabled scaling as a viable pathway for advancing environmentally benign ferroelectrics toward ultra-low-power, non-volatile electronic technologies.

</details>


### [91] [Crystal Dislocations as Atomic Scale Ratchets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30764)
*Wu-Rong Jian,Yifan Wang,Wei Cai*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种原子尺度的几何起源机制，打破了晶体缺陷在外部应力下响应的对称性。分子动力学模拟显示，面心立方镍中带有原子级割阶（jog）的位错在相反方向的加载应力下表现出不对称迁移率，且反转加载方向会显著增大阻力。该不对称性源于原子位移矢量与割阶运动机制的二阶张量本征应变之间的非常规耦合。这一发现挑战了经典塑性变形理论，并对循环蠕变（cyclic creep）等疲劳现象具有直接意义，为缺陷工程提升抗疲劳性能开辟了新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在微观尺度下，实现响应不对称性（即整流效应）在工程设计和自然界中极为罕见且困难。传统晶体微力学模型默认应力响应是对称的——反向加载仅反转缺陷速度方向而不改变其大小。本文旨在探索是否存在一种原子尺度的、几何结构根源的机制，能够打破这种固有的应力响应对称性。

Method: 采用分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟方法，以面心立方（face-centered cubic, FCC）镍（nickel）为模型材料，研究含有原子级割阶（atomic-scale jogs）的位错在外加相反方向应力下的运动行为。

Result: 发现含有原子级割阶的位错在相反方向的外加应力下表现出不对称迁移率（asymmetric mobility）：反转加载方向导致显著增大的阻力（drag）。这种不对称性源自原子位移矢量（atomic displacement vector）与割阶运动机制的二阶张量本征应变（second-order tensorial eigenstrain）之间的非常规耦合（unconventional coupling）。

Conclusion: 由于割阶是塑性变形中普遍存在的结构，该发现挑战了经典塑性变形机制的描述，对循环蠕变等疲劳现象具有直接意义，并为通过缺陷工程（defect engineering）增强抗疲劳性能（fatigue resistance）开辟了新的路径。

Abstract: The symmetry of a system's response to external stimuli is a fundamental concept in physics and materials science. At the microscopic scale, breaking this symmetry to achieve a rectified response is exceptionally difficult to engineer and remains rare in nature. Conventional micromechanics models of crystalline solids assume a symmetric response to applied stress, where reversing the load simply inverts the direction of defect velocity without altering its magnitude. In this work, we report an atomic-scale, geometry-rooted mechanism that breaks this symmetry. Molecular dynamics simulations of face-centered cubic nickel reveal that dislocations containing atomic-scale jogs exhibit asymmetric mobility under opposite applied stresses, reversing the loading direction triggers significantly higher drag. This asymmetry arises from an unconventional coupling between an atomic displacement vector and the second-order tensorial eigenstrain of the jog motion mechanism. Because jogs are ubiquitous structures in plastic deformation, this discovery challenges classical descriptions of plastic deformation mechanisms, with direct implications to cyclic creep, and opens new pathways for defect engineering to enhance fatigue resistance.

### [92] [Saturated and Anisotropic Magnetostriction in an Altermagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30773)

Method: 采用高质量MnTe单晶进行磁致伸缩测量，并结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）分析弹性应变与奈尔序参量（Néel order parameter）之间的耦合机制。

Conclusion: 这些发现打破了关于反铁磁磁致伸缩（antiferromagnetic magnetostriction）的传统认知，表明交替磁体（altermagnet）中可存在易饱和的磁致伸缩效应，为磁-力耦合研究提供了新方向。

Abstract: Magnetostriction, a fundamental phenomenon bridging magnetism and mechanics, has enabled a broad spectrum of applications. For almost two centuries, it has been mainly investigated for ferromagnets. Regarding the magnetostriction of antiferromagnets (AFMs), limitedly known examples for both conventional collinear AFMs and noncollinear AFMs predominantly exhibit non-saturating magnetic-field dependence. Herein, we report an easily saturated magnetostriction effect in a prototypical altermagnet - MnTe, which is an emerging class of collinear AFMs with special crystal symmetries. For high-quality MnTe single crystals, the magnetostriction saturates under a moderate field of ~0.7 T with an intriguing two-fold-symmetry anisotropy. First-principles calculations reveal that the saturated and anisotropic magnetostriction originates from symmetry-allowed coupling between elastic strain and its Néel order parameter. Method: 建立了反铁磁系统中LPR磁化的对称性约束规则，并通过实时含时密度泛函理论（real-time time-dependent density functional theory, rt-TDDFT）计算进行验证。

Abstract: Ultrafast light-driven magnetization, a frontier in quantum magneto-optics, has traditionally relied on circularly polarized lasers to provide external angular momentum. Here, we establish the symmetry-constrained rule for LPR magnetization in antiferromagnetic systems. Strikingly, laser excitation induces real-space demagnetization, rotation, and oscillation of atomic spins in spin-spiral monolayer NiI$_2$, whereas rotation is largely suppressed in conventional collinear antiferromagnets. ### [94] [Clustering in atom probe tomography data: coordination number metric, percolation-based parameter scaling, and size effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31107)
*Mykola Lazarev,John Banhart*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于配位数（coordination-number）度量的原子探针层析成像（APT）数据分析方法，通过标度聚类性质至逾渗阈值（percolation threshold）构造自相似变量（self-similar variable），该变量对度量和聚类参数几乎不变，可用于跨方法最优参数传递，并在考虑APT重构伪影的模拟中表现优于传统溶质密度方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原子探针层析成像（APT）中识别新相纳米级核的能力受限于聚类算法对用户自定义控制参数的敏感性，且传统方法仅依赖欧几里得距离度量（Euclidean distance metric）并只考虑溶质原子，丢弃了包含大部分空间信息的溶剂原子。

Method: 引入基于成分（composition）的配位数度量（coordination-number metric）并应用于高阶聚类（higher-order clustering）；使用多种度量研究典型APT结构中的逾渗（percolation）行为；将聚类性质标度至相应逾渗阈值（percolation threshold），构造对度量、聚类参数和结构无序几乎不变的、描述聚类的自相似变量（self-similar variable）。

Result: 自相似变量提供了对聚类的恰当描述，并实现了不同聚类方法之间最优参数的正式传递；基于配位数的方法有效补偿了不均匀膨胀（heterogeneous dilations），在包含有限空间分辨率、探测效率及其他APT重构伪影（reconstruction artifacts）的模拟中，所有测试场景下均优于基于溶质密度的方法。

Conclusion: 基于配位数度量的标度方法能够克服传统APT聚类分析对参数敏感性的局限，通过自相似变量实现跨方法最优参数传递，并在存在重构伪影时表现出更强的鲁棒性和更优性能。

Abstract: The ability to identify nanometer-scale nuclei of new phases in atom probe tomography (APT) is often limited by the sensitivity of clustering algorithms to user-defined control parameters. Conventional approaches typically rely on the Euclidean distance metric and consider only solute atoms, thereby discarding the solvent atoms that contain most of the spatial information. Here, we introduce a coordination-number metric based on the composition and apply it to higher-order clustering. Using various metrics, we investigate percolation in typical APT structures. By scaling clustering properties to the corresponding percolation thresholds, we define a self-similar variable that is almost invariant with respect to metrics, clustering parameters, and structural disorder. This variable provides a relevant description of clustering and enables the formal transfer of optimal parameters between clustering methods. We also study the characteristic clustering behavior in small precipitates and quantify how the precipitate-matrix interface alters the composition spectrum and broadens the clustering curve. Finally, using simulations that incorporate finite spatial resolution, detection efficiency, and other APT reconstruction artifacts, we show that the approach based on coordination numbers effectively compensates for heterogeneous dilations and outperforms solute-density-based methods in all tested scenarios.

Conclusion: 该ML参数化的KMC模拟框架能够在保持原子扩散动力学高保真描述的同时，通过自演进学习机制提升计算效率，为薄膜生长的大规模原子级模拟提供了有效工具，且模拟结果与理论和实验吻合良好。

Abstract: We present a kinetic Monte Carlo (KMC) simulation framework parameterized by automatically sampling machine-learning (ML) for modeling thin-film growth atom by atom. Given an interatomic potential energy function, the KMC algorithm builds an ML-based regression model for rate parameters on runtime, being trained on the local atomic environments encountered during the system evolution. New environments are continuously added to the training set in a self-evolving manner at points where the ML model estimates high uncertainty. As the simulation progresses, the ML model gains confidence, and the quick estimation of rates increasingly overtakes the relatively-expensive nudged elastic band calculations, promoting computational efficiency while retaining high fidelity description of the atomic diffusion kinetics. As a test case, we simulate the sub-monolayer growth of Ag on Ag {111}, where we demonstrate adatom islands forming in shapes and densities in accordance with the underlying atomistic interaction model, the theoretical framework, and available experimental results related to thin-film nucleation and growth.

### [96] [Topological Interstitial-Electron Conductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31195)
*Tingli He,Xiaoming Zhang,Chaoxi Cui,Yilin Han,Yang Wang,Wei Jiang,Zhi-Ming Yu,Yugui Yao*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一类新型电子导体——拓扑间隙电子导体（TIECs），通过低周期性势垒的间隙电子在电场作用下产生持久电流，并在材料边界出现拓扑表面态，从而扩展了电子导体的分类并建立了低功耗电子器件的新材料平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固体中的电子输运主要源于两种机制：金属中的自由体电子和拓扑绝缘体中的无带隙边界态。本文旨在探索第三种电子输运机制，即电化物（electrides）中由间隙电子（interstitial electrons, IEs）介导的新型导电行为。

Method: 通过理论提出拓扑间隙电子导体（topological interstitial-electron conductors, TIECs）概念，并识别出一类实际可行的交错磁电化物（altermagnetic electrides）$A_5X_3$（$A$ = Ca, Sr, Ba, Yb; $X$ = As, Sb）作为TIECs候选材料，计算其沿空隙通道的周期性势垒高度。

Result: $A_5X_3$材料中沿空隙通道的间隙电子周期性势垒极低，范围为每化学式单元13.43至67.96 meV。当间隙电子沿通道做周期运动时，在垂直于通道方向边界出现拓扑表面态（topological surface states），并持续跨越体块带隙移动。

Conclusion: 本研究扩展了电子导体的分类，揭示了电化物中未被探索的输运性质，并为低功耗电子器件建立了新的材料平台。

Abstract: Electron transport in solids arises primarily from two mechanisms: freely moving bulk electrons in metals, and gapless boundary states in topological insulators. Here, we report a new mechanism discovered in electrides. The topological interstitial-electron conductors (TIECs) proposed here are insulating electrides, but host interstitial electrons (IEs) distributed within crystal voids that traverse the entire unit cell. Without being tightly bound to real ions, the IEs generally experience low periodic potential barrier along the void channels. As a consequence, by applying a weak electric field sufficient to overcome the IE barriers but far below the system's dielectric breakdown threshold, one can expect that the TIECs would generate a persistent current contributed by the IEs and propagating along the void channels. We identify a family of realistic altermagnetic electrides, $A_5X_3$ ($A$ = Ca, Sr, Ba, Yb; $X$ = As, Sb), as TIECs. Remarkably, for $A_5X_3$ materials, the periodic potential barrier of the IEs along the void channels are ultralow, ranging from 13.43 to 67.96 meV per formula unit. This renders our proposal readily accessible to experimental verification. We further demonstrate that when the IEs of $A_5X_3$ undergo periodic motion along the channels, topological surface states will emerge at the boundary perpendicular to the channel direction, and continuously move across the bulk band gap. This pumping-like behaviour not only corroborates the topological nature of TIECs, but also rationalizes the finite-electric-field induced electronic transport within the band theory. Our findings expand the classification of electronic conductors, uncover unexplored transport properties of electrides, and establish a new material platform for low-power electronic devices.

Result: 室温下磁化沿面内两个<111>体易轴方向排列，存在180°、71°和109°的Neel型畴壁；低于Verwey转变温度后，磁化方向转变为面内[100]和[001]方向，分别对应单斜c轴面内和c轴倾斜出面的区域，但磁化始终保持在表面平面内，未检测到面外分量。

Conclusion: Fe₃O₄(110)表面在Verwey转变前后均呈现面内磁化结构，磁化方向的转变可归因于单斜c轴取向的变化，且表面磁化严格限制在面内。

Abstract: We have studied the (110) surface of Fe$_3$O$_4$ single crystals by means of spin-polarized low-energy electron microscopy (SPLEEM). After preparation by sputtering and annealing a well defined reconstructed surface was achieved, composed of rows aligned in the [010] direction. By acquiring SPLEEM images along different spin directions the vector magnetization was mapped on the surface, both at room temperature and at a temperature well below the Verwey transition. At room temperature, domains were observed with their magnetization aligned along the two <111> bulk easy axes which are in the (110) surface plane. They presented 180$^\circ$, 71$^\circ$ and 109$^\circ$ Néel-type domain walls. Below the Verwey transition, the magnetization directions changed to regions where the magnetization was oriented along the in-plane [100] and [001] directions. Those observations can be interpreted as the presence of magnetized regions on the surface where the monoclinic $c$ axis is in-plane in the former, and regions where the $c$ is out-of-plane in an oblique direction in the latter. However, the magnetization was at all times within the surface plane, with no out-of-plane component detected.

</details>


### [99] [A Practical Guide for Diagnosing Imaginary Phonon Modes in Metal--Organic Frameworks: The Case of MOF-5](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31303)
*Julia Santana-Andreo,Caterina Cocchi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文以MOF-5为代表案例，建立了一套有限位移有限位移（finite-displacement）工作流，用于识别和排除计算金属-有机框架（metal–organic frameworks, MOFs）声子谱中虚频的数值噪声源，并提供了分析剩余真实虚频以寻找低能局域极小值的策略，从而为柔性多孔框架的动力学稳定性评估提供了鲁棒、可迁移的方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 计算预测的MOF结构需要通过动力学稳定性评估来区分合成上可行的结构与不稳定的结构，但基于第一性原理（first-principles）的声子计算面临挑战：MOF的大尺寸柔性晶胞和软集体模式使得振动谱对数值设置高度敏感。

Method: 以MOF-5为代表性案例，建立有限位移工作流，系统考察数值力收敛阈值（force convergence thresholds）、实空间网格分辨率（real-space grid resolutions）、对称性标准化协议（symmetry-standardization protocols）以及替代晶胞表示（alternative unit-cell representations）对晶格稳定性预测的定性影响。排除数值噪声后，通过模式映射（mode mapping）或随机蒙特卡洛对称性破缺畸变（stochastic Monte Carlo symmetry-breaking distortions）分析剩余虚频，以定位低能局域极小值。

Result: 数值设置（如力收敛阈值、网格分辨率、对称性处理及晶胞表示）可以定性地、虚假地改变预测的晶格稳定性。通过所建立的工作流可以可靠地排除这些数值噪声源，并区分真实的动力学不稳定性。

Conclusion: 该工作流为柔性多孔框架的动力学稳定性和晶格振动评估提供了一种鲁棒且可转移的策略，有助于提升计算预测MOF结构的可靠性。

Abstract: Assessing the dynamical stability of computationally predicted metal--organic frameworks (MOFs) is essential to distinguish synthetically feasible structures from dynamically unstable ones. However, reliable first-principles phonon calculations on these systems remain challenging: their large, flexible unit cells and soft collective modes make the vibrational spectrum highly sensitive to the numerical settings. Using MOF-5 as a representative case study, we establish a finite-displacement workflow to identify and isolate the origins of imaginary phonon modes. We demonstrate how numerical force convergence thresholds, real-space grid resolutions, symmetry-standardization protocols, and alternative unit-cell representations can qualitatively and spuriously alter the predicted lattice stability. Once numerical noise is confidently excluded, the remaining imaginary modes can be analyzed through mode mapping or stochastic Monte Carlo symmetry-breaking distortions to locate lower-energy local minima. This protocol provides a robust, transferable strategy for the reliable assessment of dynamical stability and lattice vibrations in flexible porous frameworks.

### [100] [Direct Observation of Chemical Short-Range Order in CoCrNi Alloy Using Neutron Diffraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31395)
*Vinícius P. Bacurau,Camilo Salvador,Guilherme C. Stumpfa,Angelo F. Andreolli,Caroline B. Stocoa,Eric M. Mazzer,Lewis Owen,Yifan Cao,Rodrigo Freitas,Daniel Miracle,Francisco G. Coury*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过中子衍射实验证实等原子比CoCrNi合金中存在化学短程序（CSRO），表现为Q=1.85 Å⁻¹处的弥散衍射峰，该峰强度在热力学有利条件（如748 K长时间时效或798 K短时间时效）下增强。通过积分弥散散射强度量化有序度，发现气雾化样品（CSRO含量最低）仍表现出最高CSRO样品（748 K时效240 h）约70%的有序水平。预测性原子模拟再现了弥散峰的存在与位置，二维快速傅里叶变换（FT-2D）分析表明<001>晶带轴内(1 1/2 0)反射源于类D022、Pt₂Mo和D1a构型相关的结构投影。互补的小角中子散射（SANS）测量识别出半径约11 Å、厚度约1 Å的富Ni盘状区域，与纳米级CSRO特征尺度一致。这些发现表明CSRO是CoCrNi体系的内禀且能量上有利的特征，即使在快速凝固条件下仍保持稳定，并可通过低温时效进一步增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验证实等原子比CoCrNi合金中化学短程序（CSRO）的存在，并探明其结构特征与稳定性，从而为理解多主元合金（MPEAs）中的局部有序现象提供实验与计算相结合的研究框架。

Method: 采用中子衍射（neutron diffraction）识别CSRO的弥散衍射峰；通过积分弥散散射强度量化有序度；结合预测性原子模拟（predictive atomistic simulations）和二维快速傅里叶变换（FT-2D）分析衍射起源；并利用互补的小角中子散射（SANS）测量纳米尺度CSRO区域。

Result: CSRO特征弥散峰位于Q=1.85 Å⁻¹，该峰强度在热力学有利条件（如748 K时效100–240 h或798 K时效24 h）下增强。气雾化样品（CSRO最少）仍具有最高CSRO样品约70%的有序水平。模拟重现了弥散峰；FT-2D分析表明(1 1/2 0)反射来源于类D022、Pt₂Mo和D1a构型；SANS识别出半径~11 Å、厚度~1 Å的富Ni盘状纳米域。

Conclusion: CSRO是CoCrNi体系的内禀且能量上有利的特征，在快速凝固下仍稳定，并可被低温时效进一步增强。中子衍射与原子模拟的联合使用为探测多主元合金（MPEAs）中的局部有序现象提供了有效框架。

Abstract: This study provides experimental evidence of chemical short-range order (CSRO) in the equiatomic CoCrNi alloy, identified through neutron diffraction. The phenomenon manifests as a distinct diffuse peak at Q = 1.85 A-1, the intensity increases under thermodynamically favorable conditions for CSRO development such as prolonged aging (100 h and 240 h) at 748 K or shorter aging (24 h) at slightly higher temperature (798 K). The degree of ordering was measured by integrating the diffuse scattering intensity, revealing that the gas-atomized sample, i.e. the sample with the least amount of CSRO, still displays approximately 70% of the CSRO level observed in the sample subsequently aged for 240 h at 748 K, i.e. the sample with the highest amount of CSRO produced in this study. Predictive atomistic simulations reproduced both the presence and position of the diffuse peak, while two-dimensional fast Fourier transform (FT-2D) analyses indicated that reflections at (1 1/2 0) within the <001> zone axis originate from some structural projections associated with like D022, Pt2Mo and D1a motifs. Complementary small-angle neutron scattering (SANS) measurements identified Ni-rich, disk-shaped domains with radii of approximately 11 A and thicknesses of about 1 A, consistent with nanoscale CSRO characteristic length scale. These findings demonstrate that CSRO is an intrinsic and energetically favorable feature of the CoCrNi system, remaining stable even under rapid solidification and further enhanced by low-temperature aging. Combined use of neutron diffraction and atomistic modeling provides a framework for probing local ordering phenomena in multi-principal element alloys (MPEAs).

### [101] [Crystallisation kinetics of supercooled liquid palladium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31399)
*Zuzanna Kostera,Przemyslaw Dziegielewski,Konstantinos Georgarakis,Oleksii I. Liubchenko,Adam Olczak,Ryszard Sobierajski,Klaus Sokolowski-Tinten,Peihao Sun,Robert W. E. van de Kruijs,Peter Zalden,Jerzy Antonowicz*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究利用经典分子动力学（MD）模拟研究了过冷液态钯（Pd）的结晶动力学，并与快速淬火Pd薄膜的时间分辨X射线衍射测量结果相关联。模拟确定了晶体成核与生长速率，构建了时间-温度-转变（TTT）图，并揭示了均相成核（homogeneous nucleation）主导了实验薄膜中可达到的过冷度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将过冷液态金属的结晶动力学模拟与时间分辨X射线衍射实验测量结果直接关联，以验证模拟方法的可靠性，并澄清在快速淬火Pd薄膜中控制过冷度的成核机制（均相 vs. 异相成核）。

Method: 采用经典分子动力学（molecular dynamics, MD）模拟，在700–1150 K（0.38–0.65 Tm）温度范围内分析微观结构演化，以确定晶体成核与生长速率；通过原子均方位移（mean-squared displacement）获得自扩散系数；基于多次统计独立模拟构建时间-温度-转变（time-temperature-transformation, TTT）图。

Result: 自扩散系数遵循Arrhenius行为，活化能为467(6) meV/atom；稳态均相成核速率在约0.5 Tm处达到最大值约4×10^35 m⁻³ s⁻¹；晶体生长速度为米/秒量级，温度依赖性符合扩散限制的Wilson-Frenkel动力学；TTT曲线鼻点位于约0.5 Tm和100 ps处，对应的临界冷却速率约为10^13 K s⁻¹。

Conclusion: 模拟结果成功再现了实验观测到的结晶起始时间与温度，表明均相成核（homogeneous nucleation）而非异相成核（heterogeneous nucleation）主导了快速淬火Pd薄膜中可达到的过冷度。

Abstract: In this study, we employ classical molecular dynamics (MD) simulations to investigate the crystallisation kinetics of supercooled liquid palladium and relate the results to time-resolved X-ray diffraction measurements on rapidly quenched Pd thin films. Crystal nucleation and growth rates are determined over the temperature range $700$--$1150~\mathrm{K}$ ($0.38$--$0.65 T_{\mathrm{m}}$) by analysing the evolution of the microstructure during the liquid-to-crystal transition. The self-diffusion coefficient of Pd, obtained from the atomic mean-squared displacement, follows Arrhenius behaviour over the investigated temperature range, with an activation energy of $467(6)~\mathrm{meV/atom}$, consistent with available data for supercooled liquid metals. The steady-state homogeneous nucleation rate exhibits a maximum of approximately $4 \times 10^{35}~\mathrm{m^{-3} s^{-1}}$ near $0.5 T_{\mathrm{m}}$. Crystal growth occurs at velocities of the order of metres per second, with a temperature dependence consistent with diffusion-limited Wilson-Frenkel kinetics rather than the collision-limited regime. Based on multiple statistically independent simulations, a time-temperature-transformation (TTT) diagram for crystallisation onset is constructed. The TTT curve exhibits a nose near $0.5 T_{\mathrm{m}}$ and $100~\mathrm{ps}$, corresponding to a critical cooling rate for vitrification on the order of $10^{13}~\mathrm{K s^{-1}}.$ The simulations reproduce the crystallisation onset time and temperature observed in time-resolved X-ray diffraction experiments on optically molten Pd thin films quenched at $5 \times 10^{11}~\mathrm{K s^{-1}}.$ These results indicate that homogeneous, rather than heterogeneous, nucleation governs the achievable supercooling in the experimentally studied films.

Conclusion: 应变工程（strain engineering）是调控s-C₃N₆能带边沿对齐、载流子动力学和光学跃迁的有效策略，凸显了该材料在稳定的二维光催化水分解中的应用潜力。

However, its conduction-band minimum lies below the hydrogen reduction potential, preventing spontaneous hydrogen evolution. To overcome this limitation, we employ biaxial and uniaxial strains (-10% to +10%) to modulate its electronic structure. We find that compressive biaxial strains of -8% and -10% uniquely tune the band edges to straddle the redox potentials, enabling spontaneous overall water splitting. Crucially, these photocatalytically active states remain mechanically and thermally stable. Optical properties calculations show the fundamental gap in both pristine and strained structures is optically dark, with the primary absorption peak in the UV region. Furthermore, a strain-induced mobility mismatch between electrons and holes facilitates efficient charge separation. However, thermodynamic modeling of surface kinetics reveals that the s-C$_3$N$_6$ surface binds intermediates strongly, necessitating a co-catalyst to overcome kinetic barriers. Our results establish strain engineering as an effective strategy to tailor band-edge alignment, carrier dynamics, and optical transitions in s-C$_3$N$_6$, highlighting its potential for stable 2D photocatalytic water splitting.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 成功推导出一组耦合电子-声子-磁子动力学方程，该方程组可从第一性原理求解；实现了对相干（coherent）与非相干（incoherent）磁动力学在统一框架下的处理。

Conclusion: 该框架为从第一性原理理解超快磁动力学和退磁过程铺平了道路，有望为周期性体系中的飞秒磁学提供真正可预测的理论工具。

Abstract: This work introduces a theoretical framework based on the Kadanoff-Baym equations in spinor space to study ultrafast magnetization dynamics in itinerant ferromagnetic systems from first principles. By incorporating spin-orbit coupling into the ab initio Hamiltonian and generalizing the self-energies to include terms beyond the charge sector, I derive scattering integrals within the Markov approximation and quasiparticle renormalizations for electrons and phonons in the presence of spin-dependent effective interactions within a many-body perturbation theory approach. I explicitly discuss how magnons emerge in this framework, and derive, through suitable approximations, a close and tractable set of equations for coupled electron,phonon and magnon dynamics that can be solved from first principles. This approach allows to treat coherent and incoherent magnetic dynamics on an equal footing, paving the way for a first principles understanding of ultrafast magnetic dynamics and demagnetization, and opening to a truly predictive theory of femtomagnetism in periodic systems.

Abstract: The targeted discovery of inorganic materials remains challenging due to the vastness of compositional design spaces and the high cost of exhaustive screening. ### [105] [Multiplet-Selective Photoelectron Diffraction from an Altermagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31531)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直接探测交变磁序（altermagnetic order）的实空间（real-space）手段仍然稀缺，现有方法难以有效分辨交变磁畴（altermagnetic domains）。因此需要发展一种能够在实空间层面区分交变磁畴的实验方法。

Method: 采用多峰选择光电子衍射（multiplet-selective photoelectron diffraction, PED）方法，利用过渡金属核心能级多重峰（core-level multiplet）中不同区域作为不同的光电子发射源波（photoemission source waves）。对金属交变磁候选材料CrSb进行多重散射计算（multiple-scattering calculations），分析Cr 3p多峰中主要具有Y₁⁺¹和Y₁⁻¹特征的分量所产生的衍射不对称性（diffraction asymmetries），并考察圆偏振（circularly polarized）和线偏振（linearly polarized）光的影响。

Result: 选定的Cr 3p多峰特征（具有Y₁⁺¹和Y₁⁻¹主导特征）能够产生对交变磁畴敏感的稳健衍射不对称性。圆偏振光和线偏振光均可用于实现该效应，通过合适的磁畴组合、光偏振态以及多峰能窗选择，可以有效抑制非磁性衍射背景（nonmagnetic diffraction backgrounds）。

Conclusion: 提出的多峰选择光电子衍射方法可在标准动量分辨光电子能谱（momentum-resolved photoemission）设备上实现，无需专用仪器。该方法确立了核心能级光电子衍射（core-level PED）作为交变磁体磁畴分辨研究（domain-resolved studies）的实用途径。

Abstract: Direct real-space probes of altermagnetic order remain scarce. Here we introduce multiplet-selective photoelectron diffraction (PED), a methodology in which different regions of a transition-metal core-level multiplet act as distinct photoemission source waves. Using multiple-scattering calculations for the metallic altermagnet candidate CrSb, we show that selected Cr $3p$ multiplet features with predominantly $Y_1^{+1}$ and $Y_1^{-1}$ character generate robust diffraction asymmetries sensitive to altermagnetic domains. We demonstrate that both circularly and linearly polarized light provide access to the effect, while suitable combinations of domains, light polarizations, and multiplet-energy windows suppress nonmagnetic diffraction backgrounds. The proposed approach can be implemented using standard momentum-resolved photoemission instrumentation and establishes core-level PED as a practical route toward domain-resolved studies of altermagnets.

</details>

### [106] [Topological Phenomena Protected by Diabolical Textures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30421)
*Sayantan Mandal,Neelima Pulletikurty,Abhishodh Prakash*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一类由参数化量子态族（如电荷泵）的绝热空间嵌入所产生的新型拓扑现象——"diabolical textures"，并展示了它们如何导致不同的能隙态、陷阱标度临界点以及不必要的临界曲面，同时基于Kitaev的Ω谱猜想给出了系统分类框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非均匀系统中由空间嵌入参数化量子态族所引发的新型拓扑现象，揭示其临界行为与分类方法。

Method: 通过非相互作用费米子（non-interacting fermions）的微观模型实现空间嵌入的Thouless泵，结合Kitaev的Ω谱猜想（Kitaev's Ω spectrum conjecture）构建系统分类框架。

Result: 每个拓扑不同的"diabolical textures"类别产生不同的能隙态（gapped states），并由"陷阱标度"临界点（"trap-scaling" critical points）分隔；当纹理在空间中变化足够快时，临界线突然终止，产生"不必要的临界"曲面（"unnecessary critical" surface）；通过相图分析验证了该体系在临界区域附近对任意微扰（包括相互作用）的稳定性。

Conclusion: 对于任意空间维度和全局对称性的系统，可借助Kitaev的Ω谱猜想对diabolical textures进行系统分类，揭示了一类新的拓扑相及其临界行为。

Abstract: We present a new class of topological phenomena in inhomogeneous systems arising from the adiabatic spatial embedding of parametrized families of quantum states such as charge pumps and their generalizations. We demonstrate that each topologically distinct class of these "diabolical textures" gives rise to distinct gapped states that are separated by "trap-scaling" critical points. When the texture varies sufficiently rapidly in space, the critical line terminates abruptly, producing an "unnecessary critical" surface. We demonstrate our results using a microscopic model of non-interacting fermions with a spatially embedded Thouless pump. We study its phase diagram comprehensively and establish its stability to arbitrary perturbations, including interactions, in the vicinity of the critical regions. For systems in arbitrary spatial dimensions and global symmetries, we present a framework to systematically classify diabolical textures using Kitaev's $Ω$ spectrum conjecture.

</details>


### [107] [Non-Perturbative Renormalization Group for Ising-Nematic Criticality: A Closed-Form Nonlocal Ansatz](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30715)
*Hyeon Jung Kim,Kyoung-Min Kim,Ki-Seok Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文对二维金属Ising-nematic量子临界点（metallic Ising-nematic quantum critical point）进行了非微扰重整化群分析，在三圈图（three-loop）截断下发现自洽的临界指数解不存在，并推测四圈图（four-loop）的玻色子自能交叉拓扑结构是恰好边缘的（exactly marginal），能恢复多扇区自洽性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维金属量子临界问题是一个长期悬而未决的难题，被认为对理解强关联电子系统中普遍存在的非费米液体行为（non-Fermi liquid behavior）至关重要。本文旨在通过非微扰方法自洽地确定临界指数（critical exponent），而非将其作为固定唯象参数处理。

Method: 采用非微扰重整化群（renormalization group, RG）分析，直接围绕本质非局域的远红外（infrared, IR）玻色子传播子构建低能补丁场论（patch field theory），并在高度各向异性的标度维度（$[k_0]=a+1$, $[k_x]=2$, $[k_y]=1$）下进行多圈计算，评估费米子自能、Yukawa顶点及玻色子反项（counter-term）的对数修正。

Result: 在两圈图（two-loop）水平，由于运动学极点构型，所有图贡献为零；三圈图计算揭示扇区之间存在深刻的结构不对称性：费米子自能和Yukawa顶点获得非零对数修正，而玻色子反项严格为零。由此导致在三圈截断内无法找到自洽的相交不动点（intersecting fixed-point）解，未能复现量子蒙特卡洛（quantum Monte Carlo, QMC）模拟中观测到的物理值 $a \approx 1.85$。

Conclusion: 作者推测四圈图的玻色子自能交叉连接拓扑结构是恰好边缘的，能够提供恢复多扇区自洽性所需的最小平移玻色子反项。该框架建立了严格的多圈匹配方案（multi-loop matching scheme），用以唯一确定临界指数，并揭示了场反常维度（field anomalous dimensions）的稳定相空间。

Abstract: The two-dimensional metallic quantum critical problem is a long-standing puzzle that is widely believed to hold the key to resolving ubiquitous non-Fermi liquid behavior in strongly correlated electronic systems. In this study, we present a non-perturbative renormalization group (RG) analysis of the metallic Ising-nematic quantum critical point in two dimensions, formulated directly around an intrinsically nonlocal infrared (IR) boson propagator. Rather than treating the anomalous dynamical critical exponent $a$ as a fixed phenomenological parameter, we regard it as an intrinsic component of the fixed-point data to be determined from the internal consistency of the low-energy patch field theory under highly anisotropic scaling dimensions ($[k_0]=a+1$, $[k_x]=2$, $[k_y]=1$). While the leading two-loop diagrammatics vanish identically due to kinematic pole configurations, our three-loop evaluation reveals a profound structural asymmetry between the sectors: the fermion self-energy and Yukawa vertex receive non-vanishing logarithmic corrections, whereas the corresponding bosonic counter-term remains strictly zero. Consequently, we find that no self-consistent, intersecting fixed-point solution for the exponent $a$ exists within the three-loop truncation, failing to reproduce the physical value of $a \approx 1.85$ observed in quantum Monte Carlo simulations. We conjecture that the cross-linked topology of the four-loop boson self-energy diagrams is exactly marginal and yields the minimal, mandatory bosonic counter-term required to restore multi-sector self-consistency. Our framework establishes a rigid multi-loop matching scheme necessary to uniquely pin down the critical exponent, and uncovers a stable phase space for field anomalous dimensions.

</details>


### [108] [Migdal-Eliashberg and SUS-$Y^2$-SYK](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31540)
*D. V. Khveshchenko*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文分析了强声子型费米子-玻色子耦合问题中的若干细微议题，重点考察了Migdal-Eliashberg近似在Schwinger-Dyson间隙方程中的适用性，并通过Yukawa-Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev模型的（非）超对称变体对已有见解进行了评估，同时点评了其中费米子配对的（伪）全息方面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决长期存在的强声子型费米子-玻色子耦合（strong phonon-like fermion-boson coupling）问题中的若干微妙之处，并评估传统Migdal-Eliashberg近似（Migdal-Eliashberg approximation）在相关Schwinger-Dyson间隙方程（Schwinger-Dyson gap equation）及其解中的有效性。

Method: 通过对比Yukawa-Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev模型（Yukawa-Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev model）的各种（非）超对称变体，对先前在Migdal-Eliashberg近似下获得的见解进行检验。

Result: 对传统Migdal-Eliashberg近似的适用性和局限性提供了新的评估视角；揭示了强耦合体系中费米子配对可能与先前理解存在差异。

Conclusion: 强声子型费米子-玻色子耦合问题的已有理解需要结合（非）超对称模型进行重新审视；费米子配对中涉及的（伪）全息方面也值得进一步讨论。

Abstract: This note addresses a number of subtle issues pertaining to the long-standing problem of strong phonon-like fermion-boson coupling. Among the central topics are the customary Migdal-Eliashberg approximation in the pertinent Schwinger-Dyson gap equation and its solutions. The previously gained insight is assessed by contrasting it against the various (non-)supersymmetric variants of the Yukawa-Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev model. Also, some previously discussed (pseudo-)holographic aspects of fermion pairing in such models are commented upon.

### [109] [Twin Phases: Phase Transitions Without Hidden Symmetry Breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31601)
*Alison Warman,Yuhan Gai,Sakura Schafer-Nameki*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文引入了“孪生相（twin phases）”概念，指代同一广义对称荷（generalized charge）下不同有序参量（order parameter）所对应的不等价相；指出这类相之间的稳定直接相变并非自发对称破缺（spontaneous-symmetry-breaking）相变，即便在对初始对称性进行部分规范（gauging）后依然如此；并通过1+1维反常有限群对称性（anomalous finite group symmetry）实例展示了这种内在超越朗道（intrinsically beyond Landau）的相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超越朗道范式（Landau paradigm），寻找不存在隐藏对称性破缺（hidden symmetry breaking）的新型相变机制。

Method: 定义孪生相（twin phases）为在对称性 $\mathcal{S}$ 下具有相同广义荷（generalized charge）的不同不等价相；通过分析其相变性质，证明稳定直接相变不涉及自发对称破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking）；并以1+1维反常有限群对称性（anomalous finite group symmetry）为具体算例进行说明。

Result: 孪生相之间的直接相变不伴随自发对称性破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking），且在对初始对称性进行部分规范（gauging）后这一性质依然保持；揭示了内在超越朗道（intrinsically beyond Landau）的相变类型。

Conclusion: 孪生相（twin phases）概念为描述无隐藏对称性破缺（hidden symmetry breaking）的相变提供了新的理论框架，拓展了对相变分类的理解。

Abstract: We introduce the concept of twin phases for a symmetry $\mathcal{S}$, defined as inequivalent phases, whose order parameters are part of the same generalized charge under $\mathcal{S}$. Stable, direct transitions between such twin phases are never spontaneous-symmetry-breaking transitions, even after (partially) gauging the initial symmetry $\mathcal{S}$: they are phase transitions without hidden symmetry breaking. We illustrate this with an (anomalous) finite group symmetry in 1+1d, which exhibits such intrinsically beyond Landau transitions.

</details>


### [110] [Twin Algebras: Condensable Algebras beyond Anyons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31602)
*Yuhan Gai,Sakura Schafer-Nameki,Alison Warman*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文引入“孪生可凝代数”（twin condensable algebras）概念——具有相同任意子（anyon）分解但代数结构不等价的代数对象，并在群论拓扑序（group-theoretical topological orders）中系统构造了大量实例，论证它们对应具有相同基态空间但不等价序参量的对称相，可用于构造超越朗道相变（Landau transitions）的相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可凝代数（condensable algebras）在2+1维非手征拓扑序（non-chiral topological orders）中刻画有隙边界条件与界面，并用于对称有隙相的分类与相变约束。然而，可凝代数的完整结构不仅取决于其底层的任意子集合，还取决于代数结构本身，后者可能导致表面上相同的任意子分解对应不同的相——这一现象尚未被系统研究。

Method: 论文引入孪生可凝代数概念，并在群论拓扑序 $\mathcal{Z}(\text{Vec}_G^\omega)$（有限群 $G$ 带有异常 $\omega$）框架下进行分类与构造。通过分析子群数据（subgroup data）、SPT上同调类（SPT cocycles）和群作用（symmetry actions）等不同机制，识别孪生代数；特别地，利用 Gassmann 三元组（Gassmann triples）构造了无穷族孪生例子。

Result: 构造了无穷多孪生可凝代数例子，并展示出：尽管任意子内容完全相同，简化后的拓扑序（reduced topological orders）不等价。物理上，孪生代数描述具有同构基态空间但不等价序参量的不同对称相，这类孪生相之间不会发生相对自发对称性破缺（relative spontaneous symmetry breaking）。

Conclusion: 孪生可凝代数的存在表明，仅依据任意子内容不足以完整刻画对称有隙相；代数结构提供了额外的区分信息。这些孪生相可用于构建无隐藏对称性破缺的相变，这类相变本质上超越了朗道相变范式。

Abstract: Condensable algebras in 2+1d non-chiral topological orders characterize gapped boundary conditions and interfaces. Applied to the Symmetry Topological Field Theory, they allow classification of symmetric gapped phases and impose sharp constraints on possible phase transitions. A condensable algebra is specified not only by its underlying set of anyons, which end on the boundary or interface, but also by its algebra structure. We introduce the concept of twin condensable algebras, which have the same anyon decomposition, but inequivalent algebra structure. We revisit the classification of condensable algebras in $\mathcal{Z}(\text{Vec}_G^ω)$, i.e. in group-theoretical topological orders for finite groups $G$ with anomaly $ω$. In this context we are able to identify twin algebras that arise from different mechanisms, such as subgroup data, SPT cocycles, and symmetry actions. In particular, we construct infinite families of examples of twins from so-called Gassmann triples, and exhibit cases in which the reduced topological orders are inequivalent despite having identical anyon content. Physically, twin algebras describe distinct symmetric phases that have isomorphic spaces of ground states, but inequivalent order parameters. Such twin phases never exhibit relative spontaneous symmetry breaking, and can be used to construct phase transitions without hidden symmetry breaking, which are intrinsically beyond Landau transitions.

</details>


### [111] [Complex Magnetic Behavior of the Ce sawtooth chains in CeRhSn$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31118)
*P. Opletal,J. Fikáček,E. Duverger-Nédellec,A. Thamizhavel,Z. Hossain,R. Tarasenko,V. Tkáč,D. Legut,Bin Shen,P. Gegenwart,J. Custers*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 通过磁化、比热和电阻率测量，结合第一性原理（ab initio）计算，对高质量CeRhSn₂单晶进行了系统研究。该体系在3.65 K发生反铁磁（AFM）序，1.7 K发生一级铁磁（FM）序，1.5 K发生最终相变。外磁场强烈影响相变行为。计算结果支持FM基态。增强的索末菲（Sommerfeld）系数（γ = 76.5 mJ/mol·K²）最可能归因于弱近藤（Kondo）杂化，而非几何阻挫（geometric frustration）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 关于金属间化合物CeRhSn₂的基态（ground state）存在相互矛盾的报道，根源在于晶胞中两个不等价Ce位呈锯齿状排列，暗示可能存在几何磁性阻挫（geometric magnetic frustration）。为澄清这一问题，需要对该体系进行系统性的实验与计算研究。

Method: 采用磁化率（magnetization, M）、比热（specific heat, Cp/T）和电阻率（resistivity, ρ）对高质量CeRhSn₂单晶进行综合测量，并结合第一性原理（ab initio）计算。

Result: 体系表现出强磁各向异性（magnetic anisotropy），b轴为易磁化轴。观测到三个连续相变：3.65 K的反铁磁（AFM）序、1.7 K的一级铁磁（FM）序以及1.5 K的最终相变。相变温度对磁场方向高度敏感：H∥b时，最低相变被立即抑制，且TC与TN迅速合并为一个二级相变；H∥c则抑制FM序并降低TN。第一性原理计算确认FM基态。索末菲系数（Sommerfeld coefficient）γ = 76.5 mJ/mol·K²呈现增强。

Conclusion: CeRhSn₂的基态为铁磁（FM）序。观测到的索末菲系数增强最一致的归因是弱近藤杂化（weak Kondo hybridization），而非几何阻挫（geometric frustration），因为当前数据无法确凿建立阻挫的存在。

Abstract: Conflicting reports exist on the ground state of the intermetallic compound CeRhSn$_2$. This can be rooted in the sawtooth-like arrangement of two inequivalent Ce sites in the unit cell, which suggests potential geometric magnetic frustration. To resolve, we conducted a comprehensive study on high-quality single crystals of CeRhSn$_2$ by means of magnetization ($M$), specific heat ($C_p/T$), and resistivity ($ρ$). The system exhibits strong magnetic anisotropy, confirming the $b$-axis as the easy magnetic axis. We establish three successive transitions, an AFM order at $T_{N} = 3.65$K, a first-order FM order at $T_{C} = 1.7$K and final transition, at $T = 1.5$K. The transition temperatures are highly field-directional dependent: in a magnetic field, the lowest transition is immediately suppressed while $\mathbf{H} \parallel b$ rapidly merges $T_{C}$ and $T_{N}$ into a single second-order transition. Conversely, $\mathbf{H}\parallel c$ suppresses the FM order and reduces $T_{N}$. Additional ab initio calculations affirm the FM ground state of CeRhSn$_2$. The observation of an enhancement of the Sommerfeld coefficient ($γ= 76.5$mJ/mol$\cdot$K$^2$) may arise from geometric frustration, but it is most consistently attributed to weak Kondo hybridization as frustration cannot be conclusively established through our data.

</details>


### [112] [Emergence of spin entanglement with the pseudogap onset in the Fermi-Hubbard model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31240)
*Frederic Bippus,Thomas Chalopin,Gabriele Bellomia,Gergő Roósz,Titus Franz,Antoine Georges,Anna Kauch,Immanuel Bloch,Karsten Held*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过超冷原子量子模拟器（ultracold-atom quantum simulator）和基于动力学顶点近似（dynamical vertex approximation）的数值模拟，发现二维费米-哈伯德模型（two-dimensional Fermi-Hubbard model）中自旋单态纠缠（spin-singlet entanglement）仅在该模型的神秘赝能隙态（pseudogap regime）出现时才开始形成，并且在该区域内仅局限于最近邻格点（nearest-neighbour sites）。该结果否定了纯经典涨落（classical-fluctuation）理论的赝能隙解释，并将微观模型约束为在赝能隙起点发展出最近邻自旋单态纠缠的理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维费米-哈伯德模型历经数十年的理论与实验研究仍未得到完整的微观理解，而传统方法主要探测全局可观测量（global observables）和局域分辨的关联函数（locally resolved correlation functions），缺乏互补性视角。本研究旨在基于纠缠测量（measurement of entanglement）提供一种新的理解路径。

Method: 本研究采用超冷原子量子模拟器进行实验测量，同时基于动力学顶点近似进行数值模拟，以研究二维费米-哈伯德模型中纠缠与赝能隙态之间的关系。

Result: 研究发现自旋单态纠缠仅在赝能隙出现（sets in）时才开始形成，并且在该区域内与经典关联（classical correlations）不同，纠缠局限于最近邻格点。纯经典涨落理论的赝能隙解释因此被否定。

Conclusion: 研究结果不支持纯经典涨落理论的赝能隙解释，并指出微观模型必须满足在赝能隙起点发展出最近邻自旋单态纠缠的条件。

Abstract: Despite decades of intense theoretical and experimental investigation, the two-dimensional Fermi-Hubbard model still resists a complete microscopic understanding. Conventional approaches typically probe global observables and locally resolved correlation functions. Here, we develop a complementary perspective based on the measurement of entanglement. Using both an ultracold-atom quantum simulator and numerical simulations based on the dynamical vertex approximation, we find that entanglement is closely tied to the onset of the enigmatic pseudogap regime: spin-singlet entanglement emerges only as the pseudogap sets in and, in contrast to classical correlations, remains confined to nearest-neighbour sites in this regime. Our results, therefore, disfavour purely classical-fluctuation theories of the pseudogap and constrain microscopic models to those that develop nearest-neighbour spin-singlet entanglement at the pseudogap onset.

</details>

### [113] [Finite-time Scaling with Arbitrary Driving Rates: Bridging the Kibble-Zurek and De Grandi-Gritsev-Polkovnikov Limits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30938)
*Shuai Yin*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出一个广义有限时间标度（generalized finite-time scaling, FTS）框架，统一描述了量子多体系统中从慢速驱动到瞬时淬火全范围的非平衡临界动力学行为，并通过量子临界点和三临界点的数值模拟验证了该理论的普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为远离平衡态的量子多体系统建立普适的非平衡临界动力学描述是现代统计物理学的核心前沿之一。已知的Kibble-Zurek（KZ）标度仅适用于驱动速率低于某个上限的情形，而更广泛的驱动速率范围内的动力学行为缺乏统一理论。

Method: 研究将驱动动力学限制在临界区域内，发展了一个广义有限时间标度（FTS）框架，该框架能够统一描述从慢速驱动下的KZ标度到瞬时淬火极限下的De Grandi-Gritsev-Polkovnikov（DGP）标度的完整淬火速率范围。通过量子临界点（quantum critical point）和三临界点（tricritical point）的数值模拟对理论进行验证。

Result: 理论预测与数值模拟结果高度一致，证实了广义FTS形式的有效性。该框架在任意驱动速率下均表现出稳健的动态标度行为（dynamic scaling behavior）。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了覆盖全驱动速率范围的非平衡临界动力学普适理论，对量子淬火实验（quantum quench experiments）和非平衡统计力学（out-of-equilibrium statistical mechanics）具有广泛意义。

Abstract: The pursuit of a universal description for nonequilibrium critical dynamics in quantum many-body systems stands as a central frontier in modern statistical physics. For driven critical dynamics starting far from the critical point, the well-known Kibble-Zurek (KZ) scaling holds only when the driving rate lies below an upper bound. Here we study driven dynamics restricted to the critical region, and show that robust dynamic scaling behavior exists for arbitrary driving rates. We develop a generalized finite-time scaling (FTS) framework, which provides a unified understanding on the driven dynamics for the full range of quench rates, bridging the KZ scaling in the slow-driving regime and the De~Grandi-Gritsev-Polkovnikov (DGP) scaling in the sudden-quench limit. We verify this unified FTS form through numerical simulations in both quantum critical and tricritical points. The good agreement between theoretical predictions and numerical results confirms the generality of our theory. Our work establishes a universal theory for nonequilibrium critical dynamics spanning the full range of driving rates, with broad implications for quantum quench experiments and out-of-equilibrium statistical mechanics.

</details>


### [114] [Competing heterogeneities shape ordering via higher-order interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30948)
*Gangmin Son,Federico Battiston,Deok-Sun Lee,K. -I. Goh*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 基于空穴法（cavity method）构建了一个分析高阶相互作用中异质性（heterogeneity）的理论框架，并将其应用于异质超图（hypergraph）上的单纯伊辛模型（simplicial Ising model）。研究发现，团簇大小异质性和节点度异质性对相变（phase transition）行为具有截然不同的作用，且两者共存时可通过交叉序度关联（cross-order degree correlations）进一步调控相图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解高阶相互作用（higher-order interactions）中的结构异质性如何影响集体现象（collective phenomena）。以往研究多关注同质结构，而异质超图中的群大小和节点度可能扮演不同角色，但缺乏系统理论框架。

Method: 基于空穴法（cavity method）构建理论框架，并将其应用于异质超图上的单纯伊辛模型（simplicial Ising model），通过解析方法分析不同异质性类型对相变行为的影响。

Result: 群大小异质性通过大群一致性（large-group unanimity）使相变更尖锐；节点度异质性通过枢纽节点（hubs）与非枢纽节点的合作有序化（cooperative seeding）使相变更平缓。两种异质性均可导致连续-不连续双重相变（continuous–discontinuous double transitions），其中对称性破缺连续相变（symmetry-breaking continuous transition）分别由团簇或枢纽节点驱动。当两种异质性共存时，交叉序度关联（cross-order degree correlations）可调控相图，反关联（anticorrelation）会延迟群驱动的不连续跳变并加宽滞后区（hysteretic region）。

Conclusion: 揭示了超越成对相互作用（pairwise interactions）的集体现象中，大小异质性和度异质性之间复杂的相互作用机制，为理解高阶网络中的相变行为提供了理论工具。

Abstract: Higher-order interactions admit richer structural heterogeneity than pairwise networks. To understand how heterogeneity impacts collective phenomena we develop a framework based on the cavity method and apply it to the simplicial Ising model on heterogeneous hypergraphs. Unlike in homogeneous structures, group size and node degree play fundamentally different roles: size heterogeneity sharpens the transition via large-group unanimity, while degree heterogeneity softens it as hubs cooperatively seed ordering with non-hubs. Under either type of heterogeneity, continuous--discontinuous double transitions can arise, where the symmetry-breaking continuous transition is driven by pairs or by hubs, respectively. When both heterogeneities coexist, cross-order degree correlations further modulate the phase diagram, with anticorrelation delaying the group-driven discontinuous jump and broadening the hysteretic region. Our results reveal the intricate interplay between size and degree heterogeneities in collective phenomena beyond pairwise interactions.

</details>


### [115] [Cover time statistics of one-dimensional Brownian motion under stochastic resetting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31207)
*Anirban Ghosh,Sanjib Sabhapandit*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了随机重置（stochastic resetting）对一维有限区间内布朗运动覆盖时间（cover time）统计行为的影响，发现平均覆盖时间随重置速率呈非单调变化，存在最优重置率，并推导了覆盖时间分布的精确解析表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机重置作为一种搜索优化机制已被广泛研究，但其对覆盖时间（即粒子首次访问区间内所有点所需的最短时间）的影响尚不清楚，特别是在有限几何约束下的行为有待探索。

Method: 考虑扩散常数为 $D$ 的一维布朗运动，将其限制在长度为 $L$ 的有限区间内，引入随机重置过程，通过缩放重置率 $\rho = rL^2/4D$ 分析覆盖时间 $t_c$ 的统计性质，并推导了覆盖时间分布的精确解析表达式及其渐近极限。

Result: 缩放平均覆盖时间 $4D\langle t_c\rangle/L^2$ 随 $\rho$ 先减小后增大，在最优重置率 $\rho^*$ 处取最小值，呈现非单调依赖关系；覆盖时间分布的解析结果与数值模拟吻合良好。

Conclusion: 随机重置可以作为受限几何结构（confined geometry）中优化覆盖时间过程的有效机制。

Abstract: We investigate the effect of stochastic resetting on the statistics of the cover time of a one-dimensional Brownian motion with a diffusion constant $D$, confined to a finite interval of length $L$. The cover time $t_c$, defined as the minimum time required for the particle to visit every point of the interval at least once, exhibits a non-monotonic dependence on the scaled reset rate $ρ= rL^2/4D$. The scaled mean cover time $4D\langle t_c\rangle/L^2$ initially decreases with increasing $ρ$, attains a minimum at an optimal value $ρ^*$, and then increases with $ρ$, indicating an optimal resetting rate that minimizes the search duration. Furthermore, we derive an exact analytical expression for the cover time distribution, including its asymptotic limits, which agree well with numerical simulations. These results demonstrate that stochastic resetting serves as an efficient mechanism for optimizing cover-time processes in confined geometries.

</details>


### [116] [Optimization of multisite reactions in complex compartmentalized media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31418)
*T. V. Mendes,T. Guérin*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个在正常扩散介质中运动的随机游走者（random walker）需要到达并激活位于分形（fractal）阻塞亚扩散（sub-diffusion）隔间内的目标的问题。对于弱反应性靶标，隔间尺寸存在一个最优值，可使反应时间最小化，甚至比无隔间系统更快。理论预测通过三维立方晶格上的模拟得到验证，表明在靶标周围添加拥挤隔间可以加速复杂反应动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂介质中，输运和几何性质深刻影响着反应物之间随机相遇的动力学。作者希望探究当靶标位于具有分形阻塞亚扩散特性的隔间内时，双位点反应（dual-site reactions）的完成时间如何受隔间大小和靶标反应性的影响。

Method: 采用理论分析方法，考虑一个在规则扩散介质中移动的随机游走者需激活位于分形阻塞亚扩散隔间内的靶标。反应为双位点反应，要求在给定时间窗口内发生两次激活事件，每次访问靶标时以有限概率发生激活。理论预测通过在三维立方晶格（cubic lattice）上对随机游走者进行模拟验证，隔间内部分格点在临界渗流阈值（critical percolation threshold）处被阻塞。

Result: 对于弱反应性靶标（weakly reactive targets），反应时间可通过选择最优隔间尺寸达到最小化，且该反应时间可快于无隔间系统。隔间内的阻塞亚扩散虽然减缓了靶标附近的运动，但总体上加速了复杂反应的动力学。

Conclusion: 理论表明，在靶标周围添加拥挤隔间可加速复杂反应动力学，尤其对弱反应性靶标效果显著。这一发现挑战了直观认知——局部受限运动反而可能提升整体反应效率。

Abstract: In complex media, transport and geometric properties deeply influence the kinetics of random encounters between reactants. Here, we consider the situation where a random walker, moving in a regularly diffusing medium, has to reach and activate a target located inside a compartment characterized by fractal (obstructed) sub-diffusion. We focus on dual-site reactions, which end when two activation events occur within a given time window. Each activation event happens with a finite probability whenever the random walker visits the target. For weakly reactive targets, we demonstrate that the reaction time can be minimized for an optimal compartment size and can even be accelerated when compared to the same system without compartment. Our analytical predictions are validated through simulations of a random walker on a cubic lattice, where some sites inside the compartment are obstructed at the critical percolation threshold. Our theory illustrates the fact that adding a crowded compartment around a target, even if it slows down the motion in its vicinity, can accelerate the kinetics of complex reactions, especially for weakly reactive targets.

</details>


### [117] [Solving models with generalized free fermions II: Path-product expansion and conserved charges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31453)
*Kohei Fukai,Balázs Pozsgay,István Vona*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过路径积展开（path-product expansion）推导了量子自旋系统中隐藏自由费米子模和局域守恒荷的显式算子结构，并推广到更广义的爪自由（claw-free）图，同时揭示其与自旋-1/2 XXX链中Catalan树结构的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子自旋系统中，当哈密顿量的受挫图（frustration graph）属于偶空无爪自由（even-hole-free and claw-free, ECF）类时，系统具有隐藏自由费米子可解性。然而，与Jordan-Wigner变换下每个模是单个马约拉纳费米子（Majorana fermion）线性组合不同，隐藏自由费米子模及其局域守恒荷的显式算子结构一直不明确，此前缺乏直接从哈密顿量出发构造这些模的方法。

Method: 作者从Krylov基的生成函数出发，推导出一个路径积展开（path-product expansion），将每个自由费米子模表示为扩展受挫图（extended frustration graph）中诱导路径（induced paths）上的路径积线性组合。该方法无需借助转移矩阵（transfer matrix）或非局域守恒荷作为输入，直接得到模的显式形式。

Result: 该路径积展开可直接计算任意ECF受挫图下的无限温动力学关联函数（infinite-temperature dynamical correlation functions）。还得到了局域守恒荷作为诱导路径上路径积线性组合的显式表达式，且这些守恒荷可推广到超越自由费米子（ECF）类的更一般爪自由（claw-free）受挫图。进一步识别出一族统一的广义守恒荷，同时包含已知的非局域守恒荷和本文的局域守恒荷作为特例。对于Fendley原始FFD链，在齐次耦合和周期边界条件下，局域守恒荷的结构展现出与自旋-1/2 XXX链相同的Catalan树（Catalan-tree）模式。

Conclusion: 本文填补了隐藏自由费米子可解系统中模与局域守恒荷显式算子结构的空白，提供了一种不依赖于转移矩阵的直接构造方法，并将分析范围扩展到ECF类之外的爪自由图。发现的Catalan树结构揭示了与自旋-1/2 XXX链之间深层的代数联系，为理解更广泛可积系统中的隐藏自由费米子行为提供了统一框架。

Abstract: Free-fermion solvability in quantum spin systems is increasingly understood to be governed by a graph Clifford algebra defined from the frustration graph of the Hamiltonian. When the frustration graph belongs to certain classes, such as the even-hole-free and claw-free (ECF) class, the Hamiltonian is solvable by hidden free fermions: it admits a free-fermion solution although it does not reduce to a Majorana bilinear under the Jordan-Wigner transformation. However, unlike in the Jordan-Wigner case, where each mode is a linear combination of single Majorana fermions, the explicit operator structure of the hidden free-fermion modes -- and that of the local conserved charges -- has remained obscure. In this work, we derive a path-product expansion that expresses each free-fermion mode as a linear combination of path products along induced paths in the extended frustration graph. The expansion is obtained from the generating function of the Krylov basis and yields the modes directly, without using the transfer matrix or the nonlocal conserved charges as input. As an application, the mode decomposition computes infinite-temperature dynamical correlation functions for arbitrary ECF frustration graphs. We further obtain explicit expressions for local conserved charges as linear combinations of path products along induced paths; these charges apply beyond the free-fermion (ECF) class to more general claw-free frustration graphs. We also identify a unified family of generalized conserved charges that contains both the previously known nonlocal conserved charges and these local conserved charges as special cases. For Fendley's original FFD chain with homogeneous couplings and periodic boundary conditions, in a suitable basis, the structure of these local conserved charges exhibits the same Catalan-tree pattern as in the spin-$1/2$ XXX chain.

</details>

### [118] [Explicit Turn Resolution with Anisotropic Homogenisation for Efficient 3D Magneto-Thermal Finite-Element Simulation of Large-Scale No-Insulation HTS Magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31009)
*Louis Denis,Erik Schnaubelt,Julien Dular,Mariusz Wozniak,Benoît Vanderheyden,Christophe Geuzaine*

Main category: physics.acc-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出并验证了一种名为EXTRA的均匀化方法（explicit turn resolution with anisotropic homogenisation method），用于对无绝缘（NI）和金属绝缘（MI）高温超导磁体进行三维（3D）磁热有限元（FE）仿真。该方法在保证高精度的同时显著降低计算成本，可模拟含临界电流缺陷的万匝级大型超导磁体，计算时间相比逐匝解析模型最多可减少13倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无绝缘（no-insulation）和金属绝缘（metal-insulation）高温超导（high-temperature superconducting, HTS）磁体需要三维（3D）模型来描述临界电流缺陷（critical current defects）附近的电流分布，但现有逐匝解析模型计算成本过高，无法应用于大规模磁体仿真。

Method: EXTRA方法结合了匝间接触层（turn-to-turn contact layers, T2TCLs）及其邻近绕组匝的各向异性均匀化（anisotropic homogenisation）与特定T2TCLs的显式解析。内层和最外层绕组匝及相邻接触层被显式解析以正确描述电流引线附近的电流分布；对于局部Jc缺陷，缺陷附近的绕组匝和T2TCLs被显式解析。解析的T2TCLs采用表面接触近似（surface contact approximation）建模。

Result: 在50匝单饼线圈基准测试中，该方法在标称运行和热失控（thermal runaway）条件下均能复现逐匝解析有限元参考模型的交流损耗和温度分布。在三个150匝饼式线圈堆叠的仿真中，计算时间相比参考模型最多减少13倍。该方法最终成功应用于10,000匝插入式高温超导磁体的大规模3D仿真，这是逐匝解析模型目前无法实现的。

Conclusion: EXTRA均匀化方法能够在合理计算成本下实现大规模超导磁体的高精度三维磁热有限元仿真，并且是开源（open-source）的，所有复现结果的输入文件均已公开提供。

Abstract: No-insulation (NI) and metal-insulation (MI) high-temperature superconducting (HTS) magnets require three-dimensional (3D) models to describe the current distribution around critical current defects. In this work, we design and validate the EXTRA homogenisation method, standing for explicit turn resolution with anisotropic homogenisation method. It allows 3D magneto-thermal finite-element (FE) simulations of large-scale magnets to be performed with high accuracy at a reasonable computational cost. The method combines the anisotropic homogenisation of turn-to-turn contact layers (T2TCLs) and their neighbouring winding turns with the explicit resolution of specific T2TCLs. In particular, the inner- and outermost winding turns and adjacent contact layers are explicitly resolved to properly describe the current distribution near current leads. In addition, the method is able to simulate local $J_{\textrm{c}}$ defects for a broad range of turn-to-turn contact resistances, provided the winding turns and T2TCLs next to the defect are explicitly resolved. For efficiency, the resolved T2TCLs are modelled using the surface contact approximation. The consistency of the proposed method is first verified on a 50-turn single pancake benchmark. It is shown to reproduce AC losses and temperature distributions obtained with a turn-resolved FE reference model, for both nominal operation and during thermal runaway. The computational efficiency of the EXTRA method is demonstrated with the simulation of a stack of three 150-turn pancake coils, for which computation time is reduced by a factor of up to 13 with respect to a turn-resolved FE reference model. Finally, the results of a large-scale 3D FE simulation, currently out of reach of turn-resolved models, are provided for an insert HTS magnet with 10,000 turns. The EXTRA method is open-source and input files to reproduce all results are made available.

### [119] [Measurement of the cross-section for the production of a $W$ boson in association with $b$-jets in $pp$ collisions at $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31205)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文利用ATLAS探测器在LHC上采集的13 TeV质子-质子对撞数据（积分亮度140 fb⁻¹），测量了W玻色子伴随一个或两个喷注（其中至少一个来自b夸克）的产生截面，并将电子与缪子衰变道的平均赝近似截面（16.6±1.9 pb）与次领头阶QCD预言（16.8±2.3 pb）进行了比较，精度较此前7 TeV测量提升约两倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验标准模型（Standard Model）中W+b-jet过程的理论预言，并利用更高能量（13 TeV）和大统计量数据（140 fb⁻¹）提高该过程的测量精度，从而为量子色动力学（QCD）计算及可能的超出标准模型新物理提供约束。

Method: 基于ATLAS探测器在LHC上收集的√s=13 TeV质子-质子对撞数据，对应积分亮度140 fb⁻¹；选择W玻色子衰变至电子或缪子的末态，并要求伴随至少一个b-jet；在由基本轻子与喷注运动学定义的赝近似（fiducial）区域内展开微分截面测量，并对所有探测器效应进行修正。

Result: 电子与缪子道的平均赝近似截面为16.6±1.9 pb，与次领头阶（next-to-leading-order, NLO）QCD理论预言16.8±2.3 pb在误差范围内一致；微分截面作为b-jet横动量的函数也在两种衰变道中分别给出；整体测量相对精度较此前ATLAS在√s=7 TeV的结果提升约两倍。

Conclusion: 测得的结果与NLO QCD预言吻合良好，验证了理论计算在13 TeV能量下的有效性；显著提升的测量精度为后续精确检验标准模型以及探索新物理提供了更可靠的基准。

Abstract: This paper presents a measurement of the production cross-section of a $W$ boson associated with one or two jets, where at least one jet originates from a $b$-quark. The data are collected with the ATLAS detector at the LHC in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 140 fb$^{\text -1}$. Differential cross-sections are presented as a function of the transverse momentum of the $b$-jet for both the electron and muon decay modes of the $W$ boson. The results corrected for all detector effects are presented in a fiducial region defined with basic lepton and jet kinematics, and compared with theoretical predictions. The averaged fiducial cross-section of $W+b$-jets for the electron and muon channels is measured to be $16.6\pm1.9$ pb, which is consistent with the next-to-leading-order QCD prediction of $16.8\pm2.3$ pb. The relative precision of this measurement is improved by approximately a factor of two compared with the previous ATLAS measurement at $\sqrt{s}=7$ TeV.
