### [120] [Entanglement entropy of an acoustic black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30540)
*P. C. van de Graaf,H. T. C. Stoof*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种数值计算声学黑洞（acoustic black hole）纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）的方法，发现大子区域的纠缠熵呈体积律（volume law）而非面积律（area law），其根源在于视界处声子对产生导致的非可分离长程关联，且该体积律部分可由出射霍金辐射（Hawking radiation）的热熵（thermal entropy）近似描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究中黑洞纠缠熵的尺度行为尚不清楚，尤其是数值方法在声学黑洞模型中的应用仍然缺乏，因此需要开发一种数值计算方法来探讨纠缠熵的标度律及其物理起源。

Method: 采用数值计算方法，对声学黑洞模型中的纠缠熵进行直接计算，并通过分析子区域尺寸与纠缠熵的关系来判定标度行为，同时考察视界处声子对产生对长程关联的影响。

Result: 对于足够大的子区域，纠缠熵随尺寸线性增长，呈现体积律而非面积律；该体积律的起源可归因于视界处声子对产生所导致的非可分离长程关联；系统表现出局域热性（local thermal），该体积律部分可被出射霍金辐射的热熵良好近似。

Conclusion: 声学黑洞中纠缠熵的体积律行为挑战了传统面积律预期，揭示了霍金辐射与纠缠熵之间的热力学联系，为理解黑洞信息悖论提供了新的数值视角。

Abstract: We introduce a method to numerically compute the entanglement entropy of an acoustic black hole. It is shown that the entanglement entropy of sufficiently large subregions scales linearly with size and thus shows a volume law instead of an area law. The origin of this scaling can be traced back to the non-separable long-distance correlations due to the production of phonon pairs at the horizon. The system is shown to be locally thermal, such that the part of the entanglement entropy scaling with volume is well approximated by the thermal entropy of the outgoing Hawking radiation.

</details>


### [121] [Dimensionality of a strongly interacting 2D-3D Fermi-Fermi mixture from the perspective of superfluid instability and excitation properties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30986)
*Haruka Takeda,Saki Hirai,Shumpei Iwasaki,Yoji Ohashi*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文利用自洽T矩阵近似（SCTMA）理论研究了不同维度能带间吸引相互作用费米原子气体的强耦合特性，发现从3D-3D过渡到2D-3D系统时，BCS型超导相变温度Tc会因混合维度增强的配对涨落而被显著压低至零，且低维（2D）分量主导了超导不稳定性，而赝能隙现象则表现出3D特征，表明强相互作用费米气体的维度性取决于观测对象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究混合维度（mixed-dimensional）费米气体系统中，当不同维度能带间形成库珀对（Cooper pair）时，强耦合效应对超导相变温度Tc以及赝能隙（pseudogap）现象的影响。

Method: 采用自洽T矩阵近似（self-consistent T-matrix approximation, SCTMA）框架，在从3D-3D到2D-3D系统的跨维度演化中，纳入配对涨落（pairing fluctuations）效应，系统分析不同配对相互作用强度下的超导相变温度。

Result: 在2D-3D极限下，平均场BCS理论预测强耦合区Tc>0，但配对涨落因系统混合维度性而显著增强，将Tc压低至零；低维（2D）分量主导超导不稳定性，其机制与2D-2D系统相同。赝能隙现象则表现出3D特征。

Conclusion: 强相互作用费米气体的有效维度取决于所观测的物理量：超导不稳定性由低维分量主导而表现二维特征，赝能隙现象则呈现三维特征。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate strong-coupling properties of an attractively interacting Fermi atomic gas, where the Cooper-pair formation occurs between atoms belonging to different dimensional bands. Including pairing fluctuations within the framework of the self-consistent $T$-matrix approximation (SCTMA), we examine how the BCS-type superfluid phase transition temperature $T_\mathrm{c}$ varies as one moves from the 3D-3D to the 2D-3D system, in the wide parameter region with respect to the strength of the pairing interaction. In the 2D-3D limit, we find that, while the mean-field BCS theory predicts $T_\mathrm{c}>0$ in the strong-coupling regime, $T_\mathrm{c}$ is remarkably suppressed down to zero by pairing fluctuations that are strongly enhanced by the mixed-dimensionality of the system. As the origin of this, we clarify that the lower-dimensional (2D) component dominates the superfluid instability, so that the vanishing $T_\mathrm{c}$ is the same phenomenon as that in the 2D-2D case. We also point out that this can already be seen in the mean-field level, when one examines the propagation of the Goldstone mode. On the other hand, we find that the pseudogap phenomenon, which is known as a precursor of Cooper-pair formation, exhibits a 3D character of the 2D-3D system. These results indicate that the dimensionality of a strongly interacting Fermi gas depends on what we observe.

</details>


### [122] [Charged Bose polarons at finite momentum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31255)
*Grover Andrade Sánchez,Arturo Camacho Guardian*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文利用二阶微扰论下的图解方法，研究了带电玻色极化子（charged Bose polaron）的动量依赖性质，揭示了有限程离子-原子相互作用引入的特征动量尺度，并发现高动量区域存在Γ_p ∼ 1/p标度律，表明多体修饰的抑制和准自由杂质动力学的恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往研究集中于带电杂质在量子流体中的基态和静态性质，对其有限动量行为——这一决定输运、耗散和准粒子稳定性的关键因素——了解甚少。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 采用基于二阶微扰论（second-order perturbation theory）的图解方法（diagrammatic approach），并显式考虑了离子-原子相互作用的有限程（finite-range）效应。

Result: 相互作用范围引入了一个特征动量尺度，在该尺度下多体修饰（many-body dressing）和耗散最大，导致阻尼率和准粒子能量呈现非单调行为。在高动量区域，发现标度律Γ_p ∼ 1/p，标志着多体修饰的抑制和准自由杂质动力学的恢复，这与接触相互作用（contact-interaction）微扰处理所预测的发散行为形成鲜明对比。

Conclusion: 有限程相互作用对带电玻色极化子的有限动量性质至关重要，其效应修正了基于接触相互作用的传统理论预期，揭示了高动量区域准自由行为的恢复。

Abstract: Charged impurities in quantum fluids have unveiled new classes of strongly correlated many-body states across condensed matter, ultracold gases, and hybrid atom-ion platforms. While previous studies have primarily focused on their ground-state and static properties, much less is known about their finite-momentum behavior, which governs transport, dissipation, and quasiparticle stability. Here, we investigate the momentum-dependent properties of a charged Bose polaron using a diagrammatic approach within second-order perturbation theory, explicitly accounting for the finite-range nature of the ion-atom interaction. We show that the interaction range introduces a characteristic momentum scale at which many-body dressing and dissipation are maximized, leading to a non-monotonic behavior of the damping rate and quasiparticle energy. In the high-momentum regime, we uncover a scaling law $Γ_p \sim 1/p$, signaling the suppression of many-body dressing and the recovery of quasi-free impurity dynamics, in stark contrast to the divergent behavior predicted by contact-interaction perturbative treatments.

</details>
